। brahmasūtrabhāṣyam ।
śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracitam
।
jijñāsyaṃ janmarakṣālayaniyatimatipratyagajñānabandha
śreyodaṃ śāstragamyaṃ śrutigatavacanairmukhyavṛttyābhidheyam ।
bhaiṣmīsatyāsametaṃ bahuguṇavapuṣaṃ bhītipūrvāradūraṃ
bhaktiśrutyādicintyaṃ bhajanaparagatiṃ bhāvaye veṇukṛṣṇam ।
āmrastambhātsamāgamya tāmratuṇḍānnihatya yaḥ ।
namraṃ naumi jagannāthaṃ kamro apāttaṃ nṛkesarī ।
anadhītya mahābhāṣyaṃ yasya vyākṛṣyanugrahāt ।
tamupāse nṛsiṃhārkaṃ pratyūhatimirāpaham ।
pūrṇabodhagurūn vande jayāryān vyāsadeśikān ।
rāmacandragurūnāryān lakṣmīkāntagurūnapi ।
yenāyaṃ niraṇāyi madhvagurusadbhāṣyaprakāśāśayaḥ
prākhaṇḍi prativādidarśanagaṇaḥ prābandhi gurvarṇavaḥ ।
śiṣyebhyassamadāyi vittamubhayaṃ prālambhi vidyāsanaṃ
so ayaṃ śrīraghunāthatīrthagururāṭ śuddhiṃ vidadhyānmateḥ ।
jayāryaracitāṃ ṭīkāmanusṛtya yathāmati ।
jagannāthākhyayatinā kriyate bhāṣyadīpikā ।
kvacidbhāṣyavivṛtyaiva ṭīkārtho api vivicyate ।
tattvapradīpatātparyacandrikādyuktamārgataḥ ।

nārāyaṇaṃ guṇaissarvairudīrṇaṃ doṣavarjitam ।
jñeyaṃ gamyaṃ gurūṃścāpi natvā sūtrārtha ucyate ।
paramānandādyātmakasya paramātmanaḥ pratibimbatayā svataścidānandādyātmakasya jīvasya anādyavidyākāmakarmādinimittabandhadhvaṃsāya nikhilajīvajaḍātmakāt prapañcāt paramārthato atyantabhinnatayā nikhilaguṇodāratayā nirastasamastadoṣatayā paramapuruṣamavagamayituṃ sakalasadāgamānāṃ pravṛttiriti tattvam ।
yadāhuḥ 
aduḥkhamitaratsarvaṃ jīvā eva tu duḥkhinaḥ ।
teṣāṃ duḥkhaprahāṇāya śrutireṣā pravartate ।
iti ।
apravartate'; duḥkhaprahāṇasādhanaṃ paramātmānaṃ pratipādayatītyarthaḥ । teṣāṃ cārthanirṇayāya brahmasūtrāṇi cakāra bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ । tāni ca paṭalapihitanayanavat yathāvadarthāvettṛbhiḥ avidyākhyapaṭalapihitanayanapadoktasadarthaiḥ anyairanyathāvyākhyātāni
yathāvadvyācikhyāsurbhagavānānandatīrthācāryaḥ samaṅgalasyaiva saphalatvāt prāripsitabhāṣyasya kaivalyādyakhilaphalasādhanatāsiddhyarthaṃ nirantarāyaparisamāptyādyarthaṃ ca nārāyaṇapraṇāmarūpaṃ maṅgalamācaran śiṣyaśikṣārthaṃ grathayati cikīrṣitaṃ ca pratijānīte anārāyaṇam'; iti । asarvairguṇaiḥ udīrṇaṃ'; udāram utkṛṣṭam । adoṣavarjitaṃ'; doṣarahitam। ajñeyaṃ'; parokṣāparokṣākhyobhayavidhajñānaviṣayīkaraṇīyam । agamyaṃ'; prāpyam । ubhayatra sadbhiriti śeṣaḥ । nārāyaṇaṃ anatvā gurūṃśca'; iti cakārārthassamuccayaḥ । tathā ca gurūṃśca natvā sāṣṭāṅgaṃ namaskṛtya asūtrārthaḥ'; samastavedatadupabṛṃhaṇetihāsapurāṇādiśabdarāśyarthabhūto nārāyaṇākhyo brahmasūtrārtho mayā aucyate'; bhāṣyata iti yojanā।
atra guṇairudīrṇam ityanena prathamādhyāyasya, doṣavarjitam ityanena dvitīyādhyāyasya, jñeyam ityanena tṛtīyādhyāyasya, gamyam ityanena caturthādhyāyasya arthaḥ śiṣyahitatayā ādau saṅgṛhīta iti jñātavyam । anenaiva viśeṣaṇacatuṣṭayena viśeṣyavācakanārāyaṇaśabdaḥ na ḍitthādiśabdavatsāṅketikaḥ; kintu arāḥ doṣāḥ tadviruddhāḥ nārāḥ guṇāḥ teṣāmāśraya iti vā, arāṇāmāśrayo na bhavatīti vā, viṣayatayā naraviśeṣasambandhijñānāśraya iti vā, aravidhuramuktāśraya iti vā yogenotkṛṣṭaguṇavācaka ityuktaṃ bhavati । tena nārāyaṇa eva śāstrārtha iti pradarśitam । anenaiva viśeṣaṇacatuṣṭayena vandyatāprayojakāni bahuguṇatvanirdeṣatvaśāstrajñeyatvaśāstragamyatvāni coktāni ।
yadvā atra nārāyaṇamityādipadapañcakena samudraśāyitvasarvavasanotkarṣakrīḍājñānādiguṇairuccatvasamyagdoṣakarṣaṇaprakṛṣṭadyutimayatvajñāninaḥ prati prāptinirodharahitatvākhyanimittapañcakayutena nārāyaṇavāsudevasaṅkarṣaṇapradyumnāniruddhākhyamūrtaya ucyante; tāsāmetacchāstrādhyāyapādeṣu pratipipādayiṣitatvāt । tathā ca anārāyaṇaṃ natvā guṇairudīrṇaṃ natvā doṣavarjitaṃ natvā'; ityādikā tattvapradīpikoktayojanā draṣṭavyā ।
agurornāma na gṛhṇīyācchiṣyo bhāryā paterapi'; iti vacanād gurornāma nāgrahīdācāryaḥ । na ca agurūn nārāyaṇaśabdavācyān nārāyaṇapadenaiva gurunāma covāca, āsamantāt viśiṣṭassa eva hi vyāso api'; iti tattvapradīpikāvirodha iti vācyam; gurudevatayorvāstavābhedavivakṣayā tadupapatteḥ । yogarūḍhavyāsakṛṣṇādyasādhāraṇanāmavivakṣayā evamuktatvāt । gurutvanimittaśāstraprabhavatvaśāstrasampradāyapravartakatvasākṣādupadeśakatvākhyaprakārabāhulyāt gauravādvā bahumānārthaṃ vā bahuvacanaprayogaḥ । yadyapi gururvyāsaḥ, iṣṭadevatāpi sa eveti na tayorbhedaḥ, tathāpi viśeṣānugrahārthaṃ pṛthaṅnatiriti । evaṃ svasya gurudevatayoḥ bhede arucisūcanārtho apiśabdaḥ । tathā ca aapi'; tathāpi gurudevatābhedābhāve apītyarthaḥ । tattvapradīpakṛttu apiśabdātsūtrakāramapītyāha । tasyāpi viśeṣānugrahārthaṃ pṛthaṅnatirityevābhiprāyaḥ । yadvāpiśabdaḥ viśeṣaṇāntarasamuccayārthaḥ, tadvivaraṇamasyetyādi'; iti sudhoktarītyā guṇapūrṇatvopapādakajagajjanmādikāraṇatvādirūpānuktaviśeṣaṇāntarasamuccayārtho apiśabdaḥ ।
anenaiva ślokena śrotṛpravṛttyaṅgabhūtāḥ śāstrādhikāriviṣayaprayojanasambandhāśca śiṣyaśikṣārthaṃ sūcitā bhavanti।

dvāpare sarvatra jñāne ākulībhūte tannirṇayāya brahmarudrendrādibhirarthito bhagavānnārāyaṇo vyāsatvenāvatatāra ।
nanu brahmasūtrāṇāṃ prāmāṇye satyeva prekṣāvadupādeyatvam, prāyo asya prāmāṇyaprayojyatvāt । satyeva tasmin prātītikārthanirāsena yathāvadvyākhyeyatvaṃ sambhavati । prāmāṇyameva kathamityāśaṅkya āptimūlatvādinaiveti parihāramabhipretya vaktṛśrotṛprasaṅgadoṣābhāvarūpāptimūlatvopapādanāya sūtrāgatikramamāha advāpare'; ityādinā । dvāveva dharmapādau parāvavaśiṣṭau yasmin yuge, dvābhyāṃ yugābhyāṃ parasminnuttarasmin yuge iti vā, vaivasvatamanvantare mahāyugeṣu prathamadvāparāpekṣayāṣṭāviṃśe dharmapādadvayayutatvāt dvāparākhye yuge । asarvatra'; amanuṣyāṇāṃ ṛṣīṇāṃ devānāṃ ca'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ aloka iti sajjano vivakṣitaḥ'; iti prameyadīpokteśca sarveṣāṃ devaṛṣyādīnāṃ satāṃ ajñāne'; samyagjñāne aākulībhūte'; samyagjñānaṃ saguṇatvādijñānaṃ uta nirguṇatvādijñānamiti vipratipattijanyasandehaviṣayatāṃ nirguṇatvādijñānameva na tvanyaditi mithyājñānaviṣayatāṃ ca prāpte sati, tajjñānaviṣayībhūtaṃ saguṇatvādikaṃ tattvamanyadveti sandehe tādṛgviparyaye ca satīti yāvat । atannirṇayāya'; tasmin saguṇatvādijñāne tasya samyagjñānatvasya niścayārthe, idameva tattvaṃ nānyaditi viṣaye samyaktvaniścayārthamiti yāvat । abrahmarudrendrādibhiḥ'; devairiti śeṣaḥ । aarthitaḥ'; upayācitaḥ । anyapadārthānāṃ devānāṃ brahmarudrendrādibhiriti yadviśeṣaṇaṃ tat prasiddhaprabhāvānāmapi bhagavaditareṣāmaśakyamidaṃ kāryamiti pradarśanārtham । abhagavān'; samagraiśvaryavairāgyādiguṇasampanno anārāyaṇaḥ'; tannirṇayāya avyāsatvena'; vyāsabhāvena aśubhamarakatavarṇam'; ityuktavyāsarūpeṇa aavatatāra'; āvirbabhūveti । tannirṇayāyetyasyāvṛtyā yojanā । tannirṇayāyendrādibhirarthito rudraḥ brahmā ca tataḥ taiḥ sarvairupagamyottamādhikāribhiḥ arthito bhagavāniti buddhyā vivekenānvayaḥ ।

atheṣṭāniṣṭaprāptiparihārecchūnāṃ tadyogamavijānatāṃ tajjñāpanārthaṃ vedamutsannaṃ vyañjayaṃścaturdhā vyabhajat, caturviṃśatidhaikaśatadhā sahasradhā dvādaśadhā ca ।
tataḥ kiṃ prakṛte ityata āha atheti । aatha'; tasmāt tannirṇayāyāvatīrṇatvāt avatārānantarameva tattvajñānānanukūlavijātīyavyāpāravyavadhānamakṛtveti yāvat, na tu paropadeśamapekṣyeti vā । aiṣṭāniṣṭaprāptiparihārecchūnām'; iṣṭaprāptiścāniṣṭaparihāraśca tāvicchūnām । tattvapradīparītyā aprāptasukhaprāptiduḥkhaparihārecchāvatāmiti vā । mokṣasya puruṣārthatāsamarthanārthaṃ vādivipratipatteḥ tatsvarūpanirūpaṇārthaṃ caivamuktam । anyathā mumukṣūṇāmityeva brūyāt । naitāvatālam aātyantika'; iti copaskartavyam । atadyogaṃ'; tayorupāyaviśeṣaṃ nivṛttadharmaparāparatattvajñānarūpaṃ aavijānatām'; ajānānānāṃ sajjanānāṃ atajjñāpanārtham'; iṣṭāniṣṭaprāptiparihāropāyajñāpanārthaṃ। autsannam'; apapāṭhādinā tirohitaṃ avedaṃ caturdhā'; avyabhajat'; ityāvartate, atataḥ prāgeva vibhaktam'; iti apunarekaikam'; iti ca śeṣaḥ । tathā ca avāntaravedavibhāgāt prāgeva tataḥ svata eva caturdhā vibhaktāt ṛgādirūpāt mūlavedāt caturdhā vibhaktaṃ vedaṃ ṛṅnigadādirūpamupavedaṃ vyañjayan adhyāpanenābhivyajya tatastasmādekaikasmādekaiko bhāga iti caturdhā vyabhajat । ṛco ṛca uddhṛtyābhivyajya tato ṛgvedaṃ, nigadādyajurvedam, sāmnassāmavedam, ātharvaṇādatharvaṇavedaṃ kṛtavānityarthaḥ । punarekaikaṃ ca vedam ṛgvedādirūpāvāntarabhedaṃ vedam
adhyetṛṇāmalpaśaktiṃ vīkṣya caturviṃśatidhā ekaśatadhā ekottaraśatākhyaprakāreṇa sahasradhā dvādaśadhā ca vyabhajadityarthaḥ । taduktam ṛgbhāṣye 
ṛcaḥ sa ṛca uddhṛtya ṛgvedaṃ kṛtavān prabhuḥ ।
yajūṃṣi nigadāccaiva tathā sāmāni sāmataḥ ।
ityādinā svata eva caturdhā vibhaktāt mūlavedāt ṛgādirūpopavedamuddhṛtyābhivyajya tasmādavāntaram ṛgvedādi kṛtavānityarthaḥ । atra pūrvaṃ dvāparagrahaṇaṃ mahāvedāt uddhṛtasya upavedasya avāntaravedatvena avāntaravedasya ca caturviṃśatyāditvena vibhāgakathanaṃ ca akhilajñānākulībhāvasamarthanārtham । kālato vibhāgātpūrvaṃ tattacchākhāparijñānācca bhavati hyākulībhāvaḥ । taduktaṃ acakre vedataroḥ'; ityādinā । aalpamedhasaḥ'; ākulībhūtajñānān, tannivāraṇārthamiti śeṣaḥ । yadyapi 
eko vedaḥ kṛte hyāsīt tretāyāṃ sa tridhābhavat ।
sa eva pañcadhā jāto dvāparaṃ prāpya vai yugam ।
utsannassa kaliṃ prāpya vedaḥ prāyeṇa sarvaśaḥ ।
ityatharvaṇabhāṣyodāhṛtasmṛtau kṛtayuge vedaikatvasya tretāyāṃ traividhyamātrasya dvāpare pañcavidhatvasya cokteḥ, tathā sarvasyāpi vedasya kalāvevotsādokteḥ, atra tu avedamutsannam'; ityanena tretāyuge caturdhā vibhāgasya dvāpara evotsādasya coktervirodho bhāti । tathāpi avyaktamūlarāśyapekṣayā vedaikyokteḥ sambhavāt, tretāyuge prācuryeṇa bhagavadijyāsādhanatvavivakṣayā traividhyoktāvapi vastuta atharvaṇākhyaprakārāntarasattvasya aniṣedhena vidhāntarasyāpi sattvasambhavāt, dvāpare apauruṣeyasya vedasya caturvidhatve api pauruṣeyairitihāsapurāṇādibhiḥ saha pañcavidhatvasyāpi sambhavāt, bāhulyena sarvaiḥ prakārairvedasya kalāvutsāde api vyāsāvatārātpūrvaṃ dvāpare apyapapāṭhādirūpotsādasya sambhavāt avirodhaḥ।

tadarthanirṇayāya brahmasūtrāṇi cakāra ।
evamupodghātamuktvā prakṛtamāha atadarthanirṇayāya'; iti । teṣāṃ sarveṣām arthaḥ tam upakramādiyuktibhirnirṇetumityarthaḥ । abrahmasūtrāṇi'; brahma vedaḥ, tadarthaḥ parabrahma vā, tasya sūtrāṇi tatsvarūpanirṇāyakānītyarthaḥ। gītābhāṣye tu abrahmasūtrāṇi cakāra'; ityantena vakturvyāsasya nārāyaṇāvatāratvoktyā parihṛtatvāt, brahmādīnāmarthitvoktyā ca śrotṛdoṣābhāvasya vaktari tannimittavipralambhābhāvasya coktatvāt, ajñāna ākulībhūte tannirṇayāya'; ityanena ajñānanirharaṇasya prasaktatvena prasaṅgadoṣābhāvasya tata evānapahāsasya coktatvādāptimūlatā darśitā bhavati। abrahmasūtrāṇi'; ityanena brahmaparaśrutivyākhyānarūpatvāt śrutimūlatvaṃ, nyāyavyutpādakatvādyuktimūlatvaṃ ca sūcitam । tathā ca siddhaṃ brahmasūtrāṇāṃ prāmāṇyamiti bhāvaḥ ।

taccoktaṃ skānde 
nārāyaṇād viniṣpannaṃ jñānaṃ kṛtayuge sthitam ।
kiñcittadanyathā jātaṃ tretāyāṃ dvāpare akhilam ।
uktamevārthaṃ pramāṇena sthāpayati atacca'; iti । aca'; śabda evārthe । tathā ca yadasmābhiḥ advāpare'; ityādinoktaṃ tat skāndapurāṇoktameveti bhāvaḥ । na kevalamasmābhiḥ kintu skānde coktamiti samuccaye vā aca'; śabdaḥ । tathoktaṃ tattvapradīpe ayadyapyācāryaḥ svoktārthe svayameva pramāṇaṃ, sarvajñatvādavipralambhakatvācca । tathāpi skānde coktamiti prauḍhavādaṃ karoti'; iti । ana kevalamasmābhiḥ'; iti prameyadīpe api kimuktamityatastatpaṭhati anārāyaṇāt'; iti । tadupadeśādityarthaḥ । abrahmādidvārā'; iti śeṣaḥ । yadvā utpattyādyaṣṭake jñānasya praviṣṭatvāt tasya nārāyaṇajanyatvopapattiḥ । aniṣpannam'; utpannaṃ aakhilaṃ'; saguṇatvādisarvaviṣayakamityatrāpi sambadhyate । ajñānaṃ'; samyagjñānaṃ asthitaṃ'; yathotpannaṃ tathaiva saṃśayādyanāskanditameva sthitam । asatsu'; iti śeṣaḥ । jñānaviṣaye saṃśayādikaṃ nābhūditi phalitārthaḥ । atretāyāṃ'; yuge atat'; jñānaṃ akiñcit'; viṣaye aanyathājātam'; idamado veti pūrvoktasaṃśayaviṣayatām anyadeveti mithyājñānaviṣayatāṃ ca prāptamityarthaḥ । atra dvāparavat tretādirapyaṣṭāviṃśo grāhyaḥ । dvāpare yuge akhilaṃ sarvaviṣayaṃ tadanyathā jātamityanvayaḥ ।

gautamasya ṛṣeśśāpājjñāne tvajñānatāṃ gate ।
saṅkīrṇabuddhayo devā brahmarudrapurassarāḥ ।
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ nārāyaṇamanāmayam ।
nanu kālaprayuktamanyathātvaṃ cet dvāparayuge bhāgadvayasyaivānyathātvaṃ yuktaṃ, na tu sarvasyetyato viśeṣakāraṇaṃ cāha agotamasya'; iti । atu'; śabdaścārthaḥ śāpe viśeṣakāraṇatvasya jñāne vā samyaktvasya dyotakaḥ । tathā ca gautamasya ṛṣeḥ śāpācca jñāne guṇapūrṇatvādisamyagjñāne ajñānatāṃ nedaṃ tattvajñānamiti tattvajñānabhinnatvaprakārakapratītiviṣayatāṃ sandehaviṣayatāṃ ca gate prāpte sati, jñānaviṣaye samyagjñānaviruddhasaṃśayaviparyayaviṣayatāṃ gate satīti yāvat । abrahmarudrapurassarāḥ'; tadādayo adevāḥ'; asaṅkīrṇabuddhayaḥ'; ajñānādimiśrajñāninaḥ yadviṣaye jñānaṃ jātaṃ punastadviṣayagataprakāreṣu ajñānasaṃśayādimantaḥ santaḥ aśaraṇyaṃ'; tatra sādhuṃ śaraṇeṣu rakṣakeṣu agryam aanāmayaṃ'; pramāṇalakṣaṇaṭīkoktarītyā atra āmayapadaṃ rogavācakaṃ doṣāntaropalakṣakam । tathā ca nirdeṣaṃ anārāyaṇaṃ'; "sarvottamatvavijñānapūrvaṃ tatra manaḥ sadā"ityādyuktaprakāreṇa aśaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ'; śaraṇaṃ gatā ityarthaḥ । taṃ prārthayan svakāryaṃ ca vyajñāpayanniti ca draṣṭavyam । atra brahmādibuddhīnāṃ saṅkīrṇatvaṃ nāma saṅkīrṇabuddhiṣu sajjaneṣu dayāyuktatvameva, na tvitareṣāṃ buddhīnāmivājñānādimiśratvam, ajñānasaṃśayādiviṣayaviṣayakatvaṃ vā । svahatagonirmātṛmātraviṣayakagautamaśāpakālanimittābhibhavapadoktatirodhānayordeveṣvasambhavāt । brahmādidevagonirmātṛvyatiriktalokasya tu gautamahatagonirmātṛtvābhāve api sampradāyapravartakābhāvāt kālataścājñānaprāptiriti draṣṭavyam । gautamaśāpāgamaprakārastu ittham pūrvaṃ hi dvādaśavārṣikyāṃ anāvṛṣṭau satyāṃ tayā pīḍitā ṛṣayo gautamāśramaṃ annavantam adhyūṣuḥ । tatraiva bahukālaṃ tenādṛtāḥ svasvavihitakarmāṇaḥ samavartanta । atha anāvṛṣṭau śāntāyāṃ teṣāṃ svasvāśramagamanecchā samajani । tadarthaṃ gautamamanujñāṃ yayācire । tathāpi svāśramāśūnyatālobhāt na tadanujñāmalambhiṣata । tasminnevāvasare
haraśirassthasurasaritaṃ sapatnīṃ matvā tāṃ niścikāsayiṣantyā pārvatyā preṣito vināyako brahmacāriveṣeṇa pracchannastānṛṣīnupasasāra, abravīcca he tatra bhavantaḥ, kimarthamimamāśramamadhivasatha? cirakālamekaparānnāśanena yuṣmattapo vinaṅkṣyati। tasmāt svaṃsvamāśramaṃ vrajata। tatra ca mayocyamānamupāyamākarṇayata। yūyaṃ jñānatapobalāt kāñcana māyāmayīṃ māheyīṃ nirmimīdhvam । tāṃ gautamatapobalākṛṣṭabalāhakāvalīvigalitasalilavardhitasasyādau praveśayata । atha sasyagrāsinīṃ tāṃ apakrāmayituṃ prayatiṣyate gautamaḥ । tataḥ sahasā tatkamaṇḍalūdakasaṃsparśamātreṇa sā nipatiṣyati । tadā brāhmaṇāstaṃ pratibrūta yāvadimāmaśeṣamātaraṃ gāṃ notthāpayiṣyati bhavān tāvanna bhojyānnaḥ । tato haraśirassthadyusaritamavatārya tadvāriṇā abhiṣicya tāmujjīvayatu bhavān ityevamanutāpinaṃ tamabhilapyāpasaratetyuktvā herambo ambikāṃ jagāma। atha te vināyakena praṇigaditaṃ prayāṇopāyamupasṛtya anvatiṣṭhan। tenaivopāyena prātiṣṭhanta । tatastāvadgautamaḥ tapasā tryambakamārādhya mandākinīṃ anusamānīya tadvāriṇā surabhimabhiṣiṣeca । tataḥ sottasthau munistaddhatyāghāt vimuktaśca । ata eva godāvarīti tasyāḥ saṃjñā samajani । atha vināyakaceṣṭitaṃ pratibudhya ṛṣibhyaścukrodha, aśapacca gautamaḥ yadasmadannanimittajñānabalādete gāṃ niramaṃsta tat jñānamapaitviti ।

tairvijñāpitakāryastu bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ ।
avatīrṇo mahāyogī satyavatyāṃ parāśarāt ।
utsannānbhagavānvedānujjahāra harisvayam ।
caturdhā vyabhajattāṃśca caturviṃśatidhā punaḥ ।
śatadhā caikadhā caiva tathaiva ca sahasradhā ।
kṛṣṇo dvādaśadhā caiva
devaiḥ prārthito bhagavān kimakarodityata āha ataiḥ'; iti । amahāyogī'; munirūpaḥ mahāśaktirvā । apuruṣottamaḥ'; kṣarākṣaracetanābhyāṃ uttamo abhagavān'; nārāyaṇaḥ ataiḥ'; svaśaraṇāgatiṃ prāptaireva devaiḥ avijñāpitakāryaḥ'; san vijñāpitaṃ pratipāditam avatārādirūpaṃ kāryaṃ yasya saḥ, rūpeṇa amahāyogī'; nāmnā kṛṣṇaḥ aparāśarāt satyavatyāmavatīrṇaḥ'; ityanvayaḥ । avatārānantarikaprayojanamāha autsannān'; iti । asvayaṃ'; sākṣāt ahariḥ'; abhagavān'; jñānādiguṇaśālī vyāsaḥ autsannān'; apapāṭhādinā tirohitān avedān'; asvayameva'; anyopadeśamantareṇa aujjahāra'; uccāraṇena vyaktīcakāra । tāṃśca prāgeva caturdhā vibhaktān vedān punaḥ acaturdhā vyabhajat'; caturbhāgānakarot । ekaikaṃ ca bhāgaṃ apunaḥ'; caturviṃśatyādiśākhārūpeṇa ṛgvedaṃ acaturviṃśatidhā', yajurvedaṃ aekaśatadhā'; ekottaraśatākhyaikaprakāreṇa, sāmavedaṃ asahasradhā'; atharvaṇavedaṃ advādaśadhā ca'; vyabhajadityarthaḥ । bhagavattvasya mukhyatvajñāpanāya abhagavān'; iti punaruktiḥ । aeva'; śabdāḥ prakārādhikyavyavacchedakāḥ । aca'; śabdāḥ prakārāṇāṃ parasparasamuccāyakāḥ ।

punastasyārthavittaye ।
prakṛtamāha apunaḥ'; iti । pūrveṇaivāsyānvayaḥ । yadvā uttareṇāpyanvayaḥ । vedavibhāgānantaraṃ ityarthaḥ । atasya'; vedasya aarthavittaye'; arthajñānāya । vedānāṃ bahutve api arthasyaikatvāttadvivakṣayā tān vedāniti bahuvacananirdiṣṭānāmapi vedānāṃ tasyetyekavacanena nirdeśo nānupapannaḥ, tasyetyasya samudāyaikavacanatvāt । nityasāpekṣatvāt aarthavittaye'; iti samāsassādhuḥ । punaśśabdasyānantaryārthatvaṃ ca apunaraprathame bhede'; ityamaroktyā apunareva samabhyaset'; ityatra punaḥ nidrāpagamānantaramiti sudhoktyā atṛtīye punareva ca'; ityatra varatrayānantaramiti viśveśatīrthoktyā ca siddham । acakāra'; ityatrāpi akṛṣṇo vyāsaḥ'; ityanuṣajyate । nanu sūtrāntaraireva vedārthanirṇayasambhavātkiṃ brahmasūtrairiti gatārthatāśaṅkāparihārāyāha ayeṣām'; iti। asūtratvaṃ'; sūtraśabdapravṛttinimittaṃ aañjasā'; mukhyato astītyarthaḥ। asya tāni acakāra'; iti pūrveṇa aevaṃvidhāni'; ityuttareṇa vā anvayaḥ ।

alpākṣaramasandigdhaṃ sāravad viśvatomukham ।
astobhamanavadyaṃ ca sūtraṃ sūtravido viduḥ ।
kiṃ tat sūtratvaṃ yadāñjasyaṃ brahmasūtrāṇāmityata āha aalpa'; iti । yāvadakṣaratāṃ vinā śrutyarthābhyāṃ vivakṣitārthasiddhirnāsti tadarthapratipādanāya tāvanmātrākṣaramasati niyāmake tato adhikākṣararahitam aalpākṣaram'; । kecittu alpākṣarabahvakṣarayuktaparyāyapadayormadhye alpākṣarapadopetatvaṃ alpākṣaratvamityāhuḥ । evaṃ ca bhavitumarhatītyanucyamānārtham aasandigdham'; । aasandigdhārthaṃ nirṇītārtham'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ । ananyalabhyottamārthayuktaṃ asāravat'; । bahuśākhāgatapadavākyārthanirṇāyakaṃ aviśvatomukham'; । tattvapradīpe tu ekaṃ prayojanaṃ pratyapekṣitārthasya kṛtsnasya pratipādikaṃ aviśvatomukham'; ityuktam । arthajñānamantareṇa gānabhāgapūraṇādiprayojanāntarārthākṣararahitam aastobham'; । śabdārthadoṣavidhuram aanavadyam'; । yadetāvadviśeṣaṇayutaṃ tadeva asūtram'; iti asūtravidaḥ'; sūtralakṣaṇajñāḥ aviduḥ'; abhyupayantītyarthaḥ । atra bhāṣyanirṇayahetuśūnyavākyaṃ kuśalapuruṣoktalaukikavārtādikaṃ bhagavannāmamantrādikam arthāpratipādakatve api
ṛgakṣarāvyāptagānabhāgaparipūrakasāmagatastobhākṣarāṇi apaśabdopetatādṛśavākyaṃ ca vyāvartayituṃ krameṇa viśeṣaṇānīti padaprayojanaṃ tattvapradīpoktamanusandheyam । atra sarvatra dharmikathane api taddvārā sūtrapadapravṛttinimittamapyuktamiti nāsaṅgatiḥ ।

nirviśeṣitasūtratvaṃ brahmasūtrasya cāpyataḥ ।
yathā vyāsatvamekasya kṛṣṇasyānye viśeṣaṇāt ।
nanvetatsūtratvaṃ kuto brahmasūtrāṇāmāñjasyenetyata āha anirviśeṣita'; iti । abrahmasūtrasya'; iti samudāyaikavacanam । co avadhāraṇe yata ityarthe ca । aapi'; śabdo mukhyasūtratvasamuccaye । tathā ca yato brahmasūtrāṇāṃ mukhyasūtratvamasti ata eva hi anirviśeṣitasūtratvaṃ'; nirgatā viśeṣā yasmāttannirviśeṣaṃ tathākhyātaṃ nirviśeṣitaṃ tādṛśaṃ sūtrapadaṃ yasya tasya bhāvaḥ । yadvā viśeṣo viśeṣaṇaṃ, tasyābhāvo asya sañjātaḥ tādṛśaḥ sūtraśabdo yasya tasya bhāvo nirviśeṣitasūtratvam । viśeṣaṇarahitakevalasūtrapadavācyatvamasti purāṇādāvuktam । anyathā tanna syāt, vyāpakābhāve
vyāpyābhāvaniyamādityarthaḥ । atrādyapakṣe tathākhyātamityarthe ṇyantātkarmaṇi ktaḥ, dvitīye taddhitaḥ aitac'; iti vivekaḥ। anena brahmasūtrāṇāṃ mukhyasūtratve nirviśeṣitaśabdavācyatvāditi heturukto bhavati । atra hetoraprayojakatvamāśaṅkya vyāptivacanena tāṃ parihartuṃ tatra prathamaṃ yadyannanirviśeṣitaṃ tattanna mukhyamityanvayavyāptimabhipretya tatra dṛṣṭāntamāha ayathā'; iti । aeva'; ityanuvartate । tenaikaśabdārthasya mukhyatvasya vyāpakatā labhyate । tathā ca yathā ekasyaiva sataḥ kṛṣṇasya vedavyāsasya vyāsatvaṃ nirviśeṣitavyāsapadavācyatvamastītyarthaḥ । tathā ca nirviśeṣitatvānmukhyasūtratvaṃ brahmasūtrāṇāmiti vākyaśeṣaḥ । idānīṃ ye amukhyāḥ na te nirviśeṣapadavācyāḥ kintu saviśeṣapadavācyāḥ iti vyatirekavyāptimabhipretya tatra dṛṣṭāntamāha aanye'; iti । ayathā'; ityanuvartate । pūrvamekaśabdaśravaṇādatrāmukhyā iti labhyate । avyāsāḥ'; iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca yathā kṛṣṇāt aanye'; drauṇyādayo ye amukhyāste aviśeṣaṇāt'; eva viśeṣaṇamapekṣyaiva vyāsāḥ na tannairapekṣyeṇa । tṛtīyārthe vā pañcamī, saviśeṣaṇavyāsapadavācyā eveti yojanā ।

saviśeṣaṇasūtrāṇi hyaparāṇi vido viduḥ ।
nanvastu brahmasūtrāṇāṃ mukhyatvaṃ, tathāpi tadanyeṣāmapyasti, na teṣāmeva, itareṣāmamukhyatve kāraṇābhāvādityāśaṅkya, tatra nirviśeṣitatvahetoḥ samavyāptipareṇa tadarthameva prāguktavyatirekavyāptidṛṣṭāntavacanenopapāditānvayavyāptikamanumānaṃ niyāmakatvenāha asaviśeṣaṇa'; iti । aataḥ'; ityanuvartate । aparāṇīti cāvartate । ahi'; śabdo hetvarthe । tathā ca yataḥ aaparāṇi'; brahmasūtrebhyo anyāni sūtrāṇi aaparāṇi'; amukhyāni ata eva avido'; jñāninaḥ aaparāṇi'; asaviśeṣaṇasūtrāṇi'; viśeṣaṇasahitasūtrapadavācyānīti aviduḥ'; upajānantītyarthaḥ । tathā ca anyasūtrāṇāṃ saviśeṣaṇasūtratvāt amukhyatvameva, na mukhyatvamiti bhāvaḥ ।

mukhyasya nirviśeṣeṇa śabdo anyeṣāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
nirviśeṣitatvamukhyatvayoḥ saviśeṣaṇatvāmukhyatvayośca dṛṣṭāntamukhenopapāditāṃ vyāptiṃ dṛṣṭānte mukhyatvāmukhyatvayoḥ vedavibhāgagranthavistarakartṛtvatatsādṛśyādirūpānyakāraṇaprayojyatvasambhavādasiddhā vyāptirityāśaṅkāparihārāya pramāṇena sādhayati amukhyasya'; iti । evam aanyeṣām'; ityapi । tena mukhyatvāmukhyatvayorvyāpakatāsiddhiḥ । vācakatvaṃ ṣaṣṭhyarthaḥ । tathā ca yato mukhyasyaiva anirviśeṣeṇa'; viśeṣaṇābhāvena avācakaśabdo asti'; nirviśeṣitaśabdavācyatvamastīti yāvat । aanyeṣām'; amukhyānāmeva aviśeṣato'; viśeṣaṇamapekṣya, viśeṣaṇeneti vā, aśabdo'; vācakaḥ । saviśeṣaṇapadavācyatvamiti yāvat ।

iti vedavidaḥ prāhuḥ śabdatattvārthavedinaḥ ।
aiti'; evaṃ prakāreṇa aśabdatattvārthavedinaḥ'; śabdasya yathābhūtārthajñānino avedavido'; vedārthajñāḥ vṛddhāḥ aprāhuḥ'; vadantītyarthaḥ । asya "ato ayeṣāṃ sūtratvamañjasā'; asaviśeṣaṇasūtrāṇi aparāṇi amukhyāni'; ityuktaṃ yuktam"iti vākyaśeṣeṇānvayaḥ । aviśeṣitaḥ'; iti kvacitpāṭhaḥ । viśeṣaṇaṃ prāpta iti tasyārthaḥ ।
tathā ca mukhyāmukhyayornirviśeṣaṇasaviśeṣaṇaśabdavācyatve vedo vṛddhavyavahāraśca pramāṇamityuktatvānna tayoḥ kāraṇāntaraṃ śaṅkyamiti bhāvaḥ ।

sūtreṣu yeṣu sarve api nirṇayāssamudīritāḥ ।
astvetatsūtratvamañjasā brahmasūtrāṇām । tathāpi vedārthanirṇayasya sūtrāntaraireva sambhavāt kiṃ brahmasūtrairiti codyasya kathaṃ ayeṣām'; ityanena parihāra ukta ityatastadvākyoktaṃ vivṛṇoti asūtreṣu'; iti । nimittasaptamī iyam । apiḥ abhivyāptau saṅkocanivartakaḥ । nirṇayasya sarvatvaṃ viṣayadvārā tasya ca śabdadvārā bodhyam । tathā ca yebhyaḥ sūtrebhyaḥ sarve nirṇayāḥ sarvaśākhārthanirṇayāḥ bhāvyatayā samudīritāḥ, yeṣāṃ sarvaśākhānirṇāyakatvamuktaṃ
pramāṇa ityarthaḥ । yadvā nirṇīyanta iti nirṇayāḥ nirṇetavyārthāḥ । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ ayeṣām'; iti vākye tāvat brahmasūtrāṇāmevāñjasā sūtratvamityuktam । sati caivaṃ tadantargataṃ sūtradharmatayoktaṃ viśvatoṇukhatvamapi teṣāmevāñjasā bhavati । yadā caivaṃ tadā teṣāmasaṅkucitasarvaśākhānirṇāyakatvamuktaṃ bhavet, katipayaśākhānirṇāyakatve āñjasyānupapatteḥ । yata evamataḥ sarvavedaśākhārthanirṇāyakānāṃ brahmasūtrāṇām asarvanirṇāyakebhyo anyasūtrebhyo atiśayena nirṇāyakatvāt yuktaṃ atasyārthavittaye brahmasūtrāṇi cakāra'; iti । tacchabdaghaṭitaṃ tadvacanaṃ tādarthyena sūtrakaraṇavacanamiti bhavati tena śaṅkāparihāra iti ।

śabdajātasya sarvasya yatpramāṇaśca nirṇayaḥ ।
anyeṣāmapi dvitraśākhānirṇāyakatvāt kathameteṣāmeva sarvaśākhānirṇāyakatvamityucyate? anyathā tadvaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt । tathā ca aṃśe gatārthatetyāśaṅkāparihārāyāñjasyoktyā sūcitamanyaccāha aśabdajātasya'; iti। pūrvamīmāṃsādirūpasyetyarthaḥ । ata evoktaṃ sudhāyām "etanmīmāṃsopajīvinī khalu seti purāṇe paṭhyate śabdajātasyeti"iti । kartari ṣaṣṭhīyaṃ na karmaṇi । ata eva ṭīkāyāṃ śabdasamūhairiti tṛtīyā । kartṛtvaṃ ca karaṇībhūtavedetikartavyatayā । itikartavyatvaṃ ca mīmāṃsādvārā upakārakatvāt bhavati । śabdajātapadaṃ śabdapramāṇamātraparamityāśayena sambandhaṣaṣṭhīyam, sambandhaśca janyajanakabhāvaḥ iti kecit । yatpramāṇaṃ mūlaṃ yasya sa tathoktaḥ । aca'; śabdassamuccaye, asamudāhṛtaḥ'; ityasyānukarṣakaśca । itiśabdo adhyāhāryaḥ । tathā ca anyeṣāṃ dvitraśākhānirṇāyakatve api bhavatyeva brahmasūtrāṇāmevānanyāpekṣāsaṅkucitasarvaśākhānirṇāyakatvam, anyakartṛkadvitraśākhārthanirṇayasya brahmasūtramūlatvena tajjanyanirṇayopajīvitvena anyeṣāṃ śrutivyākhyānarūpatvāt । yathā śrutimūlakasmṛteravaiyarthyaṃ tadvadavaiyarthyopapattermūlena mūlino vaiyarthyābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ ।

evaṃvidhāni sūtrāṇi kṛtvā vyāso mahāyaśāḥ ।
aevaṃvidhāni'; iti । añjasā viśvatomukhatvādyupetānītyarthaḥ । asyopasaṃhārarūpatvānna atāni cakāra'; ityanena punaruktiḥ ।

brahmarudrādideveṣu manuṣyapitṛpakṣiṣu ।
adeveṣu'; ityanena karmajājānajadevadevagandharvā api saṅgṛhītāḥ । manuṣyapadaṃ "nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ" ityādāviva mananaśīlarṣiparam । pāntīti pāḥ cakravartinaḥ । kṣīti kṣayārthasya kṣeḥ rūpaṃ manuṣyottamavācakam, teṣāmitarāpekṣayā atyalpāyuṣṭvāt । manuṣyagandharvāṇāmapyupalakṣakametat । manuṣyāśca pitaraśca pāśca kṣayaśceti vigrahaḥ । anena adevarṣipitṛpanarāḥ'; ityuktāḥ pañcavidhā api muktiyogyāḥ saṅgṛhītā bhavanti । pakṣītyasyākhaṇḍatve pakṣiśabdo jaritāryādiyogyatiryakparaḥ ।

jñānaṃ saṃsthāpya bhagavān krīḍate puruṣottamaḥ ।
ajñānaṃ'; samyagjñānaṃ viśeṣajñānaṃ asaṃsthāpya'; utpādya dṛḍhīkṛtveti vā । dṛḍhīkaraṇaṃ nāma jñānaviṣaye saṃśayaviparyayanirāsaḥ । tathā ca puruṣottamo mahāyaśāḥ uttamaśloko bhagavān vyāso yeṣu sūtreṣu sarve nirṇayāḥ samudīritāḥ, yeṣāṃ sarvaśākhānirṇāyakatvamuktam, tathā sarvaiḥ śabdasamūhaiḥ jaiminyādisūtrāntarātmakairnirṇāyakaiḥ smṛtyādibhiśca kriyamāṇo lokakartṛkavedaikadeśāvāntaratātāparyanirṇayo yanmūlako yajjanyasarvavedamahātātparyanirṇayamūlakaḥ tadupajīvī taṃ vinā avāntaratātparyajñānamātreṇa muktiphalāsiddheriti coktaṃ ayeṣāṃ'; iti pūrvavākye pramāṇe ca evaṃvidhāni etādṛkprakārāṇi sūtrāṇi kṛtvā brahmarudrādideveṣu manuṣyapitṛpakṣiṣu jñānaṃ saṃsthāpya krīḍata iti mahāvākyayojanā । akrīḍate parameśvaraḥ'; iti pāṭhe aiśvaryam evaṃvidhasūtrakaraṇe asāmarthyaśaṅkānirāsakatayoktamiti dhyeyam । atra brahmādiṣu jñānasaṃsthāpanaṃ nāma pūrvaṃ sthitasyaiva jñānasya viśeṣayuktyādibhiḥ dṛḍhīkaraṇaṃ kiñcidaprāptalābhaścocyate ajānanto api viśeṣārthajñānāya sthāpanāya vā'; iti gītātātparyodāhṛtavacanāt । na ca aevaṃ jñānaṃ punaḥ prāpurdevāśca ṛṣayastathā'; iti bhāratatātparyaniraṇayavirodhaḥ, atra punaśśabdātsarvadevādīnāṃ ajñātavismṛtārthajñānaprāpteruktatvāditi vācyam, tasyāpyuktārthatvāt । viriñcetareṣāṃ tirohitārthajñānalābho vātrocyate, yata āhurgītātātparye ācāryāḥ "brahmaṇastu prāyo nāpratibhāsitam"iti । aityādi'; ityasya ataccoktam'; ityanenānvayaḥ । luptavibhaktiko ayaṃ nirdeśaḥ ।

athāto brahmajijñāsā ।
pramāṇābhāvena jīvacaitanyātiriktabrahmaṇo abhāvāt, jīvasya ca svaprakāśatvenāsandigdhatvāt, tathā ca viṣayābhāvāt pratyagrūpe brahmaṇyahamiti pratīyamāne api mokṣānuphalambhena prayojanābhāvāt tata eva tatpratibaddhādhikāryabhāvācca na brahmajijñāsā kartavyeti prāpte siddhāntitaṃ bhagavatā sūtrakāreṇa
om
athāto brahmajijñāsā ।
om iti ।
idamekaṃ sūtramekamadhikaraṇam । adhikaraṇaṃ nāma viṣayasaṃśayapūrvapakṣasiddhāntaprayojanarūpapañcāṅgasamudāyaḥ । yathātraiva jijñāsādhikaraṇe "tadvijijñāsasva"iti jijñāsābhidhāyakavākyavihitā śravaṇādirūpā jijñāsā viṣayaḥ । kartavyā na veti sandehaḥ । na kartavyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । asmin pakṣe ca śāstrasyānārambhaṇīyatvaniścayaḥ phalam । kartavyeti siddhāntaḥ ।
tatra cārambhaṇīyatvanirṇayaḥ phalaṃ, nyāyānusandhānātmakamīmāṃsārūpajijñāsāyāḥ akartavyatve nyāyagrathanātmakamīmāṃsāśāstrasyānārambhaṇīyatvāvaśyaṃbhāvāt ।
ekasyādhikaraṇasya saṅgatipañcakam । tacca śāstrasaṅgatiḥ, adhyāyasaṅgatiḥ, pādasaṅgatiḥ, pūrvādhikaraṇasaṅgatiḥ, tadviṣayavākyasaṅgatiścetyevaṃrūpam । saṅgatirapi sāmānyato dvividhā, antarbhāvarūpā ānantaryalakṣaṇā ceti । tatra śāstrādhyāyapādairantarbhāvarūpā saṅgatiḥ । pūrvādhikaraṇatadviṣayavākyābhyāṃ tu ānantaryarūpā । sāpi ākṣepikī ātideśikī aupodghātikī āpavādikī prāsaṅgikī ityādirūpeṇa bahuvidhā । tatra pañcādhikaraṇīparyantaṃ śāstrasaṅgatimātraṃ, nādhyāyapādasaṅgatī । samanvayekṣatyoradhyāyena saṅgatisatve api pādenābhāvātsaṅgatyorabhāvaḥ pañcādhikaraṇīsādhāraṇaḥ । tathā pūrvādhikaraṇatadviṣayasaṅgatī api naitadadhikaraṇasya bhavataḥ, asyaivādyādhikaraṇatvāt śrutivicārasyādyāpyanārabdhatvācca; kintvitareṣāṃ caturṇāmiti dhyeyam ।
atra sūtre ādyantayoroṅkāraḥ uccāraṇīyaḥ tatrādya eka eva dṛṣṭādṛṣṭobhayārthaḥ ata eva sūtrāvayavaḥ sarvasūtreṣu anuvṛttyarthamasaṃhitatayoccāryate । athavā ādau oṃkāradvayaṃ adṛṣṭārtho dṛṣṭārthaśceti । ante tu pakṣadvaye api adṛṣṭārtha eka evoṅkāraḥ । adṛṣṭārthatvaṃ nāma kevalaṃ sravaṇaviśaraṇarūpadoṣaparihārārthatvam । dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ tu anvetavyapadārthapratipādakatvam । tatrādisūtrāvayavabhūtaṃ aoṃ'; ityetat avyayaṃ brahmaśabdaviśeṣaṇaṃ guṇapūrṇatvavāci । brahmaśabdo api vidvadrūḍhyā mahāyogena ca viṣṇuvācī । aatha'; śabda ānantaryārthaḥ । yogyatayā aadhikārāt'; iti sambadhyate । tathā ca aatha'; adhyayanaśamadamādirūpādhikārānantaraṃ aataḥ'; svajanmajñānajanyaprasādajanyamokṣākhyaphalayuktatvāt aoṃ'; guṇapūrṇasya abrahmaṇo'; viṣṇoḥ ajijñāsā'; śravaṇādirūpo vicāraḥ kartavya iti sūtrārthaḥ । viṣṇoḥ prasādāditi aataḥ'; śabdasyārthāntaram । asya jijñāsādikāryaṃ bhavediti vākyaśeṣeṇānvayaḥ । oṃ brahmaśabdayorubhayoryaugikatve api ekasya rūḍhatvena viśeṣyavācitvaṃ anyasya yaugikatvena viśeṣaṇavācitvamāśrityānvayāṅgīkārānnānyataravaiyarthyam । "omityetadakṣaramudgīthamupāsīta"tadvijijñāsasva । tadbrahmeti"ityādyanekaviṣayavākyasaṅgrahāya cobhayoḥ prayogaḥ ।

athaśabdo maṅgalārtho adhikārāntaryārthaśca ।
ataśśabdo hetvarthaḥ ।
granthādau maṅgalācaraṇasyāvaśyaṃ kartavyatvena maṅgalaprayojakatayā athaśabdaṃ vyācaṣṭe aatha'; iti । maṅgalaṃ vighnotsāraṇāsādhāraṇakāraṇānuṣṭheyaviṣṇusmaraṇāthaśabdoccāraṇarūpamarthaḥ prayojanaṃ yasya, tathā praśastarūpānuṣṭheyamaṅgalātmako viṣṇuḥ tadguṇo vābhidheyo yasya sa tathoktaḥ । athaśabdasya maṅgalaphalakatvaṃ tu 
oṅkāraścāthaśca dvāvetau brahmaṇaḥ purā ।
kaṇṭhaṃ bhittvā viniryātau tasmānmāṅgalikāvubhau ।
iti manusmṛtisiddham । muktyarthimātrasya brahmajijñāsāyāṃ pravṛttinirasanatātparyeṇāpi prayuktasyākhaṇḍāthaśabdasya vācyamarthamāha aadhikāra'; iti । ca śabdo anuṣṭheyānanuṣṭheyākṣarārthavivakṣayā samuccaye, na kevalaṃ maṅgalaprayojakaḥ kintvānantaryābhidhāyakaśceti viṣayasamuccaye vā ।
yadvā avadhāraṇe caśabdaḥ । tenānuṣṭheyamaṅgalārambhapraśnakārtsnyārthanirāsaḥ । tatprakārastu candrikāyāmuktaḥ । tathā cādhikārānantaryamartho abhidheyo yasya sa tathoktaḥ । athaśabdasyānantaryamātrārthatve api adhikāretipadasya yogyatayā sambandhāt evamuktiḥ । anenānadhikāriṇo muktyarthimātrasya brahmavicāre pravṛttirnirastā bhavati । brahmajijñāsāyāḥ prayojanakāraṇaśūnyatāśaṅkānivartakatayā ataḥśabdaṃ vyācaṣṭe aataḥ'; iti । heturliṅgamartho yasya, hetuḥ kāraṇaṃ prasādākhyamartho yasyeti vā, sa tathoktaḥ ।

uktaṃ ca gāruḍe 
nanvathātaḥ śabdapūrvakatvaṃ sūtrāṇāṃ kiṃ nimittaṃ vighnanivartakaśabdoccāraṇādeḥ "maṅgalaṃ tataḥ"iti śabdāntaroccāraṇenāpi sambhavādityāśaṅkāṃ purāṇavacanenaiva nirākaroti auktañca'; iti । yadetat "athaśabdaḥ"ityādinoktaṃ tadgāruḍapurāṇe uktamevetyarthaḥ । na kevalamasmābhiḥ, kintu gāruḍe ceti samuccaye vā ca śabdaḥ ।

athātaśśabdapūrvāṇi sūtrāṇi nikhilānyapi ।
prārabhante niyatyaiva tatkimatra niyāmakam ।

kimuktamityastatpaṭhati aatha'; iti । yādṛcchikatvāparaparyāyāniyatatvaśaṅkāvāraṇāya aniyatyaiva'; iti । anikhilāni'; ityetat asūtrāṇi'; ityasya saṅkocavārakaṃ viśeṣaṇam । evakāro aniyamavyavṛttyarthaḥ । tathā ca he avidvan'; ādikave abrahman'; caturmukha anikhilānyapi'; vyāsajaiminyādikṛtāni sarvāṇyapyādisūtrāṇi aniyatyaiva'; niyamenaiva kalpāntarepi aathātaśśabdapūrvāṇi'; eva, athātaśśabdau pūrvau prathamaprayojyau yeṣu tathāvidhānyeva aprārabhante'; sūtrakārāḥ । aatra'; prathamaprayojyatve niyamena prathamaprayoge kenacinniyāmakena bhāvyaṃ, tanniyāmakaṃ kimiti praśnavākyayojanā ।

kaścārthaśca tayorvidvan kathamuttamatā tayoḥ ।
nanvavaśyavaktavyārthatvaṃ svarūpottamattvam arthata ādhikyaṃ vā niyāmakaṃ bhaviṣyatītyāśaṅkyādyapakṣe pṛcchati akaśca'; iti । caḥ praśnasamuccaye, avadhāraṇe vā । dvitīyastuśabdārthaḥ arthasyāvaśyavaktavyatvarūpaviśeṣamāha । tuśabdapāṭhastu svarasaḥ । tathā ca atayoḥ'; athātaḥśabdayoḥ ko asāvavaśyavaktavyo arthaḥ yena prāthamyamityarthaḥ । dvitīyamākṣipati akathaṃ'; iti । auttamatā'; svarūpataścādhikyam । na kathamapītyarthaḥ । evaṃ kathaṃśabdasya praśnaparatvamaṅgīkṛtya tṛtīyapakṣapraśnaparatvenāpi kathamityetadyojanīyam । tathā ca tayorathātaḥśabdayoḥ arthataḥ uttamatā ādhikyaṃ
kathamityarthaḥ । atra ādyatṛtīyapakṣayoravaśyavaktavyārthatārthādhikyayostadabhāvayośca loke śabdāntareṣu darśanāt athātaśśabdayostatsandehāt praśna eva na tvākṣepaḥ । dvitīyapakṣe tu svarūpādhikyasya śabdāntareṣvadarśanāt ākṣepa eveti dhyeyam । atroṅkārasya praśnādyaviṣayatvaṃ sarvaśāstrādisūtrāvayavatvābhāvāt, asravati'; iti śrutyā asisṛkṣoḥ'; ityādismṛtyā caitacchāstramātramukhyāditvena siddhatvāccetyavadheyam।

etadākhyāhi me brahman yathā jñāsyāmi tattvataḥ ।
evamukto nāradena brahmā provāca sattamaḥ ।

aetat'; praśnākṣepaviṣayībhūtaṃ niyāmakaṃ aahaṃ tattvato'; yāthārthyena ayathā jñāsyāmi'; tathā ame'; mahyaṃ aākhyāhi'; brūhiti aevaṃ nāradenoktaḥ'; pṛṣṭaḥ ākṣiptaśca asattamaḥ'; sajjīvottamaḥ abrahmā'; pratyuvācetyarthaḥ ।

ānantarye adhikārasya maṅgalārthe tathaiva ca ।
jijñāsādhikārasyāvaśyavaktavyatvena taddhetutāsādhakānantaryasya jijñāsāhetostatkartavyatāhetoścāvaśyavaktavyatvāttadarthakatvāttayoḥ prathamaprayoga iti parihāramabhipretyāvaśyavaktavyārthatvaṃ athātaśśabdayordarśayati aānantarye'; iti । parasparasamuccaye tathā caśabdau । evakāro bhinnakramaḥ; tenābhidheyontaraṃ vyāvartyate । tathā ca sautrāthaśabdaḥ aadhikārasyānantarye'; adhikāranirūpitānantaryarūpārthe tadviṣaye tanmātravācakatvābhiprāyeṇaiva sūtrakāraiḥ asamudīritaḥ'; prayukto na maṅgalādivācakatvenetyarthaḥ । avaśyakartavyaprayojanakatvācca prathamamathaśabdaprayoga iti bhāvenāthaśabdo maṅgalārtha iti svoktārthe pramāṇaṃ darśayati amaṅgalārthe'; iti । caturthyarthe saptamīyaṃ, avyayaṃ vā । arthaśabdaḥ prayojanavācī । tathā ca maṅgalarūpaprayojanārthaṃ ca athaśabdaḥ sūtrakāraissamudīritaḥ prayukto bhavedityarthaḥ। viṣṇuvācakākāraghaṭitāthaśabdoccāraṇarūpamaṅgalasya tatsādhyatvāditi bhāvaḥ । ānantarya itivat amaṅgale'; ityanuktvā aartha'; iti vacanaṃ tadvaiṣamyasūcanārtham । svavākye pramāṇakramātikramastu maṅgalasya prathamamanuṣṭheyatvāt kṛtaḥ ।

athaśabdastvataśśabdo hetvarthe samudīritaḥ ।
evamathaśabdasya avasyavaktavyārthatvarūpaṃ prathamaprayoganiyāmakaṃ pradarśya ataḥśabdasyāpi taddarśayati aataḥśabdastu hetvarthe'; iti । tuśabdo viśeṣārthaḥ । heturliṅgaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca sa cāsāvartho abhidheyaśca tasmin tadviṣaye tadvācakatayā sūtrakṛdbhiḥ asamudīritaḥ'; ityarthaḥ । gurvarthadīpikāyāntu "hetvarthe iti svavākye pramāṇe ca ataddhetutvaṃ vadan'; ityuttaravākyānusārāt bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ"ityuktam । tanniṣphalam । tathā ca vyākhyāsyāmaḥ । hetāvityanuktvā arthaśabdagrahaṇaṃ śabdādhikyādarthādhikyamiti nyāyena prakṛterheturarthaḥ pratyayasya tu hetutvamartha iti prakṛtipratyayobhayārthakathanārtham । yadvā arthaśabdasyobhayatra śravaṇātsa pūrvatrāpyanuṣañjanīya iti jñāpanāya, tadarthamātraṃ bhinnamiti dhyeyam ।

parasya brahmaṇo viṣṇoḥ prasādāditi vā bhavet ।
atra ataśśabdasyāvaśyavaktavyamarthāntaraṃ cāha aparasya'; iti । vāśabdaḥ samuccaye । uktaṃ hi prameyadīpe "vāśabdaścārthaḥ"iti । uktaṃ hi "yadi vā bhedabhinnayoḥ"iti viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāyāṃ
"vāśabdassamuccayārthaḥ"iti । tathā tattvapradīpe api "suptau mokṣe vā"ityatra "vāśabdassamuccayārthaḥ"iti । anena aataḥ'; ityetat aa'; śabdaprakṛtikaṃ tasilantaṃ padam, prakṛtyartho viṣṇuḥ, aprasādāt'; iti tu labdhārthakathanaṃ, kāraṇatvaṃ pratyayārtha ityuktaṃ bhavati । aparavyāvṛtyarthaṃ aparasya'; iti । "a iti brahma" iti śrutiṃ sūcayati parabrahmagrahaṇena । tatsthabrahmaśabdavyākhyānāya parasya brahmaṇa ityanuvādena viṣṇorityuktam । prasādādityanantaraṃ tajjijñāsādirūpaṃ kāryamiti śeṣaḥ । bhavedityasya ityarthe api ataḥśabdaḥ ityanvayaḥ । ataḥśabdaprakṛtyarthasya phalasya yathā jijñāsākartavyatve liṅgatvaṃ, na tathā tadarthaprasādasya, kintu kartavyajijñāsāyāṃ jñānamokṣayorathaśabdārthādhyayanādau ca kāraṇatvenānvaya ityāśayena pṛthaguktiḥ । yadyapi hetvarthe ityanenaivāyamartho labhyeta, hetuśabdasya liṅgakāraṇobhayārthatvāt; tathāpi asādhāraṇāsarvanāmaprakṛtikaśabdena bodhanārtamidamityadoṣaḥ ।

sa hi sarvamanovṛttiprerakassamudāhṛtaḥ ।
nanu jijñāsādyarthaṃ kiṃ bhagavatprasādena yenāsāvavaśyavaktavyārthaḥ syādityata āha asa hi'; iti । ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇuprasādaḥ prasanno viṣṇuriti yāvat asarvamanovṛttiprerakaḥ'; sarveṣāṃ adhikāriṇāṃ sarvasmin pūrṇe viṣṇau manovṛtteḥ prerakaḥ prāvaṇyahetuḥ asamudāhṛtaḥ'; prāmāṇikairityarthaḥ । jijñāsāpi sākṣātpramāṇadvārā vā manovṛtteḥ prāvaṇyameva, "jijñāsāpi saiva"iti sudhokteḥ । evaṃ sarvāsāṃ manovṛttīnāṃ tatprabhedānāṃ ṭīkāsthādipadagṛhītānāṃ jñānādhyayanādīnāṃ manovṛttisādhyamokṣādeśca prerakaḥ sampādakaḥ ityapi vyākhyeyam । asya tasmāttadarthepyataśśabdo bhavediti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ।

sisṛkṣoḥ paramādviṣṇoḥ prathamaṃ dvau vinismṛtau ।
oṅkāraścāthaśabdaśca tasmātprāthamikau kramāt ।

nanu maṅgalācaraṇādeḥ "maṅgalaṃ tataḥ"iti śabdāntareṇāpi sambhavātkimetatprayoganiyatyeti kṛtacodyasya kaḥ parihāra ityato na kevalamavaśyavaktavyārthatvādathātaḥśabdayoḥ prathamaprayogaḥ, kintu svarūpādhikyāccetyāśayena akathamuttamatā'; ityasyottaratvena tayoḥ svarūpādhikyamāha asisṛkṣoḥ'; iti । śabdayoṛ samuccaye ādyaḥ caśabdaḥ । nimittasamuccaye dvitīyaḥ । asvarūpottamau'; iti śeṣaḥ । atasmāt'; ityāvartate । tathā ca yasmāt asisṛkṣoḥ'; sraṣṭumicchoḥ aparamāt'; sarvottamāt aviṣṇoḥ'; tanmukhāt aprathamaṃ'; svasamānajātīyaśabdāntarotpatteḥ pūrvaṃ oṅkāro atha śabdaścetyetau kaṇṭhaṃ bhittvā avinissṛtau'; viniryātau, tasmātsvarūpottamau, tasmātsvarūpottamatvādeva aprāthamikau'; prathamaṃ prayojyāviti yojanā । atrākṣepāviṣayasyāpyoṅkārasya svarūpādhikyoktirbrahmamīmāṃsāśāstramātramukhyāmukhyāditvavivakṣayā pravṛttaṃ asarva ete'; iti vakṣyamāṇamanusṛtyeti draṣṭavyam । nanu dvayorekavidhaṃ prāthamikatvaṃ viruddhamityata uktaṃ akramāt'; iti । ādimadhyakramādityarthaḥ । tatroṅkārasya mukhyaṃ prāthamikatvaṃ, athaśabdasya dvitīyatayā mukhyamiti dhyeyam ।

taddhetutvaṃ vadaṃścāpi tṛtīyo ata udāhṛtaḥ ।
athaśabdasya oṅkāreṇa saha svarūpādhikayamabhidhāya ataḥśabdasyāpi tadāha atat'; iti । ataddhetutvaṃ vadan'; iti ahetvarthe'; ityasyānuvādaḥ । sa coddeśyasamarpakasya ata ityasya śabdaparatvajñāpanadvārā tṛtīyatayoktatvādividhānārthaḥ anyathā svarūpādhikyakathanadaśāsaṅgatiḥ syāt । yadyapi purovādānusārāt ataddhetutvaṃ vadan'; iti suvacam; tathāpi hetuśabdasya liṅgārthatvapakṣe tatsvarūpaṃ vivarituṃ kāraṇārthatvapakṣe tatkāryaṃ tasipratyayārthaṃ ca pradarśayituṃ ataddhetutvaṃ vadan'; ityuktam । atrātaḥśabdo asakṛdāvartate । tatraikaśśabdaparaḥ, anyo hetau, aparo viṣṇuparaḥ । atra śabdaparasyātaśśabdasya samuccayārthena apiśabdenānvayaḥ । atṛtīyaḥ udāhṛtaḥ'; ityanayorāvṛttiḥ । aprāthamikau'; ityasya vacanavyatyayenānuṣaṅga । tṛtīyaśabdo bhāvapradhānaḥ, vibhaktivyatyayaśca । tathā ca na kevalamoṅkārāthaśabdau, kintu ataddhetutvaṃ'; tasya prasannasyākāravācyasya viṣṇostatra jijñāsādau kāraṇatvaṃ tasipratyayena vadanprakṛtyaiva tasya jijñāsādermokṣahetutvarūpaṃ liṅgaṃ vā vadan aataḥ'; sarvanāmāsarvanāmaprakṛtiko ataśśabdo api yato viṣṇoḥ atṛtīyaḥ'; tṛtīyatayā audāhṛtaḥ'; uccāritaḥ ataḥ so api svarūpottamaḥ; yata evamato ataśśabdo api tṛtīyatayā prāthamika udāhṛta iti yojanā । tathā ca maṅgalaśabdena maṅgaloktāvapi tasya svarūpādhikyānukteḥ athātaḥśabdābhyāmivādhikāraprayojanayoranukteśca na tena gatārthatā, adhikāraprayonasūcanārthaṃ tayoravaśyāpekṣitatvāt । ata eva ṭīkāyāṃ "maṅgaloktyādeḥ"ityādiśabdaḥ tataśśabdena hetvānantaryapratiyogyadhikārasūcane api na tasyādisūtre niveśā yuktaḥ, tasya svarūpādhikyānuktereveti bhāvaḥ ।

akārassarvavāgātmā parabrahmābhidhāyakaḥ ।
na kevalamavaśyavaktavyārthatvāt nāpi svarūpādhikyāt athātaśśabdayoḥ prathamaprayogaḥ, kintvavayavārthataśca । ato api prathamaprayoga iti bhāvena kathamiti tṛtīyapraśnasya prākarāntareṇottaramāha aakāraḥ'; iti । tayorityanuvartate । tathā ca athātaśśabdayossambandhī aakāro'; yataḥ asarvavāgātmā'; atasmātsarvaguṇān viṣṇoḥ akāro vakti yatprabhoḥ'; ityaitareyabhāṣyadiśā sarvāsāṃ vācāmartho yatpūrṇatvaṃ tadabhidhāyakaḥ, ataḥ parabrahmābhidhāyakaḥ guṇapūrṇatvadharmiṇa eva parabrahmatvāt, dharmadharmiṇorabhedācceti bhāvaḥ।

tathau prāṇātmakau proktau vyāptisthitividhāyakau ।
evaṃ tayoḥ atathau'; taśca thaśca varṇau aprāṇātmakau'; prāṇau, doṣātmakaḥ doṣa itivat । viśeṣaṇayoḥ pratyekamanvayaḥ । prāṇaśabdo vāyuviṣṇūbhayavācī । "mahataścaturmukhāt"itivat abhimānyabhimanyamānayoḥ, "ayaṃ vai lokaḥ prathamā mahānāmnī" itivadvācyavācakayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena aikyavyapadeśaḥ । asya nirūḍhatvajñāpanāya aātmaka'; śabdaḥ । proktāviti vācyatvābhimānitvayoḥ prāmāṇikatvamāha । kramabhaṅgastu vargakramānusārāt uccāraṇalāghavācca kṛtaḥ । paramātmavācitvaṃ ca tadguṇadvāretyāha avyāpti'; iti । tasyeti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca tasya akāravācyasya parabrahmaṇo vyāptisthityabhidāyakau ityarthaḥ । tathayoretatkrameṇa yojanīyam । atrākārārtho guṇavyāptiḥ, takārārtho deśakālavyāptiḥ, thakārasya tu avikāreṇa avasthitirartha ityarthabhedo jñātavyaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu atathau prāṇātmakaṃ prāptau'; iti pāṭhabhedamaṅgīkṛtya prāṇātmakaṃ prāṇapraṇetāraṃ viṣṇuṃ vācakatvena prāptāviti vyākhyātam । yadyapi sūtre praviṣṭasya sarvanāmaprakṛtikasya ataśśabdasya naivamavayavārthakathanaṃ yujyate, asarvanāmaprakṛtikasya tu aparasya'; ityanenaiva arthata ādhikyaṃ coktam । tathāpi athaśabdasya arthata ādhikyānukteḥ tadgatavarṇayoḥ asarvanāmaprakṛtikātaśśabdagatavarṇayośca vākyārthāpraviṣṭātiśayitārthāntaroktiriyamityadoṣaḥ ।

ataśca pūrvamuccāryāḥ sarva ete satāṃ matāḥ ।
astvevaṃ, tataḥ kimityata āha aataśca'; iti । co avadhāraṇe samuccaye ca । tatra athātaśśabdaviṣaye samuccayaḥ, oṅkāraviṣaye tu svarūpata ādhikyādevetyavadhāraṇārthateti dhyeyam । aete'; ityasya vivaraṇaṃ asarve'; omathātaśśabdā iti । aataḥ pūrvaṃ'; etacchāstrādāviti ataśśabdāvṛttyā anvayaḥ । akramāt'; ityatrāpi sambadhyate । auccāryāḥ'; ityevaṃ asatāṃ'; janānāṃ sammatā ityarthaḥ । yadvā asatāṃ'; mukhyānāṃ brahmasūtrāṇāṃ pūrvaṃ ādisūtre ityarthaḥ । na cātra "sakalasūtrakārairevameva prayuktatvāt"iti sudhāvirodhaḥ, tasyāthātaśśabdamātraviṣayatvāt । ata eva "etau"iti pūrvamuktvā sakalasūtrakārairevamevetyuktam, kramāntaraṃ vihāyāvādāvevetyarthaḥ । athaśabdasya sūtrakṛteti śeṣaḥ ।

athātaśśabdayorevaṃ vīryamājñāya tattvataḥ
sūtreṣu tu mahāprājñāstāvevādau prayuñjate ।

tatkimatretyādipraśnottaramupasaṃharati aatha'; iti । tuśabdo avadhāraṇe viśeṣe ca । aevaṃ'; iti uktaprakāreṇa avīryaṃ'; svarūpādhikyādimāhātmyaṃ aājñāya'; tattvato vijñāya asūtreṣu'; vicāraśāstrādiṣu sarveṣu atau'; athātaśśabdāveva natvanyaṃ aādau'; prathamameva aprayuñjate'; prayogaṃ kurvantītyarthaḥ । amahāprājñāḥ'; ityanena sūtrakṛtāṃ śabdamārātmyatattvajñāne asāmarthyaṃ nivārayati । evakāraḥ sarvaśāstrādisūtravivakṣayoṅkāravyavacchedakaḥ । ata eva aataśca'; iti trayāṇāṃ prakṛtatvepi oṅkāravaiṣamyajñāpanāya athātaśśabdayorevoktiḥ । ata eva athātaśśabdaviṣaye upakramopasaṃhārayoḥ anikhilāni sūtrāṇi'; asūtreṣu'; iti sarvasūtroktiḥ, oṅkāraviṣaye tu tadanuktiḥ । athaśabdasyoṅkāreṇa saha pāṭhe api na sārvatrikatvaṃ, upakramopasaṃhāravirodhāt । iti śabdasya uktamityanenānvayaḥ ।

adhikāraścokto bhāgavatatantre 
athaśabdo adhikārānantaryaṃ vaktītyuktaṃ; tatra kosāvadhikāro brahmajijñāsāyāṃ, katividhaśca sa ityata āha aadhikāraḥ'; iti । caśabdo na kevalamadhikāraḥ kintu tadvibhāgaśca bhāgavatatantrākhyagranthe abhihita iti samuccaye । atra pramāṇe adhikārikathane api tadviśeṣaṇatayā devatvādirūpo apyadhikāraḥ ukto bhavatīti nāsaṅgatiḥ।

mandamadhyottamatvena trividhā hyadhikāriṇaḥ ।
kathamityatastadvākyaṃ paṭhati amanda'; iti । tvaḥ pratyekaṃ sambadhyate । itthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇe tṛtīyā । hiśabdaḥ prasiddhau ।

tatra mandā manuṣyeṣu ya uttamagaṇā matāḥ ।
atatra'; trividheṣu madhye manuṣyeṣu ye uttamagaṇāḥ te mokṣayogyeṣu mandādhikāriṇa ityuddeśyavidheyabhāvo draṣṭavyaḥ । gaṇaśabdena puruṣārthanayoktatrividhamanuṣyottamā gṛhītāḥ ।

madhyamā ṛṣigandharvā devāstatrottamā matāḥ ।
ṛṣayaśca gandharvāśca aṛṣigandharvāḥ'; । bahuvacanamādyarthe । tena pitṛpayorgrahaṇam । punaḥ atatra'; ityasya aevaṃvidhāni'; itivadupasaṃhārarūpatvānna punaruktiḥ । yadvā prathamasya atatra'; ityasya brahmajijñāsāyāmityarthaḥ । ata evoktaṃ ṭīkāyāṃ "brahmajijñāsāyāṃ"iti । tathā ca atatra'; brahmajijñāsāyāmadhikāriṇastrividhāḥ, atatra'; trividheṣvityanvayaḥ । athavā "itiśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ abhisambadhyate, ata eva dvirgrahaṇaṃ"iti tatvodyotaṭīkārītyā madhyameṣvanuṣaṅgasūcanāyādyantayostatretyuktiḥ । atatra'; teṣāmadhikāriṇām ।।

iti jātikṛto bhedastathānyo guṇapūrvakaḥ ।
aiti'; evaṃ ajātikṛto'; manuṣyarṣidevatvādirūpasāmānyanimittakaḥ tattatkulajaninimitto vā abhedaḥ'; avāntaravibhāgaḥ anyonyābhāvo vā jñeya ityarthaḥ । anena mokṣayogyatvaṃ vaidikabrahmavidyādhikārisāmānyalakṣaṇamabhipretam । nanvidaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sacchūdrādau ativyāptam । na ca sacchūdrāderviprādidehāntare brahmavidyādhikāritvānnātivyāptiriti vācyam, dehāntare sato api adhikārasyedānīntanapravṛttyanupayogitvāt, taddehāvacchedena tu anutpannabrahmāparokṣajñānitvenāsyābhāvaniścayāt । tathā ca sacchūdrādāvasyādhikārasya prāyikatvādbāhulakatvāt, ata evaitaddehe abhāvāt ata evālakṣyatvāt, asya ca mokṣayogyatvasya svarūpatvenānadhikāraḥ daśāyāmapi sattvādvyāpterdhrauvyādityataḥ prakārāntareṇa adhikāriṇaḥ svarūpamāha atathā'; iti । aanyo'; jātikṛtabhedādbheda ityasti aguṇapūrvako'; bhaktyadhyayanādiśubhadharmanimitto astīti śeṣaḥ ।

bhaktimān parame viṣṇau yastvadhyayanavānnaraḥ ।
adhamaḥ śamādisaṃyukto madhyamassamudāhṛtaḥ ।

tameva darśayati abhaktimān'; iti । pūrvamuddeśavākye bahuvacananirdeśepyatra anaraḥ'; ityādyekavacananirdeśo nānupapannaḥ, asya lakṣaṇavākyatvāt, "pramāṇāni"ityuddeśavākye bahuvacananirdeśe api "pramākaraṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ"ityekavacanena lakṣaṇoktivat । atra avaiṣṇavasya vede api hyadhikāro na vidyate ।
gurubhaktivihīnasya śamādirahitasya ca ।
ityukteḥ । adhyayanalabdhāpi viṣṇubhaktiḥ śamādikañca abhaktānadhikārikṛtādhyayanaśamādinivṛtyarthaṃ pṛthamuktam । ādiśabdena "śānto dāntaḥ"ityuktānāṃ grahaṇam । sāranityasamuccaye cāpiśabdau । aiti'; iti śeṣaḥ । anaro'; bhaktajanaḥ । asya sarvatra sambandhaḥ । tathā ca yo naraḥ parame viṣṇau bhaktimān adhyayanavāṃśca so adhamo adhikārīti prāmāṇikaiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ । yaḥ śamādisaṃyukto naraḥ sa madhyama iti proktaḥ ।

ābrahmastambaparyantamasāraṃ cāpyanityakam ।
yaḥ aābrahmastambaparyantaṃ'; caturmukhamārabhya tṛṇajīvaparyantaṃ jīvajātaṃ aasāraṃ'; asarvottamaṃ, asārapadaṃ mokṣadavaraparaṃ vā aanityakaṃ'; anityaṃ brahmādijīvānāṃ dehanāśe api svarūpanāśābhāvāt kapratyayaḥ । parabrahma tu sarvasāraṃ sarvathā nityaṃ ceti ।

vijñāya jātavairāgyo viṣṇupādaikasaṃśrayaḥ ।
avijñāya'; jñānavān san sārāsāranityānityavastuvivekavāniti yāvat । yaśca tato vivekāt ajātavairāgyaḥ'; iti vijñāya janitavairāgya iti vā । yaśca aviṣṇupādaikasaṃśrayaḥ'; viṣṇupāda eva eko mukhyaḥ saṃśrayo mama śaraṇamiti jñānaṃ yasya saḥ ।

sa uttamodhikārī syātsaṃnyastākhilakarmavān ।
yaśca asannyastākhilakarmavān'; sannyastaṃ bhagavati samarpitaṃ akhilaṃ yadakāmyaṃ karma tadvān asaḥ'; naraḥ auttamo adhikārī'; syāditi yojanā । atra sannyāso nāma bhagavān sarvāṇi karmāṇi karoti sarvakarmāṇi bhagavatpūjārūpāṇīti ca jñātvā bhrāntyā jīvakartṛkatvena jñātānāṃ karmaṇāṃ bhagavati visargaḥ । yathoktaṃ gītābhāṣye "bhagavāneva sarvāṇi karmāṇi karoti"ityādinā । anena abhaktimān parame viṣṇau'; ityādi asannyastākhilakarmavān'; ityantavākyena yānyadhikāritrayaviśeṣaṇānyuktāni tānyeva sarvāṇi militvādhikārisāmānyalakṣaṇabhūtānītyuktaṃ bhavati। na ca militānāṃ trayāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ triṣvabhāvādasambhavaḥ, bhāve vādhamādilakṣaṇasya madhyamādiṣvativyāptyāpattiriti vācyam, uttaravākye pūrvasya pūrvavākye cottarasyānukarṣeṇa sarvatra sarvasya satvābhyupagamenāsambhavābhāvāt । nanvasaṅkīrṇaviśeṣalakṣaṇānuktestraividhyāyoga iti cet atra kecit "uttaroktāprācuryeṇa"iti ṭīkāvākyasyottarayoradhikāriṇoruktānāṃ guṇānāṃ pūrvasminnadhame aprācuryeṇetyarthamāśritya pracuratamādhyayanādiguṇatrayavattvamuttamatvaṃ, pracuratarādhyayanādiguṇatrayavattvaṃ madhyamatvaṃ, tadubhayabhinnakevalaguṇatrayavattvaṃ adhamatvaṃ ityasāṅkaryamāhuḥ । ta evottaratra saṅgṛhītāḥ pūrvatrānukṛṣṭāśca guṇā uttaroktāsteṣāṃ tatratatra bhaktimānityādiyathāsthitamūloktaguṇāpekṣayāprācuryeṇeti pakṣāntaramāhuḥ । candrikāyāṃ tu pūrvapūrvasmin uttarottarasminnuktāprācuryeṇeti ṭīkārthamāśritya samānādhikaraṇānāṃ adhyayanaśamadamādisampattiviṣṇupādaikasaṃśrayatvādīnāṃ madhye yaḥ pracurādhyayanavān itare tvapracure so adhamo adhikārī । yaḥ pracurādhyayanaśamādimān anyadekamevāpracuraṃ sa madhyamaḥ । yaḥ pracuraviṣṇupādaikasaṃśrayatvādimān itare tvapracure sa uttamādhikārīti tallakṣaṇamedāt traividhyopapattiriti uktam । aiti'; śabdasya abhāgavatatantre'; ityanenānvayaḥ ।

"adhyayanamātravataḥ । nāviśeṣāt"
iti copari । 
adhyayanaṃ brahmavidyādhikāra ityuktam । tatkutaḥ? udāhṛtapramāṇe brahmavidyāyāmiti kaṇṭhato anukteḥ kutaśca tatrādhikāratraividhyamityata āha aadhyayana'; iti । mātraśabdaḥ kārtsnyārthaḥ । tathā ca yathāśaktisarvavedādhyayanavato brahmavidyādhikāriteti sūtrārthaḥ । anāviśeṣāt'; ityaparaṃ sūtram । devādīnāṃ brahmavidyādhikāritā aviśeṣātsāmānyānna, kintu tāratamyādevetyarthaḥ । aupari'; tṛtīye adhikārastāratamyena vakṣyate, sūtrakṛteti śeṣaḥ । tadabhipretasmṛtau avedoktabrahmavidyāyām'; ityuktatvāt tatrodāhṛtaśrutau jñānādhikāritraividhyasyāpyuktatvāduktaśaṅkāparihāra iti bhāvaḥ । caśabdaḥ aadhyayanavān'; iti pramāṇasamuccaye ।

"śānto dānta uparatastitikṣuḥ samāhito bhūtvā ātmanyevātmānaṃ paśyet"
śamādikamapi brahmavidyāyādhikāra ityatra kāṇvaśrutimāha aśānta'; iti । atra aātmani'; ityuktyā madhyamādhikārī sūcitaḥ, aṛṣayo antaḥprakāśāḥ'; iti śruteḥ amadhyamā ṛṣigandharvāḥ'; ityukteśca । aśānto'; bhagavanniṣṭhabuddhiḥ "śamo manniṣṭhatā buddheḥ"iti bhāgavatokteḥ । tattvapradīpe tu vaiṣṇavasiddhāntādacalanaṃ śama iti paryavasitamuktam । adānto'; nigṛhītamadaḥ, indriyanigrahavāniti yāvat । auparato'; viṣayālambuddhimān । bṛhadbhāṣyarītyā upa samīpe svahṛdayesthe viṣṇau santoṣavāniti vā । atitikṣuḥ'; śītoṣṇādidvandvasahiṣṇuḥ । asamāhitaḥ'; same sendire harau cittavṛttimān । yadvā ayathāvastu tathā jñānaṃ tatsāmyātsamamīritam'; iti vacanāt samaṃ yathārthamāhitamādhānaṃ manovṛttirūpaṃ jñānaṃ icchā ca yasya sa tathoktaḥ । tathāca yathāvastujñānādimānityarthaḥ। bhūtvetyasya pratyekaṃ sambandhaḥ । sthitamiti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca pūrvaṃ aevaṃ'; vicchabdenokto hareḥ saṃsāramocakatvajñānīśāntyādimān abhūtvā'; aātmani'; svahṛdaye sthitaṃ aātmanaṃ'; paramātmānaṃ apaśyet'; jānīyādityarthaḥ, vicārayediti lākṣaṇikārthaḥ । śāntādirbhūtvātmānaṃ vidyādityanena upanayanasya adhyayanārthatvavat śāntyāderbrahmavidyārthatvamuktaṃ bhavati । yadyapi paśyatīti śrutipāṭhaḥ tathāpi viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāyāṃ "sa tathā cakāreti kvacitpāṭhaḥ sa sadṛśaśākhāntaragato jñātavyaḥ, evamanyatrāpi"ityuktatvāt tannyāyenāyamapi sadṛśaśākhāntaragato vā paśyatītyasyārthānuvādo vetyadoṣaḥ।।

parīkṣya lokān karmacitānbrāhmaṇo ।
nirvedamāyānnāstyakṛtaḥ kṛtena ।

sārāsāranityāvivekajanyavairāgyādyapi brahmavidyāyāmeva adhikāra ityatrātharvaṇaśrutimāha aparīkṣya'; iti । abrāhmaṇo'; brahmajñānayogyaḥ alokān'; viṣṇuloketarān akarmacitān'; kāmyakarmasampāditān tata evāsāratvenānityatvena ca aparīkṣya'; vivicya tena vivekena anirvedaṃ'; kāmyakarmaṇi tatphale ca vairāgyaṃ aāyāt'; prāpnuyāt । yasmātsvarūpānandāvirbhāvarūpatvāt aakṛto'; nityapumartharūpo mokṣaḥ akṛtena'; utpattināśavatphalatvenāvadhṛtakarmaṇā anāsti', kintu jñānena ।

tadvijñānārthaṃ sa gurumevābhigacchet ।
samitpāṇiḥ śrotriyaṃ brahmaniṣṭham ।

atat'; tasmāt asaḥ'; mokṣāditaratra viraktaḥ avijñānārthaṃ'; brahmaṇo viśeṣajñānāya । asamitpāṇiḥ'; samidyuktau pāṇī yasya । yadvā samprāptau sampuṭīkṛtau ariktau vā pāṇī yasya । sa evaṃbhūtassan aśrotriyaṃ'; chandodhyetāraṃ brahmaniṣṭhameva gurum aabhigacchet'; upasīdedityarthaḥ । gurumeva na tvanyamiti vā evaśabdānvayaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu akarmacitān'; karmaṇā sañcitān aihikān mandirādīn vināśinaḥ aparīkṣya'; parito vīkṣya pāralaukikatvena tadviparītānapi karmabhiścitān svargādilokān vināśina eva parīkṣya tebhyo anirvedamāyāt'; । aakṛto'; jñānipriyo bhagavān akṛtena'; karmaṇā ana'; labhyate । tataḥ atadvijñānārthaṃ'; tasya jñānipriyasya viṣṇorvijñānārthaṃ agurumabhigacchet'; iti śrutyartha uktaḥ । atrāpi vijñānapadena brahmajñāniparabrāhmaṇapadena ca uttamādhikārī sūcitaḥ, adevādīnāṃ tu tajjñānaṃ vijñānamiti kīrtitam'; iti gītābhāṣyokteḥ, anaiva devapadaṃ prāptāḥ brahmadarśanavarjitāḥ'; iti tattātparyokteśca ।

yamevaiṣa vṛṇute tena labhyaḥ
viṣṇubhaktirapi brahmavidyāyāmadhikāra ityetatkaṭhaśrutyā darśayati ayaṃ'; iti । ātharvaṇepīyaṃ paṭhyate ।
aeṣaḥ'; icchārūpaḥ aātmā'; viṣṇuḥ ayaṃ'; adhikāriṇaṃ avṛṇute'; parigṛhṇāti atena'; eva alabhyaḥ'; prāpyaḥ tasya prasanno bhavati ।

tasyaiṣa ātmā vivṛṇute tanūṃ svām ।
tataśca atasya'; adhikāriṇaḥ aeṣaḥ'; prasannaḥ aātmā svāṃ tanūṃ'; rupaṃ avivṛṇute'; prakāśayatītyarthaḥ। atra abhaktameva ca vṛṇuta iti prasiddhaḥ'; iti prameyadīpoktarītyā vṛṇuta ityanena bhaktatvaṃ sūcitam । tattvapradīpe tu ayamevaiṣaḥ'; paramātmā bhaktidānena avṛṇute'; svīkaroti atena'; prāpyo yatastasyaiva asvāṃ tanuṃ'; prakāśayatītyuktam ।

yasya deve parā bhaktiryathā deve tathā gurau ।
sā ca bhaktiḥ viṣṇau sarvādhikā anyeṣvapi yathāyogyā brahmavidyopayoginītyarthe śvetāśvatarāṇāṃ śrutiṃ darśayati ayasya'; iti । ayathā'; ityāvartate । atathā'; iti samuccaye । akathitāḥ'; aakathitāḥ'; iti dvedhā vicchedaḥ । pūrvavedādibhirguruṇeti ca śeṣaḥ । tathāca ayasya'; adhikāriṇo adeve'; dyotanādiguṇe viṣṇau aparā'; sarvādhikā abhaktiḥ'; asti atathā'; adeve'; taditaradeveṣu brahmādiṣu ayathā'; yathāyogyā bhaktirasti, atathā gurau'; anyeṣu svottameṣu ca yathā yogyā bhaktirasti ।

tasyaite kathitā hyarthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ ।
atasya'; mahātmanaḥ kartari ṣaṣṭhīyam । tenādhikāriṇā pūrvaṃ vedādibhirguruṇā vā akathitāḥ'; aete'; uktāḥ aarthāḥ'; parāparatattvarūpāḥ aprakāśyante'; jñāyanta ityarthaḥ । yadvā aete'; śamādirūpā aarthāḥ'; guṇāstasmin aprakāśyante'; dṛśyanta ityarthaḥ । atha vā aakathitāḥ'; gurubhiranupadiṣṭāḥ aarthāḥ'; asya bhaktivaśāt aprakāśyante'; ahi'; prasiddhamityarthaḥ । aprakāśante'; iti pāṭhe tatkartṛkajñānānukūlamānakartāro bhavantītyarthaḥ ।

ityādiśrutibhyaśca । vyomasaṃhitāyāṃ ca 
aityādiśrutibhyaśca'; ityasya aadhikāra uktaḥ'; ityanenānvayaḥ na kevalamuktaśrutibhiḥ, kintu "bhaktyā tvananyayā śakya ahamevaṃ vidhorjuna jñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ" ityādismṛtibhyaśceti
caśabdārthaḥ । nanu yadyadhyayanavatāmeva brahmavidyādhikāraḥ tarhi trivarṇetareṣāmadhyayanābhāvenādhikāro na syāt । tataśca teṣāṃ brahmajñānābhāvena mokṣābhāvassyādityāśaṅkāṃ smṛtyā pariharati avyomasaṃhitāyāṃ ca'; iti । prakṛtaśaṅkānirāsapūrvakamiti śeṣaḥ । pūrvagranthasamuccaye caśabdaḥ । asyāpi aadhikāra uktaḥ'; । ityanenānvayaḥ ।

antyajā api ye bhaktā nāmajñānādhikāriṇaḥ ।
ante bhavāḥ antyāḥ teṣu jātāḥ aantyajāḥ'; trivarṇabāhyāḥ । ayaṃ cārtho "viṣṇunāmasvādhyāyo antyānāṃ"ityetadavatārikārūpatayā "nāgnirna yajñaḥ śūdrasyetyādestrivarṇabāhyānāṃ"iti nyāyadīpikayā sūcitaḥ । abhaktāḥ'; iti bhaktimānityuktabrahmavidyādhikārakathanam । evaṃ abhaktimatāṃ'; ityapi। etaccobhayanvayi । tathā ca na kevalaṃ traivarṇikāḥ, kintu ye antyajāḥ trivarṇabāhyāḥ śūdrādayaḥ pulkasāntāḥ te yadyapi vaidikabrahmajñānānadhikāriṇaḥ, tathāpi yato bhaktāḥ ato nāmajñānādhikāriṇaḥ viṣṇunāmajñānatatsvādhyāyādhikāriṇaḥ, ataste brahmajñānamuktyadhikāriṇa iti yojanā ।

strīśūdrabrahmabandhūnāṃ tantrajñāne adhikāritā ।
traivarṇikeṣvapi vedānadhikāriṇāṃ keṣāñcit, antyajeṣvapi keṣāñcidbhaktimatāṃ, uktādanyaccāha astrīśūdrabrahmabandhūnām'; iti । striyaśca śūdrāśca brahmabandhavo brāhmaṇābhāsāśca teṣāmiti vigrahaḥ । tantraṃ pañcarātrādi, tajjñāne taduktārthajñāne, tantrotpannabrahmavidyāyāmiti yāvat । apiśabdo atrāpi sambadhyate । tathāca teṣāṃ tadjñānadvārāpi mokṣopapattiriti bhāvaḥ ।

ekadeśe parokte tu na tu granthapurassare ।
tantre api na sarvatrādhikāraḥ, kintu ekadeśe eva । tatrāpi ana granthapurassare'; na svaprādhānyena granthārambhe adhikāraḥ, kintu aparokte'; pareṇānyena parārthaṃ prokte ārabdha evetyāha aekadeśa'; iti । avadhāraṇe tuśabdaḥ । tadvyāvartyamāha ana tu'; iti । stryādimātrapuraskāreṇa prāpabhyamāṇatantragranbhādau teṣāṃ nādhikāritetyarthaḥ। anena strīśūdrādimātraṃ puraskṛtya purāṇādigranthapravacanamapi na kāryamityuktaṃ bhavati । dvitīyatuśabdasyottaratrānvayaḥ ।

traivarṇikānāṃ vedokte samyagbhaktimatāṃ harau ।
tarhi vedotpannabrahmavidyāyāṃ keṣāmadhikāraḥ? pariśeṣāt traivarṇikānāṃ cet teṣāmapi kiṃ sarveṣāmadhikāraḥ? na, kiṃ tu keṣāñcidityāha atraivarṇikānāṃ'; iti । avedokteḥ'; vedotpannabrahmajñāne tu aharau samyagbhaktimatāṃ'; eva atraivarṇikānāṃ'; uktetarabrahmakṣatriyavaiśyānāṃ adhikāritetyarthaḥ । na kevalaṃ nāmādijñānādhikāra ityarthepi tuśabdaḥ ।

āhurapyuttamastrīṇāmadhikāraṃ tu vaidike ।
"sapatnīṃ me parādhamapatiṃ me kevalaṃ kuru।" ityādau strīṇāmapi vedādhikāradarśanāt kathaṃ tāsāmanadhikāra ityata uktasyāpavādamāha aāhuḥ'; iti । turapyarthe api । avaidike'; ityasya vipariṇāmenāvṛttiḥ । auttamastrīṇāṃ'; iti tatpuruṣakarmadhārayau । tathāca na kevalamuttamānāṃ devānāṃ strīṇāṃ nāmādijñāne adhikāraḥ kintu vaidike api jñāne vedotpannabrahmavidyāyāmapi vaidikāḥ adhikāramāhuriti yojanā ।

yathorvaśī yamī caiva śacyādyāśca tathāparāḥ ।
tāḥ udāharati ayathā'; iti । aeva'; evaṃ ayamī'; yamasya bhāryā śyāmalā । caśabda uktasamuccaye । ādyaśabdena umāratyādi gṛhyate । anuktasamuccaye dvitīyaścaḥ, tena manuṣyādikulotpannadevastriyo gṛhyante । tathāśabdaḥ upamāyāṃ uktasamuccaye vā । aparāḥ uttamastrībhyo anyāḥ ṛṇipatnyaḥ । avarā iti vā, uttamadevastryapekṣayā madhyamaṛṣipatnīnāṃ avaratvāditi । avyomasaṃhitāyāṃ'; iti itiśabdānvayaḥ ।

yato nārāyaṇaprasādamṛte na mokṣaḥ,na ca jñānaṃ vinātyarthaprasādaḥ।
ato brahmajijñāsā kartavyā ।

evaṃ pratijñāpramāṇopanyāsābhyāṃ ānantaryapratiyogyadhikāravivaraṇamukhenāthaśabdaṃ saṃkṣepavistarābhyāṃ vyākhyāya sūtre akartavyā'; iti padaṃ ataśśabdaparāmarśanīyasamarpakaṃ ayataḥ'; ityādikaṃ cādhyāhāryamiti darśayan aataśśabdo hetvarthe'; iti saṅkṣepeṇoktamarthaṃ viśadayati ayataḥ'; iti । ayataḥ'; ityāvartate । tathāca yatassukhameva me syāt duḥkhamīṣadapi mābhūditi sarvābhimato amokṣaḥ'; samyañcaṃ anārāyaṇaprasādaṃ ṛte'; vinā nāsti, sa ca aatyarthaprasādaḥ'; atimātraprasādaśca nāparokṣajñānaṃ vinā, tacca na brahmajijñāsāṃ vinā, aato brahmajijñāsā kartavyā'; ityarthaḥ । uktaṃ hi śabdādhikaraṇe tattvapradīpe "mokṣasyaiva paramapuruṣārthatvāt tasya ca samīco vinā viṣṇuprasādāt alabhyatvāt tasya ca atimātrasya aparokṣajñānaprasādhyatvāt tasya cāparokṣasya jijñāsāsamāyattattvādviṣṇureva jijñāsya ityuktam"iti। sāvadhāraṇānvayasyāpyupalakṣakametat । tasyātaśśabdena parāmarśānnānupapattiḥ । anena sūtre yato nārāyaṇaprasādamṛte na mokṣaḥ, kintu prasādenaiva, na ca jñānaṃ vinātyarthaprasādaḥ, kintu jñānenaiva, na ca jijñāsāṃ vinā jñānaṃ, kintu jijñānayaiva, ato brahmajijñāsā kartavyetyanvayapradarśanamukhena ataśśabdasya mokṣasādhanaprasādasādhanajñānasādhanatvāditi heturartha ityetadvivṛtaṃ bhavati । evaṃ yato nārāyaṇaprasādamṛte na jñānaṃ na jijñāsā kintu prasādenaiva iti yojanāyāṃ ataḥśabdasyārthāntaramapi vivṛtaṃ bhavati । nārāyaṇaśabdaprayogeṇa sautrabrahmaśabdo api vyākhyāto bhavati ।

yatrānavasaronyatra padaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhitam ।
vākyaṃ veti satāṃ nītiḥ sāvakāśe na tadbhavatet ।

nanu sūtre akartavyā'; iti padasyaiva adhyāhāraḥ kutaḥ adhyāhārasya niraṅkuśatvena ana kartavyā'; iti vākyasyaivādhyāhāraḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha ayatra'; iti । atra yatreti tatreti padamiti cāvartate, tathā vākyamityapi, vinetyadhyāhriyate । tathā ca ayatra'; avāntaravākye yat apadaṃ'; vinā aanyatra'; arthāntare aanavasaraḥ'; aghaṭanā atatra'; vākye tadeva apadaṃ'; apratiṣṭhitaṃ'; prāptaṃ bhavet nānyaditi asatāṃ'; nyāyaḥ, yatra vākye yasmin vākye sāvakāśe arthāntare ghaṭanāvati sati tadeva padaṃ niyamena pratiṣṭhitaṃ prāptaṃ na bhavet । evaṃ yatra mahāvākye yadavāntaravākyaṃ vinānyatrānavasaraḥ tatra mahāvākye tadeva vākyaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ, yatra yasmin mahāvākye sāvakāśe sati tadavāntaravākyaṃ niyamena pratiṣṭhitaṃ na bhavedityarthaḥ । yatra vākye yatpadaṃ vākyaṃ vāpekṣitaṃ anyatrānyasyānavasara iti vā । iti bṛhatsaṃhitāyāmuktatvāt akartavyā'; iti padamevāvaśyamadhyāhartavyamiti vākyaśeṣeṇāsyānvayaḥ । ana kartavyā'; ityadhyāhāre athātaśśabdārthādhirārāderatrānvayāyogāditi bhāvaḥ । evaṃ candrikoktarītyā ayatra'; iti śloko ayataḥ'; ityādyadhyāhārasamarthanaparatayāpi vyākhyeyaḥ ।

"tamevaṃ vidvānamṛta iha bhavati, nānyaḥ panthā ayanāya vidyate"
yaduktaṃ ayato nārāyaṇaprasādaṃ'; ityanena prasādasya mokṣasādhanatvaṃ tatkuta ityatastatra śrutiṃ pramāṇayati ataṃ'; iti । aiha'; adhikārivarge prakṛtapuruṣaśabditaṃ ataṃ'; paramātmānaṃ aevaṃ'; sahasraśīrṣatvādyuktaprakāreṇa aiha'; loke avidvān'; parokṣajñānadvārā aparokṣato jānannevānte aamṛto'; mukto bhavati, yato nārāyaṇāyanāya tatprāptirūpamokṣārthaṃ aanyaḥ'; paramapuruṣajñānāt apanthāḥ'; upāyo ana vidyate'; nāsti ata ityarthaḥ । atra jñānasya mokṣasādhanatvaṃ sākṣāt jñāyate । prasādasya mokṣasādhanatvaṃ tu ṭīkāsudhoktarītyā prasādaṃ vinā vidvatpadalakṣyāparokṣajñānamātreṇa mokṣo na bhavatītyanyathānupapattyaiva, na tu sākṣāt । nimittena naimittikopalakṣaṇāvetyavagantavyam ।

"priyo hi jñāninotyarthamahaṃ sa ca mama priyaḥ"।
ana ca jñānaṃ vinā'; iti yadaparokṣajñānasya prasādasādhanatvamuktaṃ tatkuta ityatastatra gītāsmṛtimāha apriyo hi'; iti । aahaṃ jñānino atyarthaṃ'; atyantaṃ apriyaḥ'; । ahi'; prasiddham । asa ca so apyaparokṣajñānī mama priyaḥ'; ityarthaḥ। kṛṣṇavākyametat ।

"yamevaiṣa vṛṇute tena labhyaḥ"
"ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyo mantavyo nididhyāsitavyaḥ"
prasādasya mokṣasādhanatvaṃ na kovalamarthāt jñāyate, kintu śrutyā cetyāśayena tatra kaṭhaśrutimāha ayaṃ'; iti । atraivakāro bhinnakramaḥ । tathā ca aeṣaḥ'; paramātmā aeṣaḥ'; icchārūpaḥ prasannaḥ san ayaṃ'; adhikāriṇaṃ avṛṇute'; anugṛhṇāti atena'; eva alabhyaḥ'; prāpyaḥ, na tvanyena karmaṇetyarthaḥ । ata eva viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāyām "eṣa paramātmā yaṃ vṛṇute yasya prasīdati tenaiva labhyaḥ । kathaṃ? yatastasya svāṃ tanuṃ vivṛṇute prakāśayati, tataścāsya svāṃ tanuṃ avidyāvṛtasvarūpāṃ vivṛṇute āvirbhāvayati"iti prakṛtānukūlatayā samagravākyārtha uktaḥ । yatpūrvaṃ jijñāsāyāḥ aparokṣajñānasādhanatvamupaskṛtavākyenoktaṃ tatra pramāṇatevana śrutimāha aātmā'; iti । vā ara iti viśliṣṭapāṭhaḥ। avā'; śabdo avadhāraṇe । aare'; iti yājñavalkyakartṛkamaitreyīsambodhanam । tathā ca aare'; maitreyi amṛtatvamiṣyate cettarhi aātmā'; paramātmā tvayā adraṣṭavyo'; darśanena viṣayīkartavya ityarthaḥ । darśanaṃ kena syādityākāṅkṣāyāmāha aśrotavyaḥ'; ityādi । darśanārthaṃ nididhyāsitavyaḥ । tadarthaṃ aśrotavyaḥ'; gurūpadeśamukhena ayamasya vākyasyārtha ityupaniṣadvākyārthagrahaṇarūpaśravaṇena viṣayīkartavyaḥ, tathā amantavyaḥ'; yuktyanusandhānarūpamananena viṣayīkartavyaścetyarthaḥ। anena śravaṇamanananididhyāsanātmakajijñāsāyāḥ
aṅgāṅgirūpāyāḥ jñānasādhanatvamuktaṃ bhavati ।

ityādiśrutismṛtibhyaḥ ।
aśrutismṛtibhyaḥ'; iti । śrutayaśca smṛtiśca tābhya iti vigrahaḥ । asya ayato nārāyaṇa'; itāyādinoktaṃ siddhamityanvayaḥ ।

karmaṇā tvadhamaḥ proktaḥ prasādaḥ śravaṇādibhiḥ ।
nanu atatkarma haritoṣaṃ'; aya imaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ'; ityādeḥ karmādināpi bhagavatprasādasiddheḥ kiṃ jñānena? prasādasya mokṣasādhanatābodhake "tamevaṃ vidvān"yamevaiṣa vṛṇute"ityādāviva "priyo hi"iti vākye anyaniṣedhābhāvādityāśṅkāṃ smṛtyā pariharati akarmaṇā'; iti । kāmyākāmyobhayakarmaṇeti yāvat। tathā ca akarmaṇā'; janyo yaḥ aprasādaḥ'; sa aadhamaḥ'; eva aproktaḥ'; prāmāṇikaiḥ। evaṃ aśravaṇādibhiḥ'; yaḥ prasādo bhavati।

madhyamo jñānasampattyā prasādastūttamo mataḥ ।
sa amadhyamaḥ'; । ajñānasampattyā'; aparokṣajñānaparipākena janyo yaḥ aprasādaḥ'; sa eva auttamo mataḥ'; utkṛṣṭatayā pramita ityarthaḥ । avadhāraṇārthakatuśabdasya dvirgrahaṇaṃ triṣvapyanvayasūcanārtham ।

prasādāttvadhamādviṣṇoḥ svargalokaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।
kimato yadyevamityata āha aprasādāt'; iti । tathāca aadhamāt viṣṇoḥ prasādāt'; kāmyakarmasādhyāt asvargalokaḥ'; bhāvyatayā vṛddhaiḥ aprakīrtitaḥ'; ityarthaḥ । kāmyaphalamātropalakṣakametat "parīkṣya lokān" iti śruteḥ kāmyakarmaṇāṃ vairāgyajananadvārā mokṣe apyupayogo astīti jñātavyam । evaṃ akāmyakarmasādhyāt adhamaprasādāt antaḥkaraṇaśuddhyādidvārā mokṣo bhavatītyapi jñātavyam । na ca adhamaprasādaśūnyānāṃ atidveṣiṇāṃ duryodhanādīnāṃ kathaṃ svargaprāptiriti vācyam, bhāgavatācāryarahitānāṃ tadabhāvoktāvapi tadvatāṃ tatsambhavāt । yathoktaṃ gītātātparye 
ācāryāṇāṃ tu tejasā ।
yānti svargaṃ tataḥ kṣipraṃ tamondhaṃ prāpnuvanti ca ।
tadanye naiva ca svargam ।
iti । svargaloka ityuktyā tatraiva "mokṣaḥ sāṅkalpikaḥ svargaḥ bhūtāditvaṃ phalaṃ kramāt"iti vacanokto yo nityasaṃsāribhī rājasarājasai rājasatāmasaiśca prāpya svargapratinidhitvena kalpito daityendralokaḥ sāṅkalpikaḥ svargaḥ sa iha na vivakṣitaḥ, kintu saptalokāntargato rājasasāttvikaiḥ prāpyaḥ svargaloka eveti sūcitam ।

madhyamājjanalokādiruttamastveva muktidaḥ ।
ajanalokādiḥ'; ityatra tu janatyāgena janākhyalokasyaiva pratipattayarthaṃ lokaśabdaprayoga iti jñeyam । janalokādirityatra tatpuruṣo bahuvrīhiśca vivakṣitaḥ । tuśabdo viśeṣārthaḥ । tathā ca amadhyamāt'; viṣṇoḥ prasādāt janalokasyādirmaharlokaḥ janatapolokādireva vā bhavati na muktiḥ । amuktidastu'; uttamaprasāda eva prakīrtito vṛddhaiḥ, na tvanyāviti yojanā । tathā ca karmādinā bhagavatprasādasiddhāvapi tasyānuttamatvāt jñānasādhyasyaivottamatvāt anuttamena svargādimātrasiddhāvapi mokṣāsiddheḥ tatsādhanaprasādāya jñānamapekṣitamiti bhāvaḥ । na cātra "īyustrīn karmaṇā lokān jñānenaiva taduttarān"iti vākyavirodhaḥ śaṅkyaḥ, tasya maharlokasthākṛtakabhāgaviṣayatvāt, asya ca punarāvartyabhāgaviṣayatvāt, asāmānyadarśanāllokāḥ'; iti pramāṇabalena jñānaśabdasya svabimbaviṣayayogyāparokṣavyatiriktasāmānyāvatārādyaparokṣaviṣayatvāt, tasya ca śravaṇādibhirityatra hyādipadena grahaṇādvā; nyāyāmṛtoktarītyā jñānadvāreti śeṣakaraṇādvā;
evakārasyāyogavyavacchedārthatvādvā na virodhaḥ ।

śravaṇaṃ mananaṃ caiva dhyānaṃ bhaktistathaiva ca ।
nanvastūttamaprasādāya jñānāpekṣā, tathāpi "karmaṇā jñānamātanoti"ityādeḥ karmādināpi jñānaṃ bhavatīti na tadarthaṃ jijñāsā kartavyā "ātmā"iti vākye anyaniṣedhābhāvādityāśaṅkāṃ prakṛtapramāṇaśeṣeṇa pariharati aśravaṇaṃ'; iti । atra evakārasya dvirgrahaṇaṃ sarvatra sambandhajñāpanāya । te ca śravaṇādīnāṃ kāryasādhane anyasāhityanirāsaktāḥ, "naraṃ ca nārāyaṇameva"ityādāviva anabhimatakarmādivyāvartakāśca । dvayordvayossamuccaye aca'; śabdau । atathā'; śabda upamāyām । atathaiva ca'; iti nipātasamudāyo vā । bhaktigrahaṇaṃ prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭāntārthaṃ vā ।

sādhanaṃ jñānasampattau pradhānaṃ nānyadiṣyate ।
tathā ca ajñānasampattau'; aparokṣajñānaprāptau yathā bhaktistathā śravaṇādyeva sādhanaṃ, nānyatkarmādītyarthaḥ । kā gatistarhi "karmaṇā jñānamātanoti"ityādivacanasyetyata āha apradhānaṃ'; iti । śravaṇādi pradhānaṃ sādhanaṃ aanyat'; apradhānamityeva aiṣyate'; abhyupeyate prāmāṇikaiḥ, na tvanyat sādhanameva neti yojanā । apradhānasādhanaviṣayaṃ karmādivacanamiti bhāvaḥ ।

na caitāni vinā kaścit jñānamāpa kutaścana ।
viparītaṃ kiṃ na syādityata āha ana ca'; iti । tathā ca aetāni'; śravaṇādīni avinā kaścit'; api adhikārī akutaścana'; karmādessataḥ ajñānaṃ nāpa'; evametāni śravaṇādīni santicet kutaśca karmādervinā jñānaṃ nāpeti neti yojanā । tathā ca nirapekṣānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śravaṇādyeva jñāne pradhānaṃ sākṣātsādhanaṃ, karmādi tu tadabhāvāt pāramparyeṇa sādhanamiti na vaiparītyamiti bhāvaḥ । anāradīye'; ayata uktaṃ'; iti śeṣaḥ । asya aato "yato nārāyaṇa"ityādinoktaṃ yuktaṃ'; ityupaskṛtavākyenānvayaḥ । ayato nārāyaṇa'; ityanena jijñāsāyāḥ nirviṣayatvaśaṅkānirāsāya prayuktaḥ sautro brahmaśabdo nārāyaṇapara iti vyākhyātaḥ ।

brahmaśabdaśca viṣṇāveva ।
nanu nārāyaṇaprasādamṛte na mokṣaścet tarhi tajjijñāsaiva kartavyā na brahmajijñāsā । na ca vācyaṃ nārāyaṇa eva brahmapadena vivakṣitaḥ sūtrakṛteti, brahmaśabdasya bahvarthatvena sūtrakāravivakṣāviśeṣasya durjñeyatvādityata āha abrahma'; iti । mukhya iti śeṣaḥ । caḥ aanekārtho api brahmaśabdaḥ'; iti apyarthe, yata ityarthe ca । tathā ca brahmaśabdasyānekārthatve api yataḥ saḥ viṣṇāveva mukhyaḥ ato mukhyāmukhyayormukhyasyaiva grāhyatvāt sa eva sūtrakāravivakṣito jñāyata iti yojanā । atra śabdāntaraṃ vihāya viṣṇuśabdaprayogeṇa tacchabdagatānāṃ vargapañcamaṣaṣṭhacaturthānāṃ ṇaṣavānāṃ saṅkhyārekhālekhanena sūtrāṇāṃ catuṣṣaṣṭyuttarapañcaśatasaṅkhyoktā bhavati । yadvā 
deśataḥ kālataścaiva guṇataścāpi pūrtitaḥ ।
viṣṇau brahmeti nāmaitanmukhyatonyatra na kvacit ।
ityaitareyabhāṣyokteḥ deśakālaguṇāparicchedarūpatrividhapūrtivācakabrahmaśabdavyākhyānāya tādṛśaviṣṇuśabdaprayogaḥ। ṭīkāyāṃ tu atra viṣṇugrahaṇena "saviṣṇurāha hi । taṃ brahmetyācakṣate"ityanyonyāvyavahitasūtradvayakaraṇānantarameva brahmamīmāṃsāyāḥ vyāsenārabdhatvādetadavyavahitadevamīmāṃsāntyasūtradvaye brahmatvena nārāyaṇasyaiva prakṛtatvaṃ sūcayatīti prayojanāntaramuktam । tattvapradīpe apyetadeva ayaśca devatāmīmāṃsānte "viṣṇureva hi tat śrutestaṃ brahmetyācakṣate"iti sarvadevottamatvena pratijñāto brahmatvena coktaḥ, sa eva brahmaśabdenottaramīmāṃsāyāṃ vicāryatvenocyate'; iti pāṭhabhedenoktam।

yamantassamudre kavayo avayanti tadakṣare parame prajāḥ ।
brahmaśabdasyānyatrāpi rūḍhatvādrūḍhereva mukhyavṛttitvātkuto asau viṣṇāveva mukhya ityata āha ayaṃ'; iti। abrahmaśabdaśca'; ityādi atrāpi sambadhyate । co yadyapītyādyarthe । hiśabdo yata ityarthe । śrutirāheti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca yadyapi brahmaśabdo anyatra rūḍhaḥ, tathāpi aśrutiḥ'; "yamanta"ityādikā yataḥ kavīnāṃ mate atadeva paramaṃ brahma'; ityāhuriti prayogabāhulyarūpāṃ rūḍhimāha, ato brahmaśabdo viṣṇāveva paramamukhya ityarthaḥ । anyatrājñarūḍheḥ vidvadrūḍheratimukhyatvāditi bhāvaḥ । yamantassamudre iti vākyam 
yadoṣadhībhiḥ puruṣān paśūṃśca viveśa bhūtāni carācarāṇi ।
ataḥ paraṃ nānyadaṇīyasaṃ hi parātparaṃ yanmahato mahāntam ।
yadekamavyaktamanantarūpaṃ viśvaṃ purāṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt ।
iti vākyena saha vyākhyātaṃ viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāyām । tathā hi ayamantassamudre'; vibhakttayarthe avyayībhāvaḥ samudrasyāntassthitaṃ akavayo'; jñāninaḥ aavayanti'; īṣadeva jānanti, yasmin atadakṣare'; avijñeyatvarūpapūrvaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭe prasiddhe vā avināśini aparame'; prajā adhīnāḥ santi ।

yataḥ prasūtā jagataḥ prasūtī toyena jīvānvyasasarja bhūmyām ।
ajagataḥ prasūtī'; prasūtirjanayitrī mūlaprakṛtirlakṣmīḥ ayato'; yasmāt prasūtā utpannā, sṛṣṭau abhimukhībabhūveti vā, yacca yadvastu atoyena'; tattajjīvakarmaṇā svavīryeṇa vā, toyaśabdoktāmbūpalakṣitairbhūtairvā abhūmyāṃ'; pṛthivyādiṣu lokeṣu ajīvān vyasasarja'; vividhaṃ sasarja ।

ityādyuktvā "tadevartaṃ tadu satyamāhustadeva brahma paramaṃ kavīnām"

yacca aoṣadhībhiḥ'; sahitān apuruṣān paśūṃśca carācarāṇi bhūtāni'; preraṇāya aviveśa'; । acarācarāṇi bhūtāni'; ityanenaiva siddhe yajñāṅgatvādinā viśiṣṭānāṃ vrīhyoṣadhīnāṃ grahaṇāya punarvacanam । aataḥ'; yasmāt aparaṃ'; atiśayena aanyat'; vastu aaṇīyasaṃ'; aṇīyo nāsti, yacca aparātparaṃ'; utkṛṣṭādutkṛṣṭaṃ amahato'; mahatparimāṇādapi amahāntaṃ'; mahat, ayadekaṃ'; kevalaṃ aavyaktaṃ'; svaprasādaṃ vinā atīndriyaṃ aviśvaṃ pūrṇaṃ tamasaḥ'; prakṛterajñānādvā aparastāt'; atikramya sthitaṃ atadevartaṃ'; yathārthajñānarūpaṃ atadu'; tadeva asatyaṃ'; jñānapūrvakriyāvat atadeva kavīnāṃ'; mate aparamaṃ'; mukhyaṃ abrahma'; ityāhuriti । atra atadakṣare'; iti śrutipāṭhaḥ । ayadakṣare'; iti kvacitpāṭhe yasminnityadhyāhāro na kāryaḥ । avyasasarja'; iti prāyikaḥ śrutipāṭhaḥ । avyacasarja'; ityapi kvacitpaṭhanti । atra sakārasya cakārādeśaḥ chāndasaḥ । ādyapakṣe api vi ā sasarjetyavayavavibhāgaḥ tatrāṅgo hrasvatvaṃ chāndasaṃ bahulagrahaṇāt । "indrā varuṇa vāmaham"iti śrutau ṇakārātparasyākārasya yathā hrasvatvaṃ tadvaditi nārāyaṇapaṇḍitācāryoktiḥ। "vyasasarja visasarja bahulagrahaṇāt" iti prameyadīpoktirapi hrasvābhiprāyikaiva । kecittu liṭyaḍāgamaḥ chāndaso bahulagrahaṇāditi prameyadīpārthamāhuḥ । tadāryoktātpakṣāntaram । padmanābhatīrthakṛtatattvanirṇayaṭīkāyāṃ nyāyaratnāvalyāṃ tu avayanti'; iti vicchidya atadakṣare'; ityeva ca paṭhitvā, "yaṃ puruṣaṃ samudre antaḥ kavayo vayanti vāñchanti tadakṣare yasmin tasmin akṣare nāśavarjite parame prajāstadādhārāḥ tiṣṭhanti, jagataḥ prasūtī jagajjanayitrī prakṛtiḥ yataḥ prasūtā prādurbhūtā satī toyena itaramiśritena jīvān dehavattvena vyasasarja visṛṣṭavatī"ityekānvayena "tadeva tātparyaviṣayībhūtatvādṛtaṃ tadevābādhitarūpatvātsatyaṃ tadeva kavīnāmabhimataṃ paraṃ brahma"ityartha uktaḥ । nārāyaṇapaṇḍitāryakṛtau tattvamañjaryāmapi atadakṣare'; iti paṭhitvā "yamavayanti avagacchanti yasmiṃstasmin akṣare prajāḥ santi yataḥ prasūtā parādhīnaviśeṣaṃ prāptā śrīḥ toyena karmaṇā jīvān bhūmyāṃ prakṛtyāṃ vyasasarja"ityanvayena "tadevartaṃ śaśvadekaprakāraṃ satyaṃ sādhu guṇapūrṇaṃ"ityartha uktaḥ ।

iti hi śrutiḥ ।
"tanno viṣṇuḥ"
iti vacanāt viṣṇureva hi tatrocyate ।
nanu atadeva'; iti vākye tacchabdena kuto viṣṇuniścayaḥ? samudrasthatvaliṅgāditi cet na, tasya rudrādāvapi kathañcitsambhavādityato niravakāśaviṣṇuśruterevetyāha atannaḥ'; iti । aiti vacanādviṣṇureva'; atatra'; "tadeva"iti śrutau tacchabdena aucyate'; iti niśicīyata ityarthaḥ । hiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । atra atannaḥ'; ityekadeśagrahaṇena "nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi, tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt"iti samagravākyaṃ gṛhyate । dvitīyārthe caturthyau । tathā ca yasmāt vayaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ avidmahe'; jānīmahe yataśca taṃ vāsudevaṃ adhīmahi'; dhyāyemahi atat'; tasmāt anaḥ'; asmān atat'; śubhaṃ prati aviṣṇuḥ pracodayāt'; prerayatviti śrutyarthaḥ ।

na cetaraśabdāttatprāptiḥ ।
yadyuttaravākye viṣṇuśabdaśravaṇādviṣṇurevātroktaṃ brahma, tarhi atanno rudraḥ'; ityādītaraśabdaśravaṇāt rudrāderapi mukhyabrahmatā prāptetyata āha ana ca'; iti । caśabdaḥ samuccaye । tathā ca aitaraśabdāt'; rudrādivācakaśabdabalāttasya rudrāderapi tasya mukhyabrahmatvasya aprāptirna'; ityarthaḥ ।

nāmani viśvābhi na santi loke yadāvirāsīdanṛtasya sarvam ।
kuta ityatastatprāpakaśabdānāṃ viṣṇāveva mukhyatvāditi hetūpaskārabhipretya tasyāsiddhiparihārāya viṣṇormukhyataḥ sarvanāmavācyatve śrutimāha anāmāni'; iti । aśruteḥ'; iti kvacitpañcamyantapāṭhaḥ । prathamāntapāṭhe yato ata iti śeṣaḥ । asya ana ca'; ityanenānvayaḥ । ayat'; yasmāt aanṛtasya'; ṛtabhinnasya viṣṇvitarasya lokasya jagataḥ asarvaṃ'; nāmapravṛttinimittaṃ aāvirāsīt'; abhūt tasmādutpattimatpravṛttinimittavattvāt aviśvā'; viśvāni sarvāṇi anāmāni'; aloke'; rudrādijagati aabhi'; mukhyataḥ vācakatayā ana santi'; ityarthaḥ ।

nāmāni sarvāṇi yamāviśanti taṃ vai viṣṇuṃ paramamudāharanti ।
tarhi kasmin tāni mukhyānītyata āha anāmāni'; iti । vaiśabdo avadhāraṇe । paramamiti hetugarbhaviśeṣaṇam ।
tathā ca asarvāṇi nāmāni'; ayaṃ'; aā'; mukhyato vācakatvena aviśanti'; ataṃ paramaṃ'; deśakālābhyāmaparicchinnapravṛttinimittaṃ aviṣṇuṃ vai'; vadanti vidvāṃsa ityarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu aviśvā'; viśvāni anāmāni loke'; abhito ana santi'; mukhyato na santi mukhyato na lokavācakāni ayat'; yasmāt, yataḥ puruṣāt aanṛtasya'; viṣṇvanyasya jagato janmalayādikaṃ sarvaṃ aāvirāsīt', yaṃ ca vācakatvena anāmāni ā'; samantāt aviśanti', ataṃ'; ha aviṣṇuṃ'; uttamaṃ vadantītyartha uktaḥ । etatpakṣe yacchabdasyāvṛttiḥ । dvitīyādipādatrayasya hetusamarpakatvam । pakṣadvaye api viṣṇuśabdo bhinnakramaḥ ।

iti bhāllaveyaśrutiḥ ।
"yo devānāṃ nāmadhā eva eva taṃ sampraśnaṃ bhuvanā yantyanyā"
ityevaśabdānnānyeṣāṃ sarvanāmatā ।
nanu yathā viṣṇoḥ śrutyantarasiddhasarvanāmatvenātroktaṃ brahmatvaṃ siddhyati tathā rudrādīnāmapi viṣṇvādiśabdavācyatvena atroktaṃ brahmatvaṃ kiṃ na syādityata āha ayaḥ'; iti । aityevaśabdāt'; iti itivākyasyaivaśabdāt aanyeṣāṃ'; rudrādīnāṃ asarvanāmatā'; viṣṇvādisarvaśabdavācyatvaṃ netyarthaḥ । sarvanāmatetyanantaraṃ yata evamataḥ atanno viṣṇuḥ'; ityādau nānyeṣāṃ prāptiḥ ata eva na brahmatvaṃ teṣāmiti vākyaśeṣaḥ । ayo'; bhagavān aeka eva devānāṃ'; brahmādīnāṃ anāmadhāḥ'; viśvapāśabdavadayaṃ śabdaḥ nāmadhārakaḥ na tvanye api ataṃ praśnaṃ'; praṣṭāraṃ aanyā'; anyāni abhuvanā'; bhuvanāni lokāḥ asaṃyanti'; saṃyānti mokṣe pralaye ceti śrutyarthaḥ ।

"ajasya nābhāvadhyekamarpitaṃ yasmin viśvāni bhuvanāni tasthuḥ"।
iti hi viṣṇorliṅgam ।
nanvatrāpi yacchabdena viṣṇuriti kutaḥ? viśvakarmeti śrutibalādasya sūktākhyaprakaraṇasya viśvakarmādyanyaparatayā tadgatayacchabdasyāpi tatparatvaucityādityata āha aajasya'; iti । ahi'; yasmāt iti vākye aviṣṇoḥ liṅgaṃ'; padmanābhatvākhyamasādhāraṇo dharmaḥ śrutaḥ tasmādyacchabdodito viṣṇurevetyanvayaḥ ।
utsargato liṅgāt śruteḥ prābalye api sāvakāśāyā viśvakarmaśruteḥ niravakāśaliṅgena bādhopapatteriti bhāvaḥ । śrutyarthastu aajasya'; ajanyasya puruṣasya anābhau ekaṃ'; vastu aarpitaṃ'; udbhūtam । ayasmin viśvāni bhuvanāni'; sarve caturdaśalokāḥ aadhitasthuḥ'; adhiṣṭhitāḥ iti ।

na ca prasiddhārthaṃ vinānyortho yujyate ।
nābhyarpitaṃ padmādanyatkiṃ na syādityata āha ana ca'; iti । prasiddhaṃ viṣṇunābhisthatvena prasiddhaṃ padmākhyārthaṃ avinānyo artho'; na yujyate, prasiddhibādhādityarthaḥ । viśvakarmaśrutivatpadmanābhatvaliṅgamapyanyasya kiṃ na syādityato vādmaha ana ca'; iti । padmanābhatvena prasiddhapadārthaṃ bhagavantaṃ vinā aanyaḥ'; padmanābho na yujyate prasiddhibādhādityarthaḥ ।

ajasya nābhāviti yasya nābherabhūt śruteḥ puṣkaraṃ lokasāram ।
na kevalaṃ prasiddhibalādevaitacchrutyuktaṃ padmaṃ padmanābhaśca harirityavasīyate, kintu aajasya'; iti śrutestadubhayabodhakatvena smṛtyanugṛhītatvāccetyāha aajasya'; iti । iti śruterityanvayaḥ । tathā ca aajasya nābhāviti śruteḥ'; sakāśāt alokasāraṃ'; lokādhārabhūtaṃ apuṣkaraṃ'; padmaṃ aabhūt'; iti jñāyate ।

tasmai namo vyastasamastaviśvavibhūtaye viṣṇave lokakartre ।
atasmai vyastasamastaviśvavibhūtaye'; viśvasya jagato vibhūtayaḥ sṛṣṭyādyaṣṭakaṃ jīvādau vyastāḥ vistṛtāḥ jaḍādau samastāḥ saṃkṣiptāḥ viśvavibhūtayo yenāsau vyastasamastaviśvavibhūtistasmai alokakartre'; lokasvāmine aviṣṇave namaḥ'; ityarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu samastaviśvavibhūtayo yena vyastā sa vyastasamastaviśvavibhūtiḥ । atha vā vyastāḥ samastā viśvavibhūtayo yeneti dvedhā vyākhyātam । tatra divitīyaṃ ṭīkāyāṃ vivṛtam । pūrvārdhe viṣṇuvācakaśabdābhāvāduttarārdhodāharaṇam । aiti ca skānde'; iti caśabdo bhinnakrameṇa auktaṃ'; ityadhyāhṛtapadena sambadhyate । yata evamataḥ aajasya'; ityuktaṃ padmameva, padmanābhaśca harireveti vākyaśeṣaḥ । na kevalaṃ prasiddhibādhāditi cārthaḥ ।

"paro divā para enā pṛthivyā"
iti samākhyāśrutau ।
yadā niravakāśaliṅgamātraṃ śrutibādhakaṃ tadā kimu vācyaṃ samākhyāyuktaṃ taditi bhāvenāha apara'; iti। idaṃ cāvartate, aviṣṇureva'; ityādikamatrāpi sambadhyate । tathā ca yataḥ viśvakarmasūkte "paro divā para enā pṛthivyā paro devebhirasurairyadasti"iti yā ākhyā uktiḥ tasyāḥ samā samānā aparo divā'; ityevaṃrūpa aśrutau'; āmbhṛṇīsūkte asti ato api aviṣṇureva'; viśvakarmasūktodita ityarthaḥ ।

"yaṃ kāmaye taṃ tamugraṃ kṛṇomi taṃ brahmāṇaṃ tamṛṣiṃ taṃ sumedhām"
ityuktvā ।
nanu samākhyāśrutāvapi viṣṇuḥ kuto vācya ityata āha ayaṃ'; iti । itītyanantaraṃ vākyenetyubhayatra śeṣaḥ । aparo divā'; ityetatsamastamanenāpi yojyam । atra samākhyāśrutāvityekaṃ padam। tathā ca yasmāt aparo divā'; iti samākhyāśrutau metyākhyā mākhyā tayā sahitā samākhyā "prakṛtirvāva samāsamā" iti śrutau samāsamatvokteḥ anāmaikadeśe'; iti nyāyena samābhidhāvā, ahamiti prakṛtā lakṣmīḥ "yaṃ"ityādivākyena brahmādīnāṃ svādhīnatvamuktvā "mama yonirapsvantaḥ samudre" iti vākyena "paro divā"ityuktaṃ viṣṇuṃ svakāraṇatvena samudrasthatvena cāha, tasmādviṣṇureva samākhyāśrutipratipādya ityarthaḥ। uktvetyanena lakṣmīkāraṇaṃ brahmādyanyatamaṃ kiṃ na syāditi śaṅkā vāritā । śrutau adivā'; ityādi tṛtīyā pañcamyarthe । tathā ca adivaḥ'; aśriyaḥ'; aparaḥ'; aenā'; etasyāḥ bhūmyāśca aparaḥ'; uttamaḥ । adevebhiḥ'; adevebhyaḥ'; aasuraiḥ'; asurebhyaśca aparaḥ'; uttamaḥ । kiṃ bahunā ayadasti'; tasmātsarvasmādapi paraḥ । sa viṣṇuḥ dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ paraḥ । ahaṃ tu amahinā'; mahimnā aetāvatī'; parimitā babhūva । ahametāvatī yathoktaprakārā mahimnā nāto adhiketi vā śrutyarthaḥ । ahamiti labdhapadena lakṣmīrucyate, etatsūktapravartikāyāḥ āmbhṛṇyāḥ lakṣmīrūpatvāt । tathā ca ahaṃ ayaṃ yaṃ'; rudrapadayogyaṃ jīvaṃ augraṃ'; rudraṃ kartuṃ akāmaye'; iccheyaṃ ataṃ taṃ'; ugraṃ kṛṇomi karomi । evaṃ tattatpadayogyaṃ yaṃ yaṃ abrahmāṇaṃ'; aṛṣiṃ'; asumedhāṃ'; sumedhasaṃ vā kartuṃ kāmaye taṃ taṃ tathā karomītyarthaḥ । śiṣṭavākyārthaḥ "patyurasāmañjasyāt" ityadhikaraṇe vakṣyate ।

"mama yonirapsvantaḥ samudre"
ityāha ।
tathāpi mama na svatantryamityaha amama'; iti । amama'; ayoniḥ'; kāraṇaṃ asamudre apsu'; apām aantaḥ'; tiṣṭhati । tasyādhikyaṃ kampasvarārthaḥ । patināma na grāhyamiti bhāvena nārāyaṇa ityanuktvā tadarthabodhanāyaivamuktiḥ ।

ugro rudraḥ, samudre antarnārāyaṇaḥ ।
prasiddhatvāt sūcitatvāccāsyārthasya ।
nanvatra samudrastho rudraḥ kiṃ na syāt atapyamānāya salile'; iti bhāratokteḥ na ca ramādhīnatoktivirodhaḥ, ugraśabdena kasyacitkrūrasya grahaṇasambhavādityata āha augra'; iti । bhavedityubhayatra śeṣaḥ । tathā ca atrogra ityukto rudra eva bhavet, tathā samudre antassthito nārāyaṇa eva bhavet, iti pratijñāvākyadvayārthaḥ । tatra hetumāha aprasiddhatvāt'; iti । aasyārthasya'; rudre ugraśabdavācyatvarūpārthasya prasiddhatvāt, "ugraḥ kapardī"ityādikośaprasiddhatvāt, ugraśabdena rudraśabdārthasya krauryasya jñāpitatvāccetyarthaḥ । rudro raudra ugra ityeteṣāmekārthatvāditi bhāvaḥ । evaṃ samudraśāyitvarūpārthasya "mahodadhiśayo antakaḥ"ityādiviṣṇusahasranāmaprasiddhatvāt samudre antaḥsthatvakathanena "āpo nārāḥ"iti smṛtisiddhanāraśabdoditodakāśrayatvarūpanārāyaṇaśabdārthasya asūcitatvācca'; ityarthaḥ ।

na cāvirodhe prasiddhaḥ parityajate ।
