uktanyāyena ca śrutaya etameva vadanti ।
nanu prasiddhyādisadbhāve api tatparityāgenānyasvīkāre kiṃ bādhakamityata āha ana ca'; iti। arthasyetyetadvipariṇāmenātra sambadhyate । tathā ca co yato ayamarthaḥ aprasiddhaḥ'; ato aavirodhe'; pramāṇavirodhābhāve ana parityajyate'; na tyajyata ityarthaḥ, prasiddhārthasya virodhaikāpodyatvāt, anyathā prasiddhibādhāditi bhāvaḥ । "ākāśādeva samutpadyante" "janitota viṣṇoḥ" "nakirindratvaduttaraḥ" ityādau vyabhicāravāraṇāyāvirodha iti । nanu virodhābhāvo asiddhaḥ, yato atra yadi rudro lakṣmyadhīnatayograpadenocyate tarhi "viśvādhiko rudraḥ"ityādiśrutivirodhaḥ syāt ato atra tatparityāgo yukta ityata āha aukta'; iti । karaṇavyutpattyā nyāyaḥ pramāṇam । tathā ca yato "nāmāni viśvā" ityādyuktāgamena, taduktotpattimatpravṛttinimittavattvādyanumānena, caśabdasamuccitaiḥ "vede rāmāyaṇe caiva"iti vakṣyamāṇapramāṇaiśca sādhakaiḥ aśrutayo'; "viśvādhiko rudraḥ" ityādyāgamāḥ radrādipadānāṃ viṣṇuvācitvamāśritya vā, viśvo vāyuḥ adhiko yasmādviśvādhika ityarthāśrayaṇena vā aetameva'; viṣṇumeva avadanti'; tātparyataḥ prādhānyena bodhayanti ityavagamyate । ato na "viśvādhikaḥ"ityādiśrutivirodha iti yojanā ।

vede rāmāyaṇe caiva purāṇe bhārate tathā ।
śrutīnāṃ viṣṇvekavācitve smṛtiṃ cāha avede'; iti । viṣṇureva avede rāmāyaṇe ca purāṇe tathā bhārate'; ।

ādāvante ca madhye ca viṣṇussarvatra gīyate ।
kiṃ bahunā asarvatra'; sarvagrantheṣu agīyate'; pratipādyate । teṣvapi na bhāge, kintvādau madhye ante ca, karmādikāṇḍatraye api, upakramopasaṃhārayoravāntaraprakaraṇeṣu ca, sarvatra prativākyaṃ pratipadaṃ pratyakṣaraṃ ca mukhyataḥ pratipādyata ityarthaḥ ।

iti harivaṃśeṣu । na cetaragranthavirodhaḥ,
aveda'; iti vacanasya khilākhilapārijātākhyaharivaṃśabhāgatrayagatatvasūcanāya aharivaṃśeṣu'; iti bahuvacanam । harivaṃśeṣvityanantaraṃ ayaduktaṃ'; iti śeṣaḥ, tasyāto na virodha iti, harivaṃśeṣūktanyāyena uktarītyā iti vānvayaḥ । nanu pramāṇavirodhābhāvo asiddhaḥ, yataḥ śrutivirodhābhāve apyasti pāśupatādiśāstravirodhaḥ, tatra rudrādīnāṃ sarvottamatvasya sarvakāraṇatvasya cokteḥ ityata āha ana ca'; iti। co apyarthaḥ na kevalaṃ śrutivirodhābhāvaḥ, apitarhītaravirodho api neti । aasyārthasya'; iti vartate ।

eṣa mohaṃ sṛjāmyāśu yo janānmohayiṣyati ।
kuta ityata teṣāṃ mohārthaṃ kṛtatvāditi hetvadhyāhāramabhipretya tasyāsiddhiṃ pramāṇodāharaṇena nirāha aeṣa'; iti । rudraṃ prati viṣṇuvākyametat । muhyate anena jana iti amoho'; naṭanaṃ vañcanaṃ vā । amoho'; mohakāraṇamanādikarmavāsanārupamiti tattvapradīptokterapyayamevārthaḥ, mohakaśāstramiti vyāsatīrthīyokteḥ । na ca asya ana mohaśāstrasya vaktā viṣṇurāśaṅkyaḥ, "ajasyāvakracetasaḥ" iti hi śrutiḥ'; iti tattvapradīpavirodhaḥ śaṅkyaḥ asatāmityabhiprāyāt ।
vidyamānākārācchādanenāvidyamānākārapradarśanaṃ naṭanam । avidyamānakathanaṃ vañcanam । sṛjāmītyuttamapuruṣaprayogādahamiti kartā labhyate । caśabdaḥ kriyākartṛsamuccaye । apūrvaśrutasyaitacchabdasya paścāt śruto yacchabdo viśeṣaṇam'; iti nyāyadīpokteḥ ya eṣa iti yojanā । tathā ca ahaṃ amohaṃ sṛjāmi'; karomi । aya eṣa'; mohaḥ ajanān mohayiṣyati'; ajñānamithyājñānādikaṃ prāpayiṣyati ।

tvaṃ ca rudra mahābāho mohaśāstrāṇi kāraya ।
parabādhakatvāt bāhuḥ prāṇyaṅgaṃ, mahān bāhuryasya saḥ, tasya sambuddhiḥ he amahābāho'; śatrubādhakāṅgayukta arudra'; atvaṃ ca'; mohaṃ sṛja amohaśāstrāṇi'; ca akāraya'; kuru, dadhīcyādibhiśca kāraya। he amahābhuja'; mahābhakṣaka mahākuṭileti vā he rudra ।

atathyāni vitathyāni darśayasva mahābhuja ।
teṣviti śeṣaḥ tathā ca ateṣu'; mohaśāstreṣu aatathyāni'; kvāpyavidyamānāni liṅgamūlānveṣaṇādīni avitathyāni'; vyadhikaraṇatvena vidyamānāni viṣṇuniṣṭhāni vāyuniṣṭhāni vā rudrādiniṣṭhatayocyamānāni sarvottamatvasarvasvātantryaviṣabhakṣaṇādīni adarśayasva'; pratipādayeti yāvat ।

prakāśaṃ kuru cātmānamaprakāśaṃ ca māṃ kuru ।
amām ātmānam'; ityuddeśyadvitīyāntam । parasparasamuccaye caśabdau । tathā ca lokeṣu aātmānaṃ'; svātmānamuddiśya aprakāśaṃ'; prasiddhiṃ akuru'; । na kevalametāvat, kintu amām'; uddiśya aaprakāśam'; aprasiddhiṃ ca kurvītyarthaḥ । kecittu prakāśo asyāstīti prakāśamiti arśaādyajantatvamāśritya uddeśyadvitīyānāśrayaṇena prakāśaṃ prasiddhamiti vyācakṣate ।

iti vārāhavacanāt । śaive ca skānde 
avārāhavacanāt'; ityasyetareṣāṃ mohārthaṃ kṛtatvāvagamāditi hetumukhena ana cetara'; iti pratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । liṅgamūlānveṣaṇakathā tu pūrvaṃ jagatkartṛtvaviṣaye viṣṇuviriñcayorvivādo abhūt ahameva jagataḥ kartā na matto anyaḥ iti । etasminnantare tayorgarvavināśāya tanmadhye kiñcana liṅgamudabhūt । tau tat dṛṣṭvā sarvadevasannidhau parasparaṃ samayaṃ cakratuḥ । tatra brahmā viṣṇumāha avayormadhye asya liṅgasya yo antamādiṃ ca gacchati sa bhavedadhiko loke, lokakartā ca sa prabhuḥ । tasmāddhe viṣṇo tvaṃ liṅgasya mūlagaveṣaṇāyādhastādvraja, ahamantagaveṣaṇāya ūrdhvaṃ gamiṣyāmi iti । evaṃ tau samayaṃ kṛtvā mārgamāṇau nirgatau । tatra viṣṇurvarāharūpeṇādhastādgaveṣituṃ yayau । vāṇījānistu haṃsarūpeṇordhvaṃ yayo । atha punarviṣṇuḥ svasthānaṃ samāgatya sarvadevasannidhau ahaṃ liṅgasyādimadrākṣamiti satyam āha । brahmāpi samāgatya ahamantamadrākṣamiti chadmanā mṛṣā āha । atha liṅgarūpī maheśvaraḥ tayorvacaḥ śrutvā he viṣṇo yatastvaṃ satyamevāvocaḥ ataḥ tava loke matsamā pūjā bhaviṣyati । brahmaṇastu netyuvāca । tato brahmā he rudra mamānṛtoktikṛtāparādhastvayā kṣantavya ityāha । tato rudro na mama vaco mithyā bhaviṣyati । tathāpi tvaṃ mithyoktikṛtadoṣaparihārārthaṃ gandhamādanagiriṃ vraja । tatra kratūn kuruṣva। tatastava śrautasmārtakarmasveva pūjā bhaviṣyati । na tu devālayādiṣvityuktvāntaradhīyatetyādirūpā skāndapurāṇasthā। nanu tathāpyasyārthasya skāndabrahmavaivartādipurāṇavirodhassyāt, teṣāṃ śivabrahmādipāramyaviṣayatvādityata āha aśaive ca'; iti । caśabdo apyarthassamuccaye, yadyapītyādyarthe ca aśaive'; śivotkarṣapare apīti askānde'; vacanādityanuṣaṅgadyotakaśca ।

śvapacādapi kaṣṭatvaṃ brahmeśānādayassurāḥ ।
tadaivācyuta yāntyeva yadaiva tvaṃ parāṅmukhaḥ ।

he aacyuta'; ayadaiva'; yadi ca tvameva sarvathā aparāṅmukho'; bhavasi anugrahaṃ ca karoṣi atadā'; tarhi abrahmeśānādayaḥ surāḥ'; śvapacādapi śvānaṃ pacatīti śvapaco nīcaḥ tasmādapi akaṣṭatvaṃ'; kleśayuktatvaṃ kaṣṭaṃ vā ayāntyeva'; ityarthaḥ । asya tarkatvāttasya viparyayaparyavasāne brahmādīnāṃ viṣṇvadhīnatvam atyantatadanugrahapātratvaṃ ca siddhyatīti na pramāṇavirodhaḥ । itiśabdasya aiti skānde'; ityanvayaḥ ।

brāhme ca brahmavaivarte 
nāhaṃ na ca śivo anye ca tacchaktyekāṃśabhāginaḥ ।
bālaḥ krīḍanakairyadvat krīḍate asmābhiracyutaḥ ।

abrāhme'; brahmaviṣaye । atra aaham'; iti caturmukha ucyate । ayadvat'; iti śravaṇāt atadvat'; iti labhyate । caśabdau samuccayārthau । aasmābhiḥ'; ityatra śivaścānye ca ahaṃ ca vayaṃ tairityekaśeṣaḥ । tathā ca yadyapi vayaṃ atacchaktyekāṃśabhāginaḥ'; tasyācyutasya yā śaktiḥ sāmarthyaṃ tasyaikāṃśabhāgino na bhavāmaḥ tathāpi ayadvat'; yathā abālaḥ krīḍanakaiḥ'; krīḍāsādhanapadārthaiḥ akrīḍate'; atadvat'; tathā aacyuto'; harirapi aasmābhiḥ'; karaṇaiḥ akrīḍate'; sṛṣṭyādikrīḍāṃ karotītyarthaḥ । punarna cetyuktiḥ tātparyārthā, anā'; puruṣa iti vā । itiśabdasya iti brahmavaivarte ityanvayaḥ । askānde'; abrahmavaivarte'; ityanayoḥ avacanāt'; itipadadvārā ana cetaragranthavirodhaḥ'; ityanenānvayaḥ । tathā ca teṣāṃ śaivāditve api na virodhitvam, tatrāpi viṣṇūttamatvāderapyuktyā svavirodhena śivādyutkarṣe aprāmāṇyāt । na ca viparītaṃ kiṃ na syāditi vācyam, śivādyutkarṣādeḥ śaivādipurāṇeṣvevāsādhāraṇyena prāptatvāt, tatraiva viṣṇūtkarṣoktau tatra prāmāṇyasya śivādyutkarṣādāvaprāmāṇyasya ca niścayena vaiparītyāyogāt । tasmātpāśupatādiparikalpitaśivādyuttamatvaparipāṭī darśanabhāṣayā teṣūpanyasyata iti na tadvirodha iti bhāvaḥ ।

na ca vaiṣṇaveṣu tathā । tacca "eṣa"mohaṃ ityuktam ।।
। iti jijñāsādhikaraṇam ।
tathāpi viṣṇūttamatvarūdrādhamatvayorvaiṣṇavagranthavirodho astītyata āha ana ca'; iti । samuccaye caśabdaḥ । tathā ca avaiṣṇaveṣu'; viṣṇuviṣayapurāṇādiṣvapi atathā'; viṣṇoranyasyottamatvamuktaṃ na, ata eva atathā'; śaivavat sarvottamatvādhamatvaviṣaye virodho netyarthaḥ, yena svavirodhena svaviṣaye aprāmāṇyaṃ syāditi bhāvaḥ । tarhi vaiṣṇaveṣu rāmakṛṣṇādiviṣṇukartṛkaśivastutyādi kathamucyata ityata āha atacca'; iti । castavarthaḥ । vacanādityanuvtate । tadityasyāvṛttiḥ । tathā ca co yato vaiṣṇaveṣu yacchivastutyādyucyate tattu aeṣa moham'; iti vacanājjñātena tena mohārthatvena auktaṃ'; pratyuktaṃ samāhitaṃ
ityuktamityarthaḥ । asya aato na tadvirodhaḥ'; ityadhyāhṛtenānvayaḥ ।
। iti jijñāsādhikaraṇam ।

।
brahmaṇo lakṣaṇamāha 
janmādyasya yataḥ ।
sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhāraniyamanajñānājñānabandhamokṣā yataḥ ।
etadadhikaraṇapratipādyaṃ darśayati abrahmaṇaḥ'; iti । nirbādharūḍhibalāt jīva evedaṃ brahma, tasya cāsandhigdhatvānna jijñāsyatvamiti prāptetannirākartuṃ brahmaśabdena jīvagrahaṇe bādhakarūpaṃ śrutyuktaṃ jijñāsyabrahmaṇo lakṣaṇamāha sūtrakāra ityarthaḥ । "śrutyuktaṃ lakṣaṇamāha"iti ṭīkayā "sā viṣṇorbrahmatvavidhātrī taittirīyaśrutiryāni tasya lakṣaṇānyāha tānyanena sūtreṇa bhagavānāha"iti tattvapradīpokteḥ tacchabdādhyāhāreṇa bhāṣyārtha uktaḥ । ata eva lakṣaṇamiti samudāyaikavacanamiti jñātavyam। anena pūrvatra vivakṣitabrahmajijñāsākṣepeṇeha pūrvapakṣotthānāt pūrvādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । brahmaviṣayatvācchāstrasaṅgatiḥ siddhaiva । yadyapi abrahmaśabdaśca viṣṇāveva'; ityanena brahmaśabdo viṣṇāveva mukhya ityuktam । tathāpi bhāṣyakārairuktatve api sūtrakṛtānuktatvāt brahma kiṃ jīva uta viṣṇuriti bhavatyeva sandehaḥ । sūtraṃ paṭhati ajanma'; iti । yata ityuktestadbrahmeti prakṛtaṃ bhavatīti śeṣaḥ। yadvā "janmādyasya yata iti sūtre śrutamiti vākyaśeṣaḥ"। iti sudhokteḥ śrutamiti vākyaśeṣaḥ । janma ādiryasya sṛṣṭyādisamudāyasya tajjanmādīti tadguṇasaṃvijñānabahuvrīhiḥ, tasya samāsārthaikadeśasya janmano guṇatvena viśeṣaṇatvena saṃvijñānāt । tathā ca aasya'; pramitasya jagato ajanmādi yato'; bhavati śrutamiti vā tadbrahmeti sūtrārtha ityabhipretya asya jagato janma ādipadokte sthitisaṃhṛtī yatastadbrahmetyādyanyathāpratītivāraṇāya sūtraṃ yathāvadvyācaṣṭe asṛṣṭi'; iti । atra prayojakavyāpāravācisṛṣṭisaṃhāraniyamanaśabdairlakṣaṇayā prapañcaniṣṭhajanmanāśaniyamyatvarūpaprayojyavyāpārāḥ pratipādyante । lakṣaṇāprayojanaṃ brahmaṇa upādānatvābhāvapradarśanamiti candrikoktiḥ । sṛṣṭyādīnāmaṣṭānāṃ ca pratyekaṃ lakṣaṇatvaṃ, na tu samuditaveṣeṇa, ativyāptyādyabhāvāt । etacca lakṣaṇamanantaguṇapūrṇatvasyāpyupalakṣakam । ekenopalakṣaṇasambhave api mumukṣujñeyatvātsārthakamaṣṭānāṃ vacanam । yathoktaṃ śrīmanmahābhāratatātparyanirṇaye 
sṛṣṭirakṣāhṛtijñānaniyatyajñānabandhanān ।
mokṣaṃ ca viṣṇutaścaiva jñātvā muktirna cānyathā ।
iti । yata ityanantaraṃ aśrutāḥ'; abhavanti'; iti vā śeṣaḥ । asya tadbrahmetyupaskṛtenānvayaḥ ।

utpattisthitisaṃhārā niyatirjñānamāvṛtiḥ ।
bandhamokṣau ca puruṣādyasmātsa harirekarāṭ ।
iti skānde ।
nanu jagajjanmādikartṛtvaṃ yadi viṣṇvekaniṣṭhaṃ bhavettadā brahmaśabdena jīvagrahaṇe bādhakarūpaṃ syāt; tasya viṣṇvekaniṣṭhatvameva kuto jñāyata ityata āha autpatti'; iti । asya jagato ayasmāt'; puruṣāt autpattisthitisaṃhārāḥ'; bhavanti aniyatiḥ'; niyamanam aāvṛtiḥ jñānaṃ'; ca yasmādbhavati abandhamokṣau ca'; yasmādbhavataḥ asaḥ ekarāṭ'; svatantro ahariḥ'; eva ityarthaḥ । viriñcādiṣu ativyāptiparihārārtham aekarāṭ'; iti। aiti skānde'; ityanantaraṃ avacanāt sṛṣṭyādikartā harireva'; iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

"yato vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante । yena jātāni jīvanti ।
yatprayantyabhisaṃviśanti । tadvijijñāsasva tadbrahmeti"।।
jijñāsyaṃ brahma viṣṇureva bhavet janmādikartṛtvāt ityanumāne hetvasiddhiṃ jijñāsyabrahmalakṣaṇasya tatrānupalambhakṛtāsambhavaṃ vā nirākartuṃ jagatkāraṇatvalakṣaṇaṃ jijñāsye brahmaṇi "tadvijijñāsasva"ityataḥ pūrvavākye kathitamityāha ayataḥ'; iti । vaiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । bhūtaśabdaḥ "astitvādbhūtanāmabhyaḥ sarvajīvebhya eva yat"iti gītātātparyanirṇayavacanājjīvavācī tadupalakṣitasarvajagatparaḥ । tathā ca aimāni bhūtāni yato jāyante yena jātāni'; utpannāni ajīvanti'; prāṇaṃ dadhati ayat'; ca pralaye aprayanti'; praviśanti yacca aabhi'; svecchayā samyak aviśanti'; muktau atat'; tadeva abrahma'; nānyat । mukhyataḥ tajjñānāya vedārthabhūtaṃ atadvijijñāsasva'; tadviṣayakavicāraṃ kurvityarthaḥ । itiśabdaḥ śrutistha eva । tasya aiti varuṇo bhṛgumuvāca'; iti kriyāpadenānvayaḥ ।

ya u tridhātu pṛthivīmuta dyāṃ eko dādhāra bhuvanāni viśvā ।
caturbhissākaṃ navatiṃ ca nāmabhiḥ cakraṃ na vṛttaṃ vyatīṃravīvipat ।
lakṣaṇasyātivyāptiśaṅkāṃ uktānumānasya vyabhicāraśaṅkāṃ vā parihartuṃ spaṣṭārthatvātprathamaṃ smṛtimupanyasya idānīṃ sṛṣṭyādikartṛtvaṃ pratyekamapi viṣṇvekaniṣṭhaṃ kimu sarvamiti bhāvena sthitikartṛtvasya viṣṇvekaniṣṭhatve śrutimāha ayaḥ'; iti । uśabda evārthaḥ, tridhātvityekaṃ padaṃ, utaśabdassamuccaye । tathā ca ayo'; viṣṇuḥ aekaḥ'; eva atridhātu'; prakṛtipuruṣakāladhārakaḥ apṛthivīṃ'; bhūmiṃ adyāṃ'; śriyaṃ ca aviśvā'; viśvāni sarvāṇi ca abhuvanāni'; adādhāra'; dadhāretyarthaḥ । niyamanasyāpi viṣṇvekakartṛtve śrutimāha acaturbhiḥ'; iti । sa iti śeṣaḥ, naśabda ivārthaḥ, caśabdo mātrārthaḥ । tathā ca sa bṛhaccharīro mūlarūpī viṣṇuḥ anāmabhiśca'; nāmamātraiḥ svarūpabhedaśūnyaiḥ acaturbhiḥ'; vāsudevasaṅkarṣaṇapradyumnāniruddhaiḥ asākaṃ navatiṃ'; navatisaṅkhyākān avyatīn'; deveṣu yaugiko ayaṃ śabdaḥ viśeṣeṇādhikān devān kimutānyān avṛttaṃ cakraṃ na'; vartulaṃ rathāṅgamiva yugapat aavīvipat', viparivartana iti dhātuḥ, paryavartayadityarthaḥ । aṣṭau vasavaḥ ekādaśa rudrāḥ viṣṇuvyatiriktaikādaśādityāḥ hiraṇyagarbheṇa saha daśa prajeśvarāḥ pradhānena pañcāśanmaruta iti navatiḥ । tattvapradīpe tu prathamaṃ ṭīkoktārthamabhidhāya 
ādityā vasavo rudrā marutaścāśvināvapi ।
bṛhaspatiśac kāmaśca manurdakṣo vināyakaḥ ।
bhṛguścaivāniruddhaśca dharmo nirṛtireva ca ।
kuberasahitā devāḥ navatissamprakīrtitāḥ ।
ananto garuḍo vāyuḥ catvāro brahmaṇā saha ।
iti pramāṇānusāreṇa prakārāntareṇa caturuttaranavatiruktā । tatraiva nāmavadbhiḥ kīrtimadbhiriti ca vyākhyātam ।

paro mātrayā tanvā vṛdhāna na te mahitvamanvaśnuvanti ।
na te viṣṇo jāyamāno na jāto devamahimnaḥ paramantamāpa ।
eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇānāmativyāptiṃ viṣṇvekaniṣṭhatvoktyā smṛtyā cārthāt parihṛtāmapi sākṣādanyatra lakṣaṇābhāvaṃ pratipādayantyā śrutyā nirāha aparaḥ'; iti । tattvodyotaṭīkoktarītyā muktā amuktāśceti śeṣaḥ । ata eva ṭīkāyāṃ ka ityuktam । tathā ca atanvā'; svamūrtyaiva na tu kīrtimātreṇa avṛdhāna'; aparicchinna he viṣṇo tvaṃ yato amātrayā'; miteḥ aparaḥ'; vilakṣaṇo asi aparimito asīti yāvat । ata evaṃbhūtasya ate mahitvaṃ'; jagatsṛṣṭyādirūpaṃ mahimānam aanu'; api ke api muktā amuktāśca anāśnuvanti'; na prāpnuvantītyarthaḥ । yadvā anāśnuvanti'; nānubhavantītyarthaḥ । nāśnuvantīti vartamānaniṣedhāt syāduttaratretyata āha ana'; iti । prāpnotīti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca he aviṣṇo'; adevamahimnaḥ'; ramādimahimnaḥ aparam antaṃ'; sīmānaṃ mahimatāratamyaparāvadhibhūtaṃ ate mahitvaṃ'; mahimānaṃ ajāyamāno'; na prāpnoti, jāto anāpa'; ityarthaḥ । upalakṣaṇaṃ caitat janiṣyamāṇo na prāpsyatītyapi draṣṭavyam । ata eva tattvapradīpe "paro mātrayā tanvā vṛdhāna । na te mahitvamanvaśnuvanti । ubhe te vidma rajasī pṛthivyā viṣṇo devatvaṃ paramasya vitse । na te viṣṇo jāyamāno na jāto devamahimnaḥ paramantamāpa । udastabhnā nākamṛṣvaṃ bṛhantaṃ dādhartha prācīṃ kakubhaṃ pṛthivyāḥ"iti ṛgdvayamevameva vyākhyātam । tathā hi mātrāyāḥ paraḥ parimāṇātītaḥ tanvā vṛdhānaḥ tanvā vardhamānaḥ dehena pūrṇaḥ itthaṃ bhāve tṛtīyā 
deharūpeṇa pūrṇa ityarthaḥ । yataścidānandādyātmako viṣṇorabhinnaśca dehaḥ । te mahitvaṃ mahimānaṃ nānubhavanti na prāpnuvanti ca । te tvadīyāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ prakṛteḥ rajasī rajoguṇakārye ubhe puṇyapāpe vayaṃ vidmaḥ । prakṛteḥ rajasā hi puṇyapāpe sṛjyate । paramasya te mahimānaṃ tvameva vitse । tvameva mahimnaḥ mahimasamudāyasyāntaṃ brahmaṇaḥ śriyo vā mahimānamatiśayito hi viṣṇumahimā anyamahimnāṃ param antaṃ te mahimānaṃ na kañcidāpa । yatrākaṃ nāsti tannākam । ṛṣvaṃ prakāśarūpam । bṛhantaṃ pūrṇaṃ lokam udastabhnāḥ udastabhnaḥ uccairastambhayaḥ । pṛthivyāḥ prathivyātmakasya brahmāṇḍasya prācīṃ kakubhaṃ diśaṃ indrasthāpanena dādhartha dhṛtavānasi । sarvadhāraṇopalakṣaṇametaditi ।

yo naḥ pitā janitā yo vidhātā dhāmāni veda bhavanāni viśvā ।
ityādi ca ।
jagatkāraṇatvaṃ ca brahmaṇo na vikāritvena, kintu pitṛvannimittattvenaiveti śrutyā darśayati, 
ayaḥ'; iti । ayaḥ'; eka eva anaḥ'; asmadādisarveṣāṃ ajanitā'; janayitaiva apitā'; na dattaputrapitṛvat pālakapitṛmātram । yadvā "sa eva pitṛsaṃsthastupātṛtvātpitṛnāmakaḥ"ityaitareyabhāṣyadiśā "pitā pātā"iti tattvapradīpokteḥ ajanitā'; janakaḥ apitā'; pātā cetyarthaḥ । ayo vidhātā'; viśeṣeṇa dhārakaḥ poṣakaḥ, "muktānāṃ poṣaṇaṃ ca jñānamokṣadānena"iti tattvapradīpokteḥ । "vidhātā kartā"iti prameyadīpoktiḥ । tasyā dhāraṇapoṣaṇayoriti bhāvaḥ । yo aviśvā'; viśvāni sarvāṇi bhuvanāni tadgata adhāmāni'; gṛhāṇi jīvādisvarūpāṇi ca aveda'; jānātītyarthaḥ । aityādi'; iti vākyam auktārthe pramāṇam'; iti śeṣaḥ । ādiśabdena etajjātīyakaśrutyantaraṃ "dyāvābhūmī janayan"iti ca gṛhyate ।
। iti janmādhikaraṇam ।

। śāstrayonitvādhikaraṇam ।
anumānato anye na kalpanīyāḥ ।
śāstrayonitvāt ।
atrādhikaraṇe pūrvoktajagajjanmādikāraṇatvarūpabrahmalakṣaṇasya rudrādiṣvativyāptiparihārāya jagatkāraṇe pramāṇamucyate । siddhāntapratijñāmupaskṛtya darśayati aanumānataḥ'; iti । kāraṇatveneti śeṣaḥ। tathā ca śivo jagajjanmādikartā sarvajñatvāt vyatirekeṇa yajñadattavat ityādyanumānāt viṣṇoḥ aanye'; rudrādayo api jagatkāraṇatvena ana kalpanīyāḥ'; na śaṅkyā ityarthaḥ। kuta ityatastatra hetvākāṅkṣāyāṃ sūtramupanyasyati aśāstrayonitvāt'; iti। jagatkāraṇasyeti śeṣaḥ । "tannirdhāritayuktirvā"ityanuvyākhyāpade "tannirdhāritetyataḥ paraṃ vyāptiśabdo adhyāhāryaḥ"iti sudhokteryathā tatra madhye adhyāhāraḥ, yathā vā "sarvendriyavivarjitatvādyartha uktaḥ"iti gītābhāṣyaprameyadīpe ādītyataḥ paraṃ śabdaśabdo adhyāhārya ityuktestatra yathā madhye adhyāhāraḥ, yathā vā "puruṣādvadhavikārasamūhatenakṛteṣu"iti mahābhāṣyavākye samāsamadhye teneti padādhyāhāraḥ, tathātrāpi śāstraśabdātparamekaśabdo adhyāhāryaḥ yoniśabdātprāk jñaptiśabdaśca । tathā ca ṛgādirūpaṃ śāstraṃ ca tadekamasahāyaṃ ca jñaptiyonirjñaptikāraṇaṃ yasya vastunaḥ tattathoktaṃ tasya bhāvastattvaṃ tasmāditisūtrārthaḥ । anena na jagatkāraṇamānumānikaṃ tasya śāstraikasamadhigamyatvāt dharmādivat ityanumānamuktaṃ bhavati । na ca dṛṣṭānte sādhyavaikalyam । na hi dharmādiniścayo anumānena bhavati । tathā ca anumānādanyeṣāṃ jagatkāraṇatāsādhanamayuktamiti na teṣu lakṣaṇasyātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ ।

"nāvedavinmanute taṃ bṛhantam । sarvānubhumātmana sāmparāye"
"aupaniṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ" ityādiśrutibhyaśca ।
kāraṇasya śāstraikavedyatvaṃ kuta ityata āha ana'; iti । taittirīyavākyamidam । atra hrasvokārapāṭhaḥ। aaupaniṣadaḥ'; iti śrutyantaram । atrāṅaḥ praśleṣaḥ kāryaḥ । ādiśabdena "sarve vedā yatpadaṃ" "vedāhyevainaṃ" "taṃ tvaupaniṣadaṃ puruṣaṃ pṛcchāmi" iti vākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । ataṃ'; pūrvaprakṛtaṃ abṛhantaṃ'; pūrṇaṃ asarvānubhuṃ'; sarvamanubhavatīti sarvānubhūḥ taṃ sarvajñam । yadvā sarvamanubhāvayatīti sarvānubhustaṃ ātmānaṃ sarvajagatkartāraṃ sarvasvāminaṃ vā । asāmparāye'; samyakparasyāyaḥ prāptiḥ samparāyaḥ sa eva sāmparāyaḥ, tādarthye saptamī, tathā ca mokṣāya aavedavit'; viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkoktarītyā atra vedaśabdena sadāgamā gṛhyante । tathā ca sadāgamatadarthājñānī vedaviruddhajñānī vā ana manute'; na jānāti, vedādanyat jagatkartāraṃ na pramāpayatīti yāvat । kintu vedavideva jānāti veda eva pramāpayatīti prathamaśrutyarthaḥ । puruṣo jagatkartā ā aupaniṣadaḥ upaniṣadekasamadhigamya ityanyaśrutyarthaḥ । gamyatvaṃ grāhyatvaṃ taddhitārthaḥ । ādiśabdopāttaśrutyapekṣayā aśrutibhyaśca'; iti bahuvacanam। caśabdo adhyāhṛtasādhyasamuccaye, svoktisamuccaye vā । asya śāstrayonitvādityanenānvayaḥ । kāraṇasyeti śeṣaḥ । tathā caivamādiśrutibhyaḥ kāraṇasya śāstraikayonitvāvagamāt nāsiddhiriti bhāvaḥ । nañdvayāṅghaṭitaśrutyudāharaṇena sūtra ekaśabdo adhyāhārya iti sūcitam ।

na cānumānasya niyataprāmāṇyam ।
śrutisāhāyyarahitamanumānaṃ na kutracit ।
niścayātsādhayedarthaṃ pramāṇāntarameva ca ।
aupaniṣadasyāpi kāraṇasyānumānena siddhiḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha ana ca'; iti । tathā ca aanumānasya'; anumānamātrasya aprāmāṇyam'; atīndriyārthapramāpakatvaṃ netyarthaḥ । tathā ca na tenānyasya jagatkartṛtāsādhanaṃ yuktamiti bhāvaḥ । nanu kathametat asarvadharmopapatteśca'; ityadhikaraṇe svātantryādihetunā viṣṇoḥ pūrṇatvādisiddhyaṅgīkārādityata uktam aniyata'; iti । idaṃ ca svātantryārthakaṃ pramāṇarūpaprakṛtyarthaviśeṣaṇam । anumānasyeti hetugarbham । tathā ca anumānatvādeva na tasya svātantryeṇādṛṣṭārthaniścāyakatvaṃ, pratipakṣādisambhavāt, kintvasvātantryeṇa । svātantryaṃ ca sahāyarāhityam । tacca na svātantryādihetāvasti śrutisāhāyyarahitatvena svatantratvānna pramāṇatvamiti bhāvaḥ । kuto nānumānasya niyataprāmāṇyamityata āha aśruti'; iti । smṛterapyupalakṣakametat । atra sahāyaśabdo mūlavācī । tasmātsvārthe ṣyañ । śrutiśca tatsāhāyyaṃ ceti karmadhārayaḥ, tatastena rahitamiti tatpuruṣaḥ । śrutyanugrāhyatvarahitamiti yāvat । caḥ samuccaye । evaśabdo bhinnakramaḥ । tathā ca akutracit'; asmādādyadṛṣṭe śraute arthe aśrutisāhāyyarahitamanumānam'; īśvaro na svatantraḥ cetanatvādityādi liṅgam, tathā yajñahiṃsādharmatvānumānaṃ ca tathā apramāṇāntaram'; anumānādanyat rāmakṛṣmādidoṣagrāhi mānuṣatvagrāhi ca pratyakṣaṃ aniścayāt'; sphuṭamatīndriyārthaṃ ana sādhayet'; iti yojanā । yadvā arthaṃ niścayānna sādhayenna sādhayedevetyarthaḥ । uktaṃ hi gītābhāṣye "sa niścayena yoktavyaḥ yoktavya eva bubhūṣuṇetyarthaḥ"iti uktaṃ hi prameyadīpikāyām "ayogavyavacchede niścayaśabdaḥ"iti ।

śrutismṛtisahāyaṃ yat pramāṇāntaramuttamam ।
pramāṇapadavīṃ gacchennātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।
tarhi kīdṛśasya pratyakṣāderadṛṣṭārthaniścāyakatvamityata āha aśruti'; iti । tathā ca śrutismṛtirūpasahakāriyuktaṃ ayatpramāṇāntaraṃ'; yaśodādipratyakṣaṃ tat auttamam'; । ataḥ tat apramāṇapadavīm'; anupramāṇasya pramākaraṇatvarūpāṃ paddhatiṃ agacchet'; prāpnuyādityanvayaḥ । taditi pāṭhe apyevameva yojanā । evaṃ śrutismṛtisahāyo yastarkaḥ viṣṇuḥ svatantraḥ pūrṇatvāditi samavyāptikānumānaṃ so api pramāṇapadavīṃ gacchedityanvayaḥ । aatra'; asmin viṣaye avicāraṇā'; saṃśayo ana'; kārya ityarthaḥ nātretyanena svoktārthe aprāmāṇyaśaṅkā nirākṛtā ।

pūrvottarāvirodhena ko atrārtho abhimato bhavet ।
ityādyamūhanaṃ tarkaḥ śuṣkatarkaṃ tu varjayet ।
ityādi mahākaurme ।
tarkapadasya vyāpyāropeṇetyādyanyathāpratītinirāsāya tarkasvarūpamāha apūrva'; iti । aatra'; vipratipanne vākye ako artho abhimataḥ'; tātparyaviṣayo abhavedityādyam'; evaṃbhūtavimarśapūrvakaṃ apūrvottarāvirodhena'; upakramopasaṃhārāvirodhena tadaikarūpyeṇaliṅgāntarasyāpyupalakṣaṇametat tathā ca upakramāditātparyaliṅgaiḥ atra tātparyaviṣayārtho ayameva bhavedityādyaṃ yat aūhanaṃ'; yatpramājñānaṃ tatsādhanaṃ liṅgaṃ sa eva atarkaḥ'; atrābhimataḥ । aśuṣkatarkaṃ'; śrutismṛtisahāyarahitaṃ tannirapekṣaṃ cetanatvādi tarkaṃ tu varjayet, tenātīndriyārthaniścayo na kārya ityarthaḥ । kecittu ka ityasyobhayārthatvamāśrisya "kaśchandasām" iti vākyam aatra'; ityanena parāmṛśyate । ata eva aityādyam'; ityapi yuktamityāhuḥ । akaurme'; ityanantaraṃ purāṇe yata uktamiti śeṣaḥ । asya ana ca'; ityanenānvayaḥ ।

śakyatvāccānumānāṃ sarvatra ।
na kevalaṃ śrutyādisāhityahīnānumānasya prāmāṇyābhāve sādhaka sadbhāvaḥ, api tu tatprāmāṇyābhyupagame bādhakaṃ cāstītyāha aśakyatvāt'; iti । prayoktumiti śeṣaḥ । aanumānām'; iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī । caśabdo na kevalamityuktasamuccayārthaḥ । tathā ca śrutyādisāhityahīnānām aanumānāṃ'; cetanatvavastutvādirūpakevalahetūnāṃ asarvatra'; rudrāderjagatkāraṇatvābhāvādau śaśādeḥ śṛṅgitvādau sādhyo api prayoktuṃ aśakyatvāt'; nānumānasya niyataprāmāṇyamiti yojanā ।

sarvatra śakyate kartumāgamaṃ hi vinānumā ।
tasmānna sā śaktimatī vināgamamudīkṣitum ।
atraiva pramāṇamāha sarvatreti । ahi'; yasmāt aāgamaṃ vinā'; taddhīnā aanumā'; asarvatra'; īśvarakāraṇatvābhāvādau akartuṃ'; prayoktuṃ aśakyate'; atasmāt'; anumā aāgamaṃ vinā udīkṣitum'; udīkṣayituṃ jñāpayitum arthamiti śeṣaḥ aśaktimatī'; sāmarthyayutā netyarthaḥ । avārāhe'; ityasyāpi akaurme'; itivadanvayaḥ । tasmātkevalānumānasyānirṇāyakatvācchāstreṇaiva kartṛtvaniścaya iti sthitam ।

reto dhāturvaṭakaṇikā ghṛtadhūmādhivāsanam ।
jātismṛtirayaskāntaḥ sūryakānto ambubhakṣaṇam ।
pretya bhūtāpyayaścaiva devatābhyupayācanam ।
mṛte karmanivṛttiśca pramāṇamiti niścayaḥ ।
iti mokṣadharmavacanānna nāstikyavādo yujyate ।
nanvatīndriyārthābhāvena pratyakṣetarasyāprāmāṇyātkathaṃ śāstrādīśvarasiddhiriti nāstikyavādaṃ mokṣadharmavacanena nirācaṣṭe reta iti । reta ityādiprathamaikavacanāntānāṃ padānāṃ pratyekaṃ pramāṇamiti padenānvayaḥ । aatrārthe'; iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca retodhātvādi aatrārthe'; atīndriyārthasattve anumānādiprāmāṇye ca pramāṇaṃ pramāpakaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ। bhāṣyakārīyadvitīyetiśabdasya evaṃ mokṣadharmavacanātpratītairhetubhirnāstikyavādo na yujyata iti yojanā । nāstikā eva nāstikyaṃ, nāstikasamudāyo vā nāstikyam । tathā ca nāsti paralokaḥ, dharmo nāsti, adharmo nāstīti dhiyā vāda ityarthaḥ । yadvā nyāyadīpikoktarītyā āstikyaṃ dharmādāvastyanena prayojanamiti bhāvo buddhiḥ, tatpūrvako vādaḥ, tadanyo nāstikyavāda ityarthaḥ । retodhātvādīnāmanumāpakatvaprakārastvittham retaśśabditacaramadhātuśarīrayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvo na pratyakṣaḥ, kintvanvayavyatirekākhyānumānagamya iti tatprāmāṇyasiddhiḥ । mṛtaśarīre siktasya retasaḥ śarīrākāraṇatvena yadadhiṣṭhite śarīre siktaṃ retaḥ śarīrātmanā pariṇamati tajjīvasiddhiḥ। vandhyādisarvaśarīre siktasya retasaḥ kāryākaratvena yatpreritaṃ retaḥ kāryakaraṃ tadīśvarādṛṣṭasiddhiḥ । tata eva tatpratipādakāgamaprāmāṇyasiddhiḥ । evaṃ vātapittādidhāturapathyādinā jīvaccharīre kvacideva vikriyate, na mṛtaśarīre, nāpi jīvatsarvaśarīreṣu । tato jīveśvaratadbodhakāgamaprāmāṇyādisiddhiḥ । vaṭakaṇikāpadoktavaṭabījādvaṭa utpadyata iti suprasiddham, na ca bharjitāyāstasyāḥ, nāpyabharjitābhyassarvābhya iti tatprerakeśvādṛṣṭasiddhiḥ । ghṛtena jīvaccharīra eva pīnatā jāyate, na mṛtaśarīre kṣiptena nāpi jāvatsarvaśarīreṣu । adhūmādhivāsanaṃ'; nāma puṣpādisampattyarthaḥ dhūmena vṛkṣasya saṃskāraḥ । tenāśuṣkavṛkṣeṣveva puṣpādisampattiḥ, na śuṣke, nāpyaśuṣkeṣu sarveṣu । etābhyāmapi liṅgābhyāṃ jīveśvarādṛṣṭādisiddhiḥ । keṣāñcitsādhanaviśeṣāt ajātismṛtiḥ'; pūrvajanmasmṛtirbhavati anenaiva puṇyena evaṃ svargo anubhūtaḥ, anena pāpenetthaṃ narakamanubhūtamiti । sā ca kasyacideva, na sarvasya, na cetanādyabhāve sā yuktetyato api cetanādṛṣṭādisiddhiḥ । ayaskāntākhyaśilāviśeṣeṇāyo bhramati, na cācetane ceṣṭakatvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ, nāpi sarvacetanānāmityetasmādapi tatprerakeśvarādṛṣṭādisiddhiḥ । sūryakāntākhyaśilāviśeṣeṇāgnirjāyate, na cāsau śaktiracetane yuktā । ato api prerakeśvarādṛṣṭādisiddhiḥ । ambubhakṣaṇena jīvaccharīra eva tṛṣṇā nivartate, na ca tanmṛtaśarīre pātrāntare vā nihitaṃ pacyate । nāpi jīvatsarvaśarīreṣu । tasmādapi jīveśvarādisiddhiḥ । pretyetyanantaraṃ sthitasyeti śeṣaḥ । apretya'; jīvaṃ vihāya sthitasya dehasya abhūtāpyayo'; bhūteṣu laya ityarthaḥ । tathā ca maraṇena dehasya pṛthivyādipañcabhūteṣu layo bhavati, na jīvato, na cecchayetyato api tanniyāmakeśvarādisiddhiḥ । evaṃ devatābhyupayācanena keṣāñcideva sampadādikaṃ bhavati, evaṃ mṛte dehe ceṣṭānivṛttirbhavati, na purā na svecchayā । ato api jīveśvarādṛṣṭādisiddhiriti ।

darśanācca tapa ādiphalasya ।
yuktyantareṇāpi nāstikyavādaṃ dūṣayati darśanācceti । ādiśabdena pāpaṃ gṛhyate। tathā ca svādhyāyabrahmacaryādirūpātyutkaṭatapaādiphalasya tejassvitvādeḥ pratyakṣata eva darśanācca na nāstikyavādo yujyata ityarthaḥ । puṇyapāpākhyātīndriyavastunastatsādhakānumānāgamaprāmāṇyasya cāṅgīkāryatvāditi bhāvaḥ ।

ṛgyajussāmātharvāśca bhārataṃ pañcarātrakam ।
mūlarāmāyaṇaṃ caiva śāstramityabhidhīyate ।
nanu yadyanumānasyāniścāyakatvena śāstrādeva kāraṇatvasiddhiḥ, tarhi pāśupatādiśāstreṇa rudrāderjagatkāraṇatvasiddhiḥ syādityata āha ṛgiti । akārānto ayamatharvaśabdaḥ । ṛkca yajuśca sāma cātharvaśceti tathoktāḥ । evaśabdasya ṛgādikameveti sambandhaḥ । amūlarāmāyaṇamevetyavāntararāmāyaṇavyudāsaḥ'; iti sudhoktiḥ । caśabdau samuccaye ।

yaccānukūlametasya tacca śāstraṃ prakīrtitam ।
ato anyo granthavistāro naiva śāstraṃ kuvartma tat ।
iti skānde ।
tarhi mānavādyaśāstraṃ syādityata āha yacceti । co avadhāraṇe, dvitīyo apyarthe । tathā ca aetasya'; ṛgādeḥ ayat'; yadeva aanukūlam'; aviruddhārthapratipādakaṃ mānavādi purāṇādikaṃ vā atat'; sarvamapi aśāstraṃprakīrtitaṃ'; prāmāṇikaiḥ aataḥ'; etasmāt vedāt tadanukūlācca aanyaḥ'; viruddhaḥ udāsīnaśca yo agranthavistāraḥ'; pāśupatādirūpagranthavistaraḥ atannaiva śāstram', kintu akuvartma'; kutsitamārgaḥ, mārga iva mārgaḥ, kutsitajñānopāyo amānamityarthaḥ। ṛgādikamevetyevakārastu viruddhādiviṣaya iti bhāvaḥ । skānde purāṇe ityuktamityanvayaḥ । pāśupatādeḥ kuvartmatvamitiśabdārthaḥ ।

sāṅkhyaṃ yogaḥ pāśupataṃ vetāraṇyakameva ca ।
ityārabhya vedapañcarātrayoraikyābhiprāyeṇa pañcarātrasyaiva prāmāṇyamuktamitareṣāṃ bhinnamatatvaṃ pradarśya mokṣadharmeṣvapi ।
ito api pāśupatādikaṃ kuvartmetyāha sāṅkhyamiti । atraivaṃ yojanā na kevalaṃ skānde, kintu mokṣadharmeṣvapi । asāṅkhyaṃ yogaḥ pāśupataṃ vedāraṇyakameva ca'; aityārabhya'; upakramyādhītena
pañcarātras kṛtsnasya vaktā nārāyaṇassvayam ।
jñāneṣveteṣu rājendra sarveṣvetaddhiśiṣyate ।
ityuttaravākyena sāṅkhyādiṣu prakṛteṣvapi tatparityāgena pañcarātrasyaiva prāmāṇyarūpamādhikyamuktaṃ yato ataḥ pāśupatādikaṃ kuvartma amānameveti । nanvanena pañcarātraprāmāṇyameva bhavennānyāprāmāṇyamityata āha itareṣāmiti । vedapañcarātrayoranyeṣāṃ sāṅkhyādīnāmityarthaḥ। abhinnamatattvaṃ'; viruddhadarśanatvaṃ apradarśya'; jñāpayitvā pratipādyeti yāvat।
sāṅkhyaṃ yogaḥ pāśupataṃ vedāraṇyakameva ca ।
jñānānyetāni bhinnāni nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।
iti vākyaśeṣeṇeti śeṣaḥ । pradarśyetyasya pañcarātrasyaiva prāmāṇyamuktamityanenānvayaḥ । parasparaviruddhānāmekaprāmāṇyoktāvanyāprāmāṇyalābhāditi bhāvaḥ । tarhi vedāraṇyakasyāpyaprāmāṇyaṃ syādityata āha vedeti । aaikyābhiprāyeṇa'; iti । ekārthatvarūpamūlamūlibhāvābhiprāyeṇetyarthaḥ । tathā ca pañcarātrasya vedasamānārthatvena tatprāmāṇyoktau vedaprāmāṇyamevoktaṃ bhavatīti na tasyāprāmāṇyamiti bhāvaḥ । na caikyābhiprāyaḥ kutaḥ kalpyata iti vācyam, yato adṛṣṭaviṣayasya pauruṣeyasya pañcarātrasya nirmūlatve aprāmāṇyādādhikyakathanamasaṅgataṃ syāt । asāṅkhyam'; īśvarāvatārānyakapiloktaṃ śāstram ।
kapilo vāsudevākhyaḥ tantraṃ sāṅkhyaṃ jagāda ha ।
sarvāgamaviruddhaṃ ca kapilo anyo jagāda ha ।
ityuktatvāt । ayogo'; hi hiraṇyagarbhoktaṃ pātañjalam । apāśupataṃ'; paśupatinā proktam । araṇye nirjane deśe adhyetavyatvādāraṇyakamityupaniṣaducyate । vedāścāraṇyakāni ca, teṣāṃ samāhāraḥ vedāraṇyakaṃ, dvandvaikavadbhāvo vā । varṇāśramarājadānadharmādipratipādyadharmabahutvāt mokṣadharmāṇāṃ bhedādvā mokṣadharmeṣviti bahuvacanam । ata eva tattvapradīpe mokṣadharmeṣviti bahuvacanaṃ dharmabhedādityuktam । mokṣadharme hi 
sāṅkhyaṃ yogaḥ pāśupataṃ vedāraṇyakameva ca ।
jñānānyetāni bhinnāni utāho neti cocyatām ।
iti vaiśampāyanoktaṃ prativacanaṃ cāsti । ime yudhiṣṭhirabhīṣmakartṛke ca । bhagavataḥ jñānāni jñānasādhanāni bhinnāni bhinnamatāni । viruddhanāmapi matānāṃ na sarveṣāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ sambhavati vastuno bahurūpatvābhāvāt, kintvekasyātra prāmāṇyamitareṣāmaprāmāṇyaṃ vācyam । tatra kasya prāmāṇyaṃ kasya vāprāmāṇyamiti punaryudhiṣṭhirajanamejayahārdapraśnottaramāha bhīṣmo vaiśampāyanaśca । "sāṅkhyasya vaktā kapilaḥ"ityārabhya "pañcarātrasya kṛtsnasya"ityanena jñāneṣu jñānasādhaneṣu etatpañcarātram । abhiprāyastu paramāptatamena nārāyaṇena sarvasya pañcarātrasya kṛtatvātprāmāṇyaṃ tāvatsiddham, viruddhānāṃ caikaprāmāṇye anyāprāmāṇyaṃ ca। etaccādyavākyasthavedāraṇyakapadena vedamūlakapañcarātrasyottaravākyasthapañcarātrapadena ca mūlabhūtavedāraṇyakasyopalakṣaṇāmaṅgīkṛtyobhayorekavākyatāyāmeva sambhavati । anyathā pañcarātrasya pūrvamaprakṛtatvena pūrvottaravākyayorasaṅgatatvāpātaḥ । upalakṣaṇāmaṅgīkṛtyaikavākyatāyāṃ ca svīkṛtāyāṃ vedapañcarātrayoreva prāmāṇayaṃ siddhyati । na tadviruddhapāśupatādīnāmiti teṣāmaprāmāṇyameveti ।

śāstraṃ yoniḥ pramāṇamasyeti śāstrayoni ।
evaṃ sūtraṃ vyākhyāya yatpareṇoktaṃ śāstrasya yoniriti tadayuktamiti bhāvena svābhimatārthaṃ darśayati śāstramiti । kāraṇārthakena yoniśabdena yogyatayā jñaptessambandhe pramāṇamiti paryavasyatītyabhiprāyeṇa ayoniḥ pramāṇam'; iti vyākhyātam । aasya'; jagatkāraṇasya aiti śāstrayoni'; ityanantaraṃ tuśabdo adhyāhāryaḥ । ata eva gītābhāṣye "iti tu śāstrayonitvam"ityuktam । turevārthaḥ । tathā ca śāstraṃ yoniḥ pramāṇaṃ yasya tacchāstrayonītyeva śāstrayonipadārtho brahma, na tu śāstrasya yonītyarthaḥ। paravyākhyānaṃ tūktānupayuktamayuktaṃ ceti ṭīkāyāmeva dūṣitam ।
। iti śāstrayonitvādhikaraṇam ।

। samanvayādhikaraṇam ।
ajñānāṃ pratīyamānamapi netareṣāṃ śāstrayonitvam ।
kutaḥ?
tat tu samanvayāt ।
atrādhikaraṇe jagatkāraṇasya śāstrayonitvānna lakṣaṇātivyāptiriti pūrvādhikaraṇaphalākṣepaparihāramukhena tasya lakṣaṇatvasiddhaye viṣṇoreva jagatkāraṇatvena śāstragamyatvaṃ netareṣāmapīti samarthyate । pūrvapakṣasūcanapūrvakaṃ siddhāntamāha ajñānāmiti ।। itareṣāṃ iti sambandhe । samuccayārthasyāperubhayatrānvayaḥ । pratītyā āgamopalakṣaṇā vā । tathā ca na kevalaṃ pāśupatādyuktam, kintu aajñānāṃ'; śrutitātparyārthājñānibhirāpātataḥ jñāyamānamapi na kevalaṃ viṣṇoḥ kintu aitareṣāṃ'; rudrādīnāmapi śāstrayonitvaṃ, jagatkāraṇatvena śāstragamyatvaṃ netyarthaḥ । nanu pratītyāderajñānamūlatvādikaṃ parikalpyānyeṣāṃ kāraṇatayā śāstrayonitvāgrahaṇe ko heturiti pṛcchati kuta iti । pratīyamānamapītyanenāsyānvayaḥ । tatra hetukathanāya sūtramupanyasyati tattviti । yata ityādau grāhyam ।

anvaya upapattyādi liṅgam ।
sūtrākṣarāṇi vyācaṣṭe anvaya iti । anvīyate svārthena sambadhyate tatparatayā jñāyate śāstraṃ śabdo vānenetyanvayaḥ upapattyāditātparyaliṅgamityarthaḥ । sūtrānusārādekavacanaṃ samudāyābhiprāyam । tena copakramādīnāṃ kvacidavirodhaṃ sūcayati । ādipadaṃ śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāmapi grāhakam । atra śrutyādiṣaṭkaṃ ca grāhyamiti ṭīkokteḥ । atra vākye śrutyādiṣaṭkamapyādipadena grāhyamiti hi tasyārthaḥ । parantu śrutyādīnāmupakramādivattātparyagrāhakatvābhāvādāgamārthamātranirṇāyakatvāt nātra tannidarśakapramāṇoktiḥ । ata evottaratra 
śrutirliṅgaṃ samākhyā ca vākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ tathā ।
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ balīyaḥ syādevamāgamanirṇaye ।
iti tatrāpi pramāṇaṃ vakṣyati । uktaṃ hi pramāṇalakṣaṇaṭīkāyām "upakramādīnāṃ tātparyaliṅgatvameteṣāṃ punarartha eveti viśeṣajñāpanārtho yogavibhāgaḥ"iti । na caivam "atra śrutyādiṣaṭkaṃ ca grāhyam"iti ṭīkāyāṃ tātparyagrāhakeṣvantarbhāvoktirayukteti vācyam, yato atretyasya samanvayaśabdārtha ityevārtho na tātparyagrahakeṣviti, aākāśastalliṅgāt'; aśabdādeva pramitaḥ'; ityādau śrutiliṅgādibhirāgamārthaniraṇayadarśanena teṣāmapi anvīyate śaktirūpasambandhavattayā jñāyate padajātamebhiritivyutpattyā anvayaśabdārthatvaucityāt । na copakramopasaṃhārābhyāsāpūrvatāphalārthavādopapattayaḥ śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyāśca tātparyaliṅgānīti jñānapādīyasudhāvirodha iti vācyam, atra śakterapi saṃyojanāt । ata eva candrikāyāmupakramādipramāṇakaḥ śaktitātparyalakṣaṇassambandhaḥ samanvaya ityuktam । atradipadaṃ śrutyādīnāmapi grāhakam । vyutkrameṇānvayaḥ । anenātra bṛhatsaṃhitāvacanodāharaṇaṃ vakṣyamāṇasya śrutirliṅgamiti vacanasyopalakṣakamiti sūcitam ।

uktaṃ ca bṛhatsaṃhitāyām 
upakramopasaṃhārāvabhyāso apūrvatā phalam ।
arthavādopapattī ca liṅgaṃ tātparyanirṇaye ।
iti ।
kāni tānyupapattyādīni kutra ca liṅgānītyata āha uktaṃ ceti । upapattyādītyanuṣajyate। na kevalamupapattyādyuktaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ, kintu tajjñāpyaṃ coktamiti cārthaḥ । asmaduktamupapattyādi liṅgaṃ bṛhatsaṃhitāyāmapyuktamiti vā । kimuktamityatastatpaṭhati upakrameti । prakaraṇādirupakramaḥ tadanta upasaṃhāraḥ । upakramopasaṃhāraśca tau tathoktau । atropakramopasaṃhāratadaikarūpyābhyāsāpūrvatāphalārthavādāśceti pramāṇalakṣaṇokteḥ pratyekavivakṣayā viśakalitāvupakramopasaṃhārau dvau samudāyavivakṣayā ubhayāvirodhalakṣaṇaṃ ekārthatvalakṣaṇaṃ vā tadaikarūpyamapi pṛthaktātparyagrāhakamanusandheyam । ata eva dvivacanaprayogaḥ । ekaprakārāsakṛduktirabhyāsaḥ । prācuryeṇa pramāṇāntarāsiddhārthabodhakatā apūrvatā । phalavadarthapratipādakaṃ phalam । stutiḥ, nindā, ekakartṛkopākhyānarūpā parakṛtiḥ, anekakartṛkopākhyānarūpaḥ purākalpaśca, arthavādaḥ । atātparyanirṇaye'; vākyatātparyaniścaye aliṅgaṃ'; sādhanamitiyarthaḥ। yadvā nirṇetavye tātparye sādhye aliṅgaṃ'; heturityarthaḥ। liṅgamityasya upakramādipadaiḥ yathāyogyaṃ pratyekaṃ sambandhaḥ । smṛterupakramāditve api virodhe uttarottaraprābalyasūcanāya bhāṣye upapattyādīti vyatyasyoktiḥ । sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvena upapatterupakramādibhyaḥ pṛthaguktiḥ । yadvā etaccopakramādi svārthe śabdātmakamapi idametatparam abādhe satyetadupakramatvāt
ityādirūpeṇa vākyatātparye liṅgaṃ ca bhavati । upapattistu yathāgnyādirūpasvarthe tathā tātparye api ayametattātparyaviṣayaḥ upapannatvāt iti prakāreṇa liṅgarūpeti pṛthaguktiḥ ।

upakramāditātparyaliṅgaiḥ samyaṅnirūpyamāṇe tadevaśāstragamyam ।
sūtraṃ yojayati upakramādīti । aśāstre'; iti śeṣaḥ । samityasyārthaḥ samyagiti । sarvasminnityapi draṣṭavyam । anirūpyamāṇe'; ityanena saṃśabdārthasya adhyāhṛtakriyayānvayo darśitaḥ । tuśabdasyārtha eveti । aśāstrayoni'; ityanuṣaktapadasyārthaḥ śāstrāgamyamiti । tathā ca yato atrānvayapadoktaiḥ śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyopakramādibhiḥ śaktitātparyaliṅgaiḥ asaṃ samyak'; balābalavimarśapūrvakaṃ asarvasmin'; śāstre ṛgādirūpe anirūpyamāṇe'; vicāryamāṇe ekārthe śaktitātparyarūpavyāpakadharmavattayā avagamyamāne atadeva'; viṣṇvākhyaṃ brahmaiva aśāstragamyaṃ'; tatpramāṇakaṃ pratīyate, na rudrādi, ato ajñānāṃ pratīyamānamapi netareṣāṃ śāstrayonitvamiti yojanā । liṅgairiti tṛtīyayā nirūpyamāṇe iti saptamīprayoge ca upakramādikaṃ tātparyahetuḥ । tātparyaṃ ca śāstrapramāṇakatve heturiti sūcitaṃ bhavati । na kevalamupapattyādikaṃ samanvayaśabdārthaḥ, kintu taddhetukaḥ śāstrajanyapramāgocaratvarūpaḥ śāstrayonitve hetubhūtaḥ । "tatparatvasambandho api"iti sudhokteḥ । anena asamanvayāt'; sāvakāśatvaniravakāśatvādinā balābalaniścayapurassaraṃ anyatarabādhayā vākyārthavimarśarūpasamyagvicāritatvalakṣaṇasamyakttvayuktādupakramā
diśaktitātprayaliṅgasamudāyātmasamanvayāt sarvaśāstrasya bhagavatyeva samyagvacanavṛttyā śaktitātparyākhyasambandhāvagamāt tadviṣṇvākhyaṃ brahmaiva jagatkāraṇatayā śāstrayoni na rudrādīti asamanvayāt'; ityasyāvṛttyā sūtrayojanā darśitā bhavati ।

māṃ vidhatte abhidhatte māṃ vikalpyo apohyā ityaham ।
ityasyā hṛdayaṃ sākṣānnānyo madveda kaścana ।
iti bhāgavate
।
nanu karmavidhānādirūpaśāstrasya kathaṃ brahmaparatetyāśaṅkāṃ bhagavadvākyena pratiṣedhati māmiti। yadyapi bhāgavate "ityasyā hṛdayaṃ loke"iti pāṭhaḥ, tathā pūrvottarārdhayorvyutkrameṇa pāṭhaśca dṛśyate। tathāpyācāryokteranyakalpīyo ayamityadoṣaḥ । ekādaśaskandhe uddhavaṃ prati kṛṣṇavacanametat । atrāsmacchabdena kṛṣṇa ucyate । tathā ca "vasante vasante" ityādi karmavidhātrī śrutiḥ amām'; uddiśyaiva matpūjātvena karmavidhatte । indrādyabhidhātrī amāmabhidhatte'; madguṇānaiśvaryādīnabhidhatte । aahaṃ vikalpyaḥ'; kalpanaṃ vidhānaṃ tathā ca 
catvāri vākparimitā padāni tāni vidurbrāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ ।
guhā trīṇi nihitā neṅgayanti turīyaṃ vāco manuṣyā vadanti । 
iti śrutyā yā vāgvaktṛttvānnimittādvākbdito hariḥ tasyā yāni sthānāpekṣayā aparimitāni'; paricchinnāni acatvāri padāni'; vāsudevādirūpāṇi tāni ye manīṣiṇaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ta eva viduḥ । tatra vāco hṛdayaguhāyāṃ nihitāni vāsudevāditrīṇi rūpāṇi amanuṣyāḥ'; sādhāraṇāḥ aneṅgayanti'; na jānanti । aturīyam'; aniruddhākhyaṃ tu avadanti'; jānanatītyevaṃrūpeṇa ahameva catuṣṭvasaṅkhyāviśiṣṭavāsudevādivividharūpatayā bahutvena vidheya ityarthaḥ । aahamapohyaḥ'; ana surāṃ pibet'; ityādivākyenāpriyāditi śeṣaḥ। tathā ca "niṣedhabuddhiviṣayamapriyaṃ hi hareḥ smṛtam"iti bhāgavatatātparyokteḥ surāpānādikaṃ madaprītisādhanatvāt niṣidhyate ityapriyadvārā ana surāṃ pibet'; ityādinā ahameva niṣedhya ityarthaḥ । athavā ahamapriyādapohyaḥ mamāprītikarātsurāpānaśabditāt "surā harerguṇā me syuḥ"iti cintanāttapadapekṣya apohyo niṣedhya ityarthaḥ । taduktaṃ bhāgavatatātparye vidhirūpatvena kalpanaṃ vikalpaḥ catvāri vāgityādi । tatra vāgityanuvādaḥ ।
vidhibhāge hareḥ pūjaivābhidhāne ca tadguṇāḥ ।
vikalpe tadbahutvaṃ cāpyapohe tu tadapriyam ।
ucyate sarvavedeṣu tacca veda sa eva hi । tathā 
surā harerguṇāḥ proktāste me syuriti cintanam ।
surāpānamiti proktaṃ tanna kuryātkathañcana ।
tattvapradīpe tu adve vā va brahmaṇo rūpe'; iti vikalpya vividhaṃ kalpayitvā atatra yassa ātmā'; iti sadoṣādapohyo nirdeṣatvena vidheyo apyahamevetyarthaḥ uktaḥ । atra tattvapradīpapakṣe vikalpyeti lyap । ṭīkākṛtpakṣe tu vikalpyaśabdassamāsāntargato vyasto veti viśeṣaḥ । iyaṃ ca bhagavati
vākyasamanvayarītiḥ ādyasya itiśabdasya prakārārthasya hṛdayamityanenānvayaḥ । dvitīyasya evaṃbhūtāyā ityarthaḥ । tathā ca hyevaṃbhūtāyā vidhiniṣedhādirūpāyā anyaparatvena pratītāyāścāsyāśśruteriti amāṃ vidhatte'; ityādyuktaprakāreṇa ahṛdayaṃ'; tātparyam aahameva veda'; jānāmi amadanyaḥ kaścana'; ko api viśeṣataḥ prāyaḥ na veda na jānātītyarthaḥ । bhāgavata ityanantaraṃ tadeva śāstragamyamityuktatvāt na kathamitiśaṅkāvakāśa iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।।
। iti samanvayādhikaraṇam ।

।
nanu yato vāco nivartante । aprāpya manasā saha ।
atrādhikaraṇe saṃśabdoktaṃ vācyatvaṃ kārtsnyaṃ cākṣipya samādhīyate । pūrvapakṣayati nanviti । aityādibhiśśrutibhiḥ'; iti tṛtīyāpañcamyarthe । tathā ca atat'; pūrvasūtre tacchabdoktaṃ brahmaśabdagocaraṃ śāstroktaṃ kāraṇaṃ na, kutaḥ? yato na śabdagocaraṃ śāstramukhyārthaḥ na, tadapi kutaḥ? yato na śabdagocaraṃ śabdāvācyaṃ, nacekṣaṇīyatvavirodhaḥ tadasiddheḥ । kutaḥ? yato na tadgocaraṃ jñānaviṣayaḥ na, ajñeyamiti yāvat । na cāvācyatvājñeyatvayorasiddhiḥ । "yato vāco nivartante"ityādi śruteriti yojanā। ayato vācaḥ'; iti vākye avācyatvasya aaprāpya manasā saha'; ityajñeyatvasya ca uktatvāditi bhāvaḥ । "trayī na śrutigocarā"ityatra gocaraśabdasya viśeṣyaliṅgatayā prayogāt ana tacchabdagocaram'; iti sādhu । sudhāyāṃ tu śabdānāṃ gavāṃ jñānānāṃ caraścaraṇaṃ vṛttiryasmin tacchabdagocaramiti vyadhikaraṇabahuvrīhiṃ caraścaraṇamasyāstīti matvarthīyācpratyayāntatvaṃ cāśritya śabdagocaramityasya sādhutvamuktam । ayataḥ'; iti taittirīyavākyam । yato avāco'; vedā vāgindriyāṇi ca amanasā'; manorūpendriyeṇa saha atamaprāpya'; tadviṣayakavṛttijñānamajānantya eva nivartante । taṃ brahmaṇa ānandaṃ vidvānna bibheti ityarthaḥ । guṇaguṇinorabhedāśrayeṇaitadudāhṛtam ।

aaśabdamasparśamarūpamavyayaṃ tathārasaṃ nityamagandhavacca yat'।
aaśabdam'; iti kāṭhakavākyam । atra sarvatra yacchabdo yojyaḥ । na vidyate śabdo guṇaḥ pramāṇaṃ vā yasmiṃstattathoktam । prākṛtaśabdaguṇaśūnyaṃ śabdapramāṇāviṣayaḥ śabdabhinnaṃ cetyarthaḥ । aasparśaṃ'; sparśaguṇaśūnyaṃ tata eva sparśaliṅgāviṣayaḥ tadbhinnaṃ ca, aarūpaṃ'; rūparahitam ata eva cakṣuṣapratyakṣāviṣayastadbhinnaṃ ca । aarasaṃ'; rasaguṇaśūnyaṃ rasabhinnaṃ ca । agandhamityasyāpyupalakṣakametat ।
anena pañcamātrāvilakṣaṇatvamapyuktam । aavyayaṃ nityam'; ityābhāyāṃ svarūpato dehataśca nāśaśūnyatvamucyate । agandhavadityanena gandhavatpṛthivīlakṣaṇatvamuktam । anenopalakṣaṇayā pañcamahābhūtavilakṣaṇatvamapyuktaṃ bhavati । asya anicāyya taṃ mṛtyumukhātpramucyate'; ityanenānvayaḥ।

aavacanenaiva provāca'; 
aavacanena'; ityanyacchrutivākyam । aavacanena'; vacanavṛttiṃ vinaiva lakṣaṇayā aprovāca brahma guruḥ'; śiṣyāyopadideśeti pararītyārthaḥ ।

ayadvācānabhyuditaṃ yena vāgabhyudyate yacchrotreṇa na śruṇoti yena śrotramidaṃ śrutam'
ityādibhiśśrutibhiḥ na tacchabdagocaram ।
ayadvācā'; ityanyattalavakāravākyam । avācā'; taduccāryeṇa śabdena yat aanabhyuditam'; anuktam । yena vāk aabhyudyate'; ucyate । śrotrendriyeṇa na śṛṇoti puruṣaḥ । yenedaṃ śrotraṃ śrutaṃ tadeva brahma tvaṃ viddhītyarthaḥ । atra pūrvapakṣarītyā vacanavṛttiniṣedhaḥ । ādipadenaivaṃjātīyakā śrutirgṛhyate ।

netyāha 
īkṣater nāśabdam ।
asa etasmājjīvaghanātparātparaṃ puriśayaṃ puruṣamīkṣate'; 
aātmanyevātmānaṃ paśyet'; 
avijñāya prajñāṃ kurvīta'; 
ityādivacanairīkṣaṇīyatvādvācyameva ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati neti । tathā ca atra sūtrakāraḥ iti pūrvapakṣyuktaṃ śrutitātparyāparijñānaprāptaṃ brahmaṇo avācyatvaṃ neti niṣedhatītyarthaḥ । sūtraṃ paṭhati īkṣateriti । atra tadityanuvartate । tacca ādhyāyaparisamāpteḥ vidheyasamarpakamapīhoddeśyasamarpakam । na vidyate śabdo vācako yasya tadaśabdam । tathā ca atat'; brahma aaśabdaṃ'; śabdāvācyaṃ na, kintu vācyameva । kutaḥ? īkṣateḥ । dhātunirdeśo ayaṃ, tathaiva sudhokteḥ । tathāpi śabdamātrasyāsādhakatayā tena tadartho lakṣyate । tena prakṛtānukūlatayekṣaṇīyatvaṃ vivakṣyate । tathā ca aīkṣateḥ'; īkṣaṇīyatvāt jñānaviṣayatvādityarthaḥ ityāśayena sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe sa iti । idaṃ ca ṣaṭpraśnavākyam । atra "yaḥ punaretaṃ trimātreṇaumityanenaivākṣareṇa paraṃ puruṣamabhidhyāyīta sa tejasi sūrye sampanno yathā pādodarastavacā vinirmucyate evaṃ ha vai sa pāpmanā vinirmuktaḥ sa sāmabhirunnīyate brahmalokam"iti pūrvavākye prakṛto yaḥ akārokāramakārākhyāṃśatrayayuktapraṇavoktaprakāreṇa paramātmānamabhidhyāya tamaparokṣīkṛtya ca tejorūpe sūrye sampannatvagvinirmuktasarpavadvidhūtapāpassāmābhimānidevaiḥ satyākhyaṃ brahmalokaṃ prāptaḥ praṇavopāsako jīvaḥ saḥ ajīvaghanāt'; jīvasārāttacchreṣṭhāt aetasmāt'; caturmukhāttadupadeśena aparātparam'; uttamāduttamaṃ apuriśayaṃ'
sakaladehāntargataṃ apuruṣaṃ'; pūrṇaṃ vāsudevaṃ paramātmānaṃ aīkṣate'; jānātītyarthaḥ । yadyapi ṣaṭpraśnaṭīkāyāṃ "jīvaghanādviriñcāttadupāsanayeti yāvat, īkṣate punarabhivṛddhajñāno bhavati । īkṣitvāca taṃ prāpnoti"ityukterīkṣateraparokṣajñānārthatvaṃ pratīyate । tathāpi mūle jñānasāmānyaviṣayatvarūpekṣaṇīyatvahetorasiddhiparihārāya asyāḥ śruterupanyastatvāt "hiraṇyagarbhopadeśena"iti ṭīkokteśceha prakṛtānuguṇyādīkṣatiḥ parokṣajñānārtho vyākhyeyaḥ। aātmani'; ityaparaṃ kāṇvavākyaṃ jijñāsānaye vyākṛtam । avijñāya'; ityanyadvājasaneyavākyam। abrāhmaṇo'; brahmaniṣṭho dhīraḥ ataṃ'; paramātmānamevaṃ śāstreṇācāryādvā avijñāya'; parokṣato jñātvā aprajñāṃ'; prakṛṣṭamapokṣajñānaṃ akurvīta'
sampādayedityarthaḥ । evamādivākyairityarthaḥ । ādiśabdena "ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ" "ajaātmā mahān dhruvaḥ" "tameva dhīro vijñāya" ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । avagamopalakṣakametat । anenāsiddhiḥ parihṛtā । tadanyathānupapatteriti śeṣaḥ । vācyameveti sautranañdvayalabdhārthoktiḥ । na tvavācyaṃ nāpi lakṣyamiti evaśabdārthaḥ । tadityanenāsyānvayaḥ । aniyamasūcanāya sūtrabhāṣyayoḥ pratijñāhetvorvyutkrameṇoktiḥ ।

aupaniṣadatvānnāvacanenekṣaṇam ।
nanvastvīkṣaṇīyatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ, tathāpi na tadanyathānupapattyā tasya vācyatvaṃ vācyaṃ pratyakṣādināpīkṣaṇīyatvopapatterityata āha aupaniṣadatvāditi । tadityetadvipariṇamyānuvartate । tathā ca atasya'; brahmaṇaḥ aaupaniṣadatvāt'; upaniṣadekasamadhigamyatvāt aavacanena'; vacanetarapramāṇena aīkṣaṇaṃ'; jñānaṃ netyarthaḥ । tathā ca śrutismṛtisāhāyyarahitapratyakṣādyavedyatvaviśiṣṭekṣaṇīyatvānyathānupapattyā brahmaṇo vācyatvaṃ siddhyatyeveti bhāvaḥ । pariśeṣapramāṇaparatayā vā idamāvṛttya vyākhyeyam । yojanā tu brahmaṇaśrutiṣūktaṃ īkṣaṇaṃ pramāṇenaiva hi bhavet । prasaktapramāṇeṣu ca anāvacanena'; vacanetarapramāṇenekṣaṇaṃ sambhavati aupaniṣadatvāt vacanenaiva bhavadīkṣaṇaṃ nāvacanena vacanavṛttyanyalakṣaṇādinā sambhavati । kutaḥ? aavacanena'; bhāvapradhāno bahuvrīhiḥ । avacanatvenāvācyatvena nimittena ataḥ pariśeṣādīkṣaṇaṃ vācyatvameva sādhayatīti ।

asarve vedā yatpadamāmanti tapāṃsi sarvāṇi ca yadvadanti'; ।
nanu śrutisiddhamavācyatvaṃ kathamīkṣaṇīyatvayuktimātreṇa dūṣyate? aprābalyamāgamasyaiva'; iti yuktitaḥ śruteḥ prābalyokterityataḥ sautro heturāgamopalakṣaka iti bhāvena vācyatve śrutismṛtī cāha sarva iti । kaṭhānāmiyaṃ śrutiḥ। sarve vedā ayatpadaṃ'; yasya brahmaṇaḥ svarūpam aāmananti'; mukhyavṛttyā satātparyaṃ pratipādayanti । sarve vedāḥ sarvāṇi tapāṃsi prasiddhāni ayat'; brahma prati avadanti'; yaduddeśena kartavyānīti bodhayantītyarthaḥ । tattvapradīparītyā atapāṃsi'; ālocanarūpā yuktaya iti vā । sarvairvedairahameva avedyo'; mukhyataḥ pratipādyaḥ । ahaṃ avedāntakṛt'; brahmasūtrakṛt avedavit'; vedārthajñānī ceti gītāsmṛtyarthaḥ । ādipadāt aatha kasmāducyate'; anāmāni sarvāṇi'; avacasāṃ vācyamuttamam'; ityādessaṅgrahaḥ । tathā ca śrutau aāmananti'; iti sākṣādvācyatvokteḥ, smṛtau ca aahameva'; ityavadhāraṇopapattaye mukhyatayā vedyatvasya vivakṣaṇīyatvāt tasya ca vācyatvaṃ vināyogātsarvaśabdalakṣaṇāyāścāsambhavādvācyatvamevābhyāṃ siddhyatīti bhāvaḥ । smṛtibhyaścetyasya vācyamevetyanenānvayaḥ । ādiśabdopāttaśrutismṛtyapekṣayā bahuvacanam । na kevalamīkṣaṇīyatvahetoriti cārthaḥ ।
vedaiśca sarvairahameva vedyo vedāntakṛdvedavideva cāham ।
ityādiśrutismṛtismṛtibhyaśca ।

avācyatvādikaṃ tvaprasiddhatvāt ।
nanvevaṃ vācyatvasya yuktyādisiddhatve avācyatvājñeyatvābhidhāyakodāhṛtaśruteḥ ayato vācaḥ'; ityādirūpāyāḥ kā gatirityata āha avācyatvādikamiti । ajñeyatvamatarkyatvaṃ ca ādiśabdārthaḥ । tuśabdaḥ śaṅkāvyāvartakaḥ bhinnakrameṇāvadhāraṇe vā । tathā ca aaprasiddhatvāt'; sākalyena agocaratvānnimittādeva brahmaṇi aavācyatvādikam'; avācyatvādivyapadeśo yujyata iti na tadvirodha iti bhāvaḥ । anena siddhānte aaśabdam'; ityāderaprasiddhatvātsākalyena vācakaśabdaśūnyamityādirthaḥ । aavacanena'; ityasya tu sākalyena vacanamantareṇetyartha ityuktaṃ bhavati ।

na tadīdṛgiti jñeyaṃ na vācyaṃ na ca tarkyate ।
paśyanto api na paśyanti mero rūpaṃ vipaścitaḥ ।
itivat ।
nanvaprasiddhinimittako avācyatvādivyapadeśaḥ kva dṛṣṭa ityata āha na taditi । yasmāt avipaścito'; jñānino mero rūpaṃ paśyanto api aīdṛgiti'; sākalyena ana paśyanti'; na jānanti । anenāprasiddhatvahetuḥ sūcitaḥ । tasmānmero rūpaṃ na jñeyaṃ pratyakṣeṇa । na vācyaṃ śabdena । ana tarkyate'; nānumīyate ca liṅgenetyucyata ityarthaḥ । itivaditi । iti vākya ivetyarthaḥ । asyāvācyatvādikamiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । tathā ca yathā merurūpe aprasiddhinimittakāvācyatvādivyapadeśastathā brahmaṇyapīti bhāvaḥ ।

aprasiddheravācyaṃ tadvācyaṃ sarvāgamoktitaḥ ।
atarkyaṃ tarkyamajñeyaṃ jñeyamevaṃ paraṃ smṛtam ।
iti gāruḍe ।
na kevalaṃ apaśyantaḥ'; ityuktyanyathānupapattimātreṇaiva aprasiddherajñeyatvātarkyatvāvācyatvavyapadeśa iti vyavasthā siddhā, api tu smṛtisiddhā ceti bhāvenāha aprasiddheriti । tadbrahma yataḥ aparaṃ'; pūrṇam atassākalyenāprasiddhatvādavācyamucyate । sarvasadāgamoktatvāttatprasiddhatvādvācyaṃ ca bhavatītyarthaḥ । evamaprasiddhiprasiddhibhyāṃ tat atarkyam anumeyaṃ ca ajñeyaṃ jñeyaṃ jñānipratyakṣagamyaṃ ca asmṛtaṃ'; smṛtikārairuktamityarthaḥ । gāruḍe ityanantaraṃ uktamiti śeṣaḥ । asyāpyavācyatvādikamityanenānvayaḥ ।

na cāśabdatvamitarasiddham ।
evaṃ ayato vācaḥ'; ityādiśrutīnāṃ yuktyādibalādarthāntaropapatterna tadbalācchabdāvācyaṃ brahmeti sūtraṃ vyākhyāyāpavyākhyāṃ pratyākhyāti na ceti । caśabdaḥ svasiddhamapi netisamuccaye । tathā ca jagatkāraṇaṃ aaśabdaṃ'; pradhānaṃ na, kutaḥ? aśabdaṃ hi tat । aaśabdaṃ'; pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ neti vā, kutaḥ? aīkṣateḥ'; atadaikṣata'; iti jagatkāraṇasyekṣaṇakartṛtvaśravaṇātpradhānasya cācetanatvena tadasambhavāditi sāṅkhyamatanirākaraṇaparatayā vyākhyāne prathamapratijñāyāṃ hetūkṛtam aaśabdatvam'; aśrautatvam
aitarasiddhaṃ'; svetarasāṅkhyasiddhaṃ na, na kevalametāvat, kintu svasiddhamapi na, sāṅkhyena vaidikatvābhyupagateḥ । sūtrakāreṇa aajāmekām'; ityādi śrutyuktatvāṅgīkārāt ।
yadvā tattvapradīparītyā māyinā sāṅkhyaṃ prati hetutvenopanyastamaśabdatvaṃ māyītarasya sāṅkhyasya na siddhaṃ nāpi sāṅkhyetaramāyisiddhamuktahetubhyāmeva । tathā cāsiddhiriti na tadvyākhyānaṃ yuktamitibhāvaḥ । evamaśabdatvaṃ śrautatvaṃ brahmaṇassāṅkhyetaramāyisiddhaṃ na, tanmate avācyatvāt । cakārādīkṣitṛtvamapi siddhaṃ na, tasyekṣatisvarūpatvādityapi vyākhyeyam । tathā ca hetudvayamapi svapakṣapratikūlamiti na paravyākhyā yukteti bhāvaḥ tattvapradīpe tu anaca'; ityādibhāṣyaṃ aitarasiddhaṃ'; māyisiddhamaśabdatvaṃ na śrutyarthaḥ uktanyāyena brahmaṇo vācyatvāt । evam aaśabdatvam'; avācyatvaṃ brahmaṇa itarasya māyino api na siddham । brahmaṇi vyavahārābhāvaprasaṅgāt iti dvedhā vyākhyāyaparakṛtavyākhyāpratyākhyānāya paroktahetoṣṭīkārītyāsiddhyuktiparatayāpi vyākhyātam ।

gauṇaścennātmaśabdāt ।
īkṣaṇīyatvasya hetorvyadhikaraṇāsiddhimākṣipya samādhātuṃ sūtram aoṃ gauṇaścennātmaśabdāt'; iti । asyārthaḥ ayataḥ ātmanyevātmānaṃ paśyet'; ityādiśrutyukta ātmā agauṇaḥ'; sattvādiguṇabaddho jīva evātastadanyathānupapattyā vācyo api sa eva syānna nirguṇaḥ paramātmeti cet na, kutaḥ? aātmānaṃ paśyet'; itīkṣaṇīye tasminnātmaśabdaśravaṇāditi । aātmapatasāmānādhikaraṇyāya pulliṅganirdeśaḥ'; ।

na ca gauṇa ātmā dṛśyo vācyaśca na nirguṇa iti yuktam ।
ātmaśabdāt ।
sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe na ceti । atra yato adṛśyaḥ'; īkṣatiśrutau dṛśyatayoktaḥ aātmā'; jīvākhyo gauṇa eva atastadanyathānupapattyā vācyo api sa eva syāt ana nirguṇaḥ'; guṇātīto viṣṇuḥ adṛśyaḥ'; īkṣatiśruttyuktaḥ । gauṇagrahaṇe bādhakasyetarajñāpakasya cābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ । ato na sa vācyaḥ iti codyaṃ na yuktam । kutaḥ? aātmaśabdāt'; aātmanyeva'; iti vākye īkṣaṇīye tasmin ātmaśabdaśravaṇāddṛśyo nirguṇa eva, ata evekṣatyā liṅgena vācyo api sa eva bhavediti yojanā । yadyapi sudhāyāṃ gauṇapadaṃ māyāśabalitaiśvaryādidharmayuktasaguṇabrahmaparatayā vyākhyātaṃ tathāpi pūrvapakṣiṇo māyāśabalitaṃ vā guṇabaddhā jīvā vā dṛśyā vācyāśca, na sarvathā nirguṇaṃ brahmetyāśayānna virodhaḥ ।

yo guṇaissarvato hīno yaśca doṣavivarjitaḥ ।
heyopādeyarahitaḥ sa ātmetyabhidhīyate ।
etadanyasvabhāvo yaḥ so anātmeti satāṃ matam ।
anātmanyātmaśabdastu sopacāraḥ prayujyate ।
iti vāmane ।
nanvātmaśabdasadbhāve kuto ayaṃ nirguṇo na gauṇa ityata āha ya iti । yaḥ asarvataḥ'; prakāreṇa aguṇaiḥ'; sattvādibhiḥ śūnyaḥ yaśca dukhakhādidoṣarahitaḥ yaśca heyopādeyarahitaḥ । bhāvapradhāno ayam । heyatvasahitopādeyatvarahita iti । upādeya evetyarthaḥ । tattvapradīparītyā svābhāvikadoṣarahito guṇapūrṇatvenāptakāmatvādupādeyarahita iti vā । tattvodyotaṭīkārītyā doṣābhāvāddhāturabhāvādvā heyatvarahitaḥ, laukikaguṇābhāvādupādāturanyasya svatantrasyābhāvādvā upādeyatvarahitaḥ aniṣṭābhāvāddheyaṃ nāsti, apūrtyabhāvādupādeyamasya nāstīti vā tathoktaḥ । ya evaṃ bhūtassa ātmetyabhidhīyate । ya etadviruddhasvabhāvavān so anātmeti satāṃ mataṃ sammatamitythaḥ । kvacit ahṛdi hyeṣa ātmā'
ityādāvetadanyasvabhāve apyātmapadaprayogāt
kathaṃ so anātmetyata āha anātmanīti । aanātmani'; ātmaśabdamukhyārthabhinne jīve aātmaśabdaḥ'; asopacāraḥ'; upacāraḥ paramamukhyavṛttyanyamukhyavṛttiḥ tatsahitastadvṛttika ityarthaḥ। tuśabdo viśeṣārthaḥ । avāmane'; ityanantaraṃ anirguṇaikaniṣṭhatvenoktāt'; iti śeṣaḥ । asya nāyaṃ dṛśyo
vācyaśca gauṇaḥ, kintu nirguṇa evetyanenānvayaḥ ।

adve vāva brahmaṇo rūpe ātmā caivānātmā ca ।
tatra yaḥ sa ātmā sa nityaḥ śuddhaḥ kevalo nirguṇaśca ।
atha ha yo anīdṛśaḥ so anātmā'; iti talavakārabrāhmaṇam ।
atraiva pramāṇāntaramāha dve vāveti । abrahmaṇaḥ'; parabrahmaṇaḥ rūpaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca rūpe । tatrādyo rūpaśabdaḥ svarūpaparaḥ dvitīyo rūpyate jñāyate brahmākhyamiti vyutpattyā pratimāparaḥ । vāveti nipātasamudāyaḥ prasiddhidyotakaḥ । te rūpe darśayati ātmeti । ātmaśabdamukhyavācyastadavācyaścetyarthaḥ । atatra'; ātmanātnormadhye asa yaḥ'; ityanvayaḥ । anyathā paunaruktyāt । tathā ca asaḥ'; prasiddho ayaḥ'; ātmā ātmaśabdamukhyārtho viṣṇuḥ asaḥ nityaḥ'; dehahānyādirahitaḥ aśuddhaḥ'; karmalepavidhuraḥ akevalaḥ'; jaḍāmiśraḥ anirguṇaḥ'; sattvādiguṇābaddha ityarthaḥ । co viśeṣaṇasamuccaye । evaṃ prathamoddiṣṭātmaśabdārthaṃ lakṣaṇamukhena pradarśya athānātmānamuktalakṣaṇavyatirekamukhena darśayati atheti । yasmādātmā evaṃ bhūtaḥ aatha'; tasmāt ayo anīdṛśaḥ'; nityatvādirahitaḥ ha prasiddhaḥ । aso anātmeti'; satāṃ sammatamityarthaḥ । abrāhmaṇam'; ityanantaraṃ yato nirguṇasya viṣṇorevātmatvaṃ vaktīti śeṣaḥ । asyāpi avāmane'; itivadanvayaḥ ।

na ca mukhye satyamukhyaṃ yujyate ।
nanūpacāreṇāpyātmaśabdasya gauṇe prayogasadbhāvātsa eva śrutyukto dṛśya ātmā kiṃ na syādityata āha na ceti । amukhye'; ātmapadamukhyārthe nirguṇe dṛśyatayekṣatiśrutipratipādye sambhavati sati amukhyārthagauṇagrahaṇaṃ na yujyata ityarthaḥ । atra satītyanena mukhyasambhavākhyo heturuktaḥ । amukhyaṃ na yujyata ityanena sādhyam । ubhayasamuccaye śaṅkāparihārasamuccaye vā caśabdaḥ ।

tanniṣṭhasya mokṣopadeśāt ।
nanu ātmaśabdo mukhyata eva gauṇātmaparaḥ kiṃ na syāt । na coktaśrutismṛtivirodhaḥ, tatrātmaśabdo nirguṇe viṣṇau mukhyo jīveṣvamukhya ityanukteḥ ātmanātmaśabdayoścetanācetanaviṣayatvasambhavāt । kiñca ātmānātmaśabdayoḥ prasiddhacetanācetanaparatveśruterārjavaṃ, prasiddhārthāparityāgāt, rūpaśabdasyānekārthākalpanācca । na ca jīve nirdeṣatvādyayogaḥ, duḥkhādidoṣasyaupādhikatvena jīvasyāpi svabhāvato nirdeṣatayā śruteḥ svabhāvaviṣayatvopapatterityāśaṅkāṃ parihartuṃ sūtraṃ paṭhati oṃ tanniṣṭhasya iti।। tathā ca atanniṣṭhasya'; asya ātmajñāninaḥ amokṣopadeśāt'; nātmaśabdamukhyavācyo gauṇa iti sūtrārthaḥ ।

na hi gauṇātmaniṣṭhasya mokṣaḥ ।
tanniṣṭhasya mokṣopadeśe api kuto ayamātmā na gauṇa ityaprayojakatvamāśaṅkhyāha na hīti ।
gauṇamokṣapadasamabhivyāhṛto hiśabdo virodhākhyahetusūcakaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt agauṇātmaniṣṭhasya'; guṇabaddhajīvajñāninaḥ tajjñānādguṇabandhanivṛttirūpo amokṣo'; na sambhavati, virodhāt tasmāt ana hi'; nāprayojakatā śaṅkyetyarthaḥ ।

yasyānuvittaḥ pratibuddha ātmā asmin sandohe gahane praviṣṭaḥ ।
sa viśvakṛtsa hi sarvasya kartā tasya lokaḥ sa u loka eva
ityātmaniṣṭhasya mokṣa upadiśyate ।
asiddhiśaṅkāṃ parihartuṃ ko asāvātmaniṣṭhasya mokṣopadeśa ityatastaṃ darśayati yasyeti । atra śrutiḥ svaprayuktamuśabdam eveti vyācaṣṭe । au'; ekaḥ pradhāna iti vā । tacchabdo viṣṇutajjñāniparaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ asarvasya kartā'; tasmādeva aviśvakṛt'; vāyukartā apratibuddhaḥ'; svatassarvajñaḥ aasmin sandohe'; sanduhyate puruṣārtho aneneti vā kāryakāraṇasaṅkhātarūpatvādvā bhūtasamudāyarūpatvādvā sandohanāmake madhyadehe sthite agahane'; gambhīre hṛdayaguhāsthāne apraviṣṭaḥ'; saḥ aātmā'; viṣṇuḥ ayasya'; yenopāsakena aanuvittaḥ'; samayagjñātaḥ atasya'; adhikāriṇaḥ au'; pradhānaḥ tasya viṣṇoryo alokaḥ'; sa eva lokaḥ sthānaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ । asandoghe'; iti pāṭhe apyayayamevārthaḥ asandehe'; iti pāṭhe anekārthasaṅkaṭa ityarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu sa viśvakṛt kṛtakṛtyaḥ । kutaḥ? yataḥ sa hi paramātmā prasannaḥ sarvaśaktiḥ sarvamasya jñāninaḥ kāryaṃ karotītyuktam । asmin pakṣe prathamaḥ prathamāntatacchabdo viṣṇujñāniparaḥ, viśvaśabdaḥ kṛtyaparaḥ, sarvaśabdo jñānikāryaparaḥ । ṭīkākṛtpakṣe tu prathamaḥ prakṛtaviṣṇuparaḥ, viśvaśabdo vāyuparaḥ, sarvaśabdo jagatpara iti bhedaḥ । pakṣadvaye api dvitīyatṛtīyau viṣṇutallokapara। aiti'; ityevaṃrūpe bṛhadāraṇyake aātmaniṣṭhasya'; tajjñānino amokṣa upadiśyate'; । asya yata ityupadiśyate ato ana gauṇa ātmā'; iti vakṣyamāṇapratijñayānvayaḥ । sūtrasya tu na gauṇa ātmaśabda iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । ātmetyanena sautratacchabdo nātmaśabdaparaḥ, kintvarthataḥ pradhānātmapara ityuktaṃ bhavati ।

ayamātmā brahma 
ātmaśabdo viṣṇāveva mukhyaḥ na jīveṣvityatra na kevalaṃ tanniṣṭhasyetyādinoktamanumānaṃ mānam, kintu sūtrakṛdabhipretāḥ spaṣṭaśrutismṛtayaśceti bhāvena tāṃ tāścāha ayamiti । brahmetyantasya upadiśyata iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । aayamātmā'; ramābrahmādiṣu ādānādikartṛtvena sthitaḥ ātmā abrahma'; viṣṇureveti māṇḍūkaśrutyarthaḥ
"so ayaṃ viṣṇū ramābrahmarudrānantādigaḥ sadā । ādānādanakartṛtvādātmā"iti māṇḍūkabhāṣyoktaḥ ।

brahmeti paramātmeti bhagavāniti śabdyate ।
dattaṃ durvāsasaṃ somamātmeśabrahmasambhavān ।
cetanastu dvidhā prokto jīva ātmeti ca prabho ।
jīvā brahmādayaḥ proktā ātmaikastu janārdanaḥ ।
itareṣvātmaśabdastu sopacāraḥ prayujyate ।
tasyātmano nirguṇasya jñānānmokṣa udāhṛtaḥ ।
saguṇāstvapare proktāstajjñānānnaiva mucyate ।
paro hi puruṣo viṣṇustasmānmokṣastatassmṛtaḥ ।
iti pādme ।
"vadanti tattattvavidastattvaṃ yajjñānamadvayam । brahma"ityaparaṃ bhāgavatavākyam । advayaṃ samādhikaśūnyaṃ jñānasvarūpaṃ yattattvaṃ vadanti jñāninaḥ tat deśakālādiṣu bṛṃhitatvāt sarvāntaryāmitvādyaiśvaryādiguṇavāttvācca nimittāt abrahmeti paramātmeti bhagavāniti śabdyate'; abhidhīyata ityarthaḥ । asyāpi pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ । tatraiva caturthaskandhe "dattam"ityanyadvākyam । etacca aanasūyā tathaivātrerjajñe putrānakalmaṣān'; iti pūrvārdhenaivānvetavyam ।
patnī marīcessukalā suṣuve kardamātmajā ।
kāśyapaṃ pūrṇimānaṃ ca yayorāpūritaṃ jagat ।
iti prakṛtena samuccayārthastathāśabdaḥ । tathā ca anasūyākhyā atribhāryā atreḥ sakāśāt aātmeśabrahmasambhavān'; ātmā viṣṇurīśorudraḥ brahmā caturmukhaḥ ātmā ceśaśca brahmā ca te tathoktāḥ taissaha bhavantītyātmeśabrahmasambhavāḥ tān aakalmaṣān'; apāpān yo dattaḥ durvāsāḥ somaścaitān putrān ajajñe'; janayāmāsetyarthaḥ । yadvā anasūyā atrerdattādīn janayāmāsa, te ca ātmeśabrahmasambhavā iti vipariṇāmena vyākhyeyam । atra brahmāveśena sahotpanne candre niruktasambhavaśabdo mukhyaḥ । sākṣādviṣṇurudrāṃśatvena tatsambhūtayordattadurvāsasostu chatrinyāyenāmukhya iti draṣṭavyam । yadyapi "atreḥ patnyanasūyā trīn jajñe atiyaśasaḥ sutān । dattam"iti bhāgavatapāṭhaḥ, tathāpyanuvyākhyāne evaṃ paṭhitatvāttathaiva sudhāyāṃ vyākhyātatvāttadanyakalpīyaṃ pāṭhāntaraṃ bhaviṣyatītyadoṣaḥ । asyāpītyupadiśyata ityanenānvayaḥ । cetanastviti pāvākyam । aprabho'; iti kasyacitsambodhanam । tatreti śeṣaḥ । ādyastuśabdo viśeṣārthaḥ । dvitīyo avadhāraṇe । tathā ca ajīvāḥ brahmādayaḥ proktāḥ ātmā tu'; tacchabdamukhyavācyastu ajanārdano'; viṣṇuḥ aekaḥ'; eva proktaḥ pramāṇeṣu । aitareṣu'; brahmādiṣu aātmaśabdaḥ sopācāraḥ'; paramamukhyavṛttyapekṣayā hīnavṛttiyukta iti jñānibhirabhidhīyata ityartaḥ । kutastasyaivātmatvaṃ nānyeṣāmityata āha tasyeti । yataḥ atasya'; nirguṇasya ātmano ajñānānmokṣo'; bhavatīti "yasyānuvittaḥ" ityādau audāhṛtaḥ'; uktaḥ ato ayamātmā nirguṇo viṣṇureva nānyaḥ । kutaḥ? tasyaiva viṣṇornirguṇasya mokṣadātṛtvasambhavāt, anyeṣāṃ tadasambhavādityarthaḥ । ātmajñānānmokṣopadeśe api kuto netareṣāmātmatvaṃ teṣāmapi mokṣadātṛtvasambhavādityata āha saguṇā iti । tathāca aapare'; viṣṇoranye brahmādayo yataḥ asaguṇāḥ'; sattvādiguṇabaddhā eva na svatastadvidhurāḥ ataḥ atajjñānānnaiva'; sarvathā amucyate'; adhikārītyarthaḥ, guṇabaddhātmavijñānāt guṇabandhanivṛttirūpamokṣāyāgāditi bhāvaḥ । nanu viṣṇāvapi nirguṇatvenāstu mokṣadātṛtvasambhāvanā, tanniścayastu kuta ityata āha paro hīti । ahi'; yasmāt aviṣṇuparaḥ'; svatantraḥ । tattvapradīparītyā sarvottama iti vā, apuruṣaḥ'; pūrṇaḥ atasmānmokṣastato'; viṣṇorbhavedeveti smṛtaḥ smṛtyukta ityarthaḥ। aiti pādme'; ityasyāpi ityupadiśyata iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ।

heyatvāvacanāc ca ।
atamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānamanyā vāco vimuñcatha ।
amṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ'; 
ityanyeṣāṃ heyatvavaca
nādasyāheyatvavacanānna gauṇa ātmā ।
yuktyantareṇātmaśabdādito na gauṇa ityāha sūtrakṛt heyatveti । atra heyatvaṃ nāma mokṣārthaṃ prādhānyena jñeyatvenāvihitatvam । tathā ca na kevalaṃ tanniṣṭhasya mokṣopadeśāt, kintu "tamevaikam"iti śrutau ātmano heyatvāvacanāt, pratyuta ajānatha'; ityaheyatvavacanāt, jīvasya ca "anyā vāco vimuñcatha"iti mumukṣubhirheyatvavacanācceti sūtravṛttimabhipretya sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe tamiti । he ṛṣayaḥ atam'; ātmānaṃ viṣṇum aeva ekaṃ'; pradhānaṃ ajānatha'; jānīdhvam । aanyāḥ'; jīvādiviṣayiṇīḥ avācaḥ vimuñcatha'; tyajata, prādhānyena viṣṇvitarān na jānīdhvamityarthaḥ । ajānatha ātmānam'; iti viśleṣo viṣṇoḥ sarvato vilakṣaṇatvapradarśanārthaḥ । vikaraṇavyatyayastu chāndasaḥ । amṛtasyetyekavacanaṃ samudāyavivakṣayā । tathā ca aamṛtasya'; muktavargasya aeṣaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ setuḥ'; mukhyāśraya ityarthaḥ । aiti'; ityevaṃrūpāyāṃ muṇḍakaśrutau aanyeṣāṃ'; jīvānāṃ aheyatvavacanāt'; ityanena caśabdasamucceyaṃ darśitam । sautranaño vyatyāsena anvayamabhipretya samucceyāntaramāha asya viṣṇoraheyatveti । caśabdaḥ samuccaye । sūtre gauṇasūtrādanuvṛttasya "na gauṇa ātmaśabdaḥ"ityasyārthamāha neti । gauṇa ātmaśabdamukhyavācyo na, kintu nirguṇo viṣṇurevetyarthaḥ। tathā ca ātmaśabdādīkṣatiśrutyukto api nirguṇa eveti siddham। tasyekṣatyanyathānupapattyā vācyatvamiti bhāvaḥ ।।

svāpyayāt ।
pūrṇamadaḥ pūrṇamidaṃ pūrṇātpūrṇamudacyate ।
pūrṇasya pūrṇamādāya pūrṇamevāvaśiṣyate ।
"sa ātmana ātmānamuddhṛtyātmanyeva vilāpayatyathātmaiva bhavati"।
sa devī bahudhā bhūtvā nirguṇaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।
ekībhūya punaśśete nirdeṣo harirādikṛt ।
yuktyantareṇāpi nirguṇasya viṣṇorvācyatvamupapādayatsūtramupanyasyati svāpyayāditi । sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe pūrṇamiti । aado'; mūlarūpaṃ apūrṇam'; aidam'; avatārarūpaṃ ca apūrṇam'; । apūrṇam'; avatārarūpaṃ sṛṣṭikāle apūrṇāt'; mūlarūpāt audacyate'; udgacchati । tattvapradīparītyā amuṣmādidaṃ saṅkhyāmātreṇodacyate ekameva bahusaṅkhyaṃ bhavati viśeṣādeveti vā । pralaye mūlarūpaṃ apūrṇasya'; svasya apūrṇam'; avatārarūpam aādāya'; svīkṛtyaikībhūya apūrṇameva'; anyatrālīnaṃ sadeva svayam aavaśiṣyate'; iti bṛhadāraṇyakaśrutyarthaḥ । asa'; ityanyāśrutiḥ । tadarthastu asa'; viṣṇuḥ aātmanaḥ'; svasmāt mūlarūpāt aātmānam'; avatāragataṃ svasvarūpaṃ auddhṛtya'; sṛṣṭikāle pṛthagvyaktīkṛtya pralaye aātmani'; svasvinneva avilāpayati'; ekībhāvayati । aatha'; anantaraṃ sa viṣṇuḥ aātmaiva'; mūlarūpyeva abhavati'; avaśiṣyata iti । asa devaḥ'; iti skāndasmṛtiḥ śrautatacchabdārthavivaraṇarūpā । adevo'; dyotanādeḥ anirguṇaḥ'; sattvādiguṇebhyo niṣkrāntaḥ tata eva guṇakāryadoṣahīnaḥ apuruṣottamaḥ'; kṣarākṣaracetanottamaḥ aādikṛt'; viśvasyotpattikartā prathamakartā vā asaḥ'; śvetadvīpago ahariḥ'; ādisṛṣṭau abahudhābhūtvā'; varāhādibahurūpāṇi sṛṣṭvā apunaḥ'; atha pralaye aekībhūya'; mūlarūpeṇa tānyekatāṃ prāpayitvā ahipatau aśete'; yoganidrāṃ karotītyarthaḥ । itītyasya iti śrutyuktatvāccetyadhyāhāreṇa avācyameva tat'; iti paramasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

svasyaiva svasminnapyayavacanāt ।
na hi gauṇātmani nirdeṣasya layaḥ ।
etacchrutyukto api nirguṇaḥ kutaḥ? gauṇa eva kiṃ na syādityastatra sautraṃ hetuṃ sāvadhāraṇasvaśabdāvṛttyā yojayati svasyaiveti । evakāro bhinnakramaḥ । itiśabda āvṛtto atrāpi yojyaḥ। vacanādityāvartate । na gauṇa ityanuvartate । svāpyayapadaṃ pūrṇatvasyāpyupalakṣakam । tathā ca pūrṇamiti śrutau svāpyayapadopalakṣitapūrṇatvasya vacanāt svasya svasminnevāpyayavacanācca, sa iti spaṣṭaśrutāvapi ātmanyeva vilāpayīti svasya svasminnevāpyayavacanāt, tasya ca nirguṇahariniṣṭhatāyāḥ smṛtau vacanācca ayaṃ nirguṇa eva na gauṇa iti yojanā । vācyatve svāpyayasya sākṣāddhetutvābhāvāt sūtre bhāṣye ca caśabdābhāvaḥ । yadyapyatropalakṣaṇābhiprāyakaṭīkārītyā pūrṇatvahetusamuccāyakaścaśabdo anuvartanīyaḥ । tathāpyasya vācyatve sākṣadahetutvāttatra hetvantarasya jñāpakacaśabdo nānuvartanīyaḥ । na ca
śrutyuktatvāccetyadhyāhṛtahetau caśabdāvaśyaṃbhāvāt kathaṃ tadabhāva iti vācyam, sūtraśrutahetau caśabdābhāva ityabhiprāyāt । ata eva ṭīkāyāṃ tatretyuktam । tathā cāyaṃ sūtrārthaḥ na kevalaṃ nirguṇaviṣṇvākhyaṃ brahma īkṣaṇīyatvādvācyam, kintvetacchrutyuktatvācca । śrutyuktaṃ nirguṇameva na gauṇamiti kutaḥ? purṇatvātsvasya svasminnapyayācca, gauṇasyāpūrṇatvāt anyasmin layena svāpyayaśūnyatvācceti । śrutyuktasvāpyayapūrṇatvayorasiddhiparihārāya hetau sādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyopapādanāya ca śrutismṛtyorvacanādityuktaṃ bhāṣye । nanvayaṃ svāpyayavān anyatrālīnaśca gauṇassyāt, nirguṇo anyo astīti cet na, yadyayaṃ svāpyayavān gauṇaḥ tarhyayaṃ nirguṇaścobhau pralaye anyatra layahīnau tiṣṭhataḥ? uta ekasminnanyasya layo bhavati? nādyaḥ "idaṃ vā agne naiva kiñca nāsīt" ityādiśrutivirodhāt, atra pralaye dvitīyamātraniṣedhāt । dvitīye na tāvadgauṇasya nirguṇe layaḥ, tasya svāpyayavattayā avasthānābhyupagamāt । tathā ca nirguṇasya saguṇe layo vācyaḥ । sa ca na sambhavatītyāha na hīti । agauṇātmani'; jīve anirdeṣasya'; sattvādiguṇabandharūpadoṣahīnasya nirguṇasya viṣṇorlayo nopapadyata ityarthaḥ । hiśabdena "yatprayanti" ityādiśrutivirodhāditi hetuḥ sūcitaḥ । tasmānnirguṇasya svasminneva layo vācya ityato ayamananyalīno nirguṇa eveti tasyaiva śrutyuktatvādvācyatvaṃ siddhamiti bhāvaḥ । atra naye gauṇādivyapadeśaḥ sattvādiguṇayuktatvatadabhāvarūpadharmāśrayajīvaparamātmaviṣayaka eva, na tu mukhyāsambhave gauṇāśrayaṇādityatreva nirguṇo ayamityatreva vā mukhyārthaguṇahīnaviṣaya iti sūcanāya nirguṇasyeti vaktavyatve api nirdeṣasyetyuktam ।

na ca kāsucicchākhāsvanyathocyate ।
gatisāmānyāt ।
sarve vedā yuktayaḥ supramāṇā brāhmaṃ jñānaṃ paramaṃ tvekameva ।
prakāśayante na virodhaḥ kutaścidvedeṣu sarveṣu tathetihāse ।
iti paiṅgiśrutergaterjñānasya sāmyameva ।
nanvastu nirguṇasya viṣṇorvācyatvopapattau satyāṃ kāraṇatvena śāstragamyatvam । taccopakramādibalāt prasiddhaśākhāsveva kāraṇatvena pratipādyatvaparyavasitam । aprasiddhaśākhāsu punaranyo api kāraṇatvena ucyatām । na ca tā na santi, tāsāmānantyeneyattāniścayādityata āha na ceti ।। tathā ca akāsucit'; aprasiddhaśākhāsu aanyathā'; anyo nirguṇāt saguṇo api aanyathā'; akāraṇatvādeḥ kāraṇatvena ātmaśabdamukhyavācyatvena mokṣajanakajñānaviṣayatvena ca, nirguṇo vā aanyathā'; akāraṇatvādinā aucyate'; ucyatāmiti ana'
iti yojanā । anānyathā'; ityanena sūtre gauṇasūtrānnetyasyānuvṛttiḥ anyathetyadhyāhāraśca sūcitaḥ । atattu sam'; ityuktādanyathā netyarthaḥ । kuto netyatastatra hetutvena sūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe gatīti । uttarasūtrapadākarṣaṇena sarvādhikārisādhāraṇaṃ gatisāmānyasya śrutatvāditi yojanāmabhipretya asiddhiparihārāya tatsūtrasūcitāṃ śrutimāha sarva iti । vedā ityasya vivaraṇaṃ asarve'; iti । tathā ca asarve vedāḥ'; tathā asupramāṇāḥ'; suṣṭhu pramāṇaṃ pramāṇānantaraṃ mūlabhūtaṃ yāsāṃ tāḥ ayuktayaḥ'; । atathetihāse'; iti vakṣyamāṇānurodhādatretihāsā apyupalakṣyāḥ । tathā cetihāsāśca । abrāhmaṃ'; brahmaikaviṣayam aekam'; ekavidhameva ramārthaviṣayakatvāt aparamam'; uttamaṃ ajñānaṃ'; aprakāśyante'; utpādayanti, na punaranekam । ataḥ asarveṣu vedeṣu'; tathā yuktiṣu atathetihāse'; itihāseṣu akutaścit'; kaścidapi viṣayakṛto vā prakārakṛto vā avirodho na'; ityarthaḥ jñānarūpamekameva brahmasvarūpaṃ
jñāpayantīti vā । śruteriti pañcamī tṛtīyārthe । gaterityasya vyākhyā jñānasyeti । sāmānyāditi sautrapade prātipadikārthamāha sāmyamiti । viṣayaguṇānāmananyathoktyā sāmyamityarthaḥ । "na hyekatra jñānānandādikamuktvānyatrājñānādirūpatvaṃ brahmaṇa ucyate"iti tattvapradīpokteḥ kathyata iti śeṣaḥ । na tu viṣamatvamiti vā svayameva sākṣānna tvanyamukheneti vā evaśabdārthaḥ । tathā ca asarve vedā'; iti śrutyā svayameva sākṣādgateḥ sarvaśākhotpādyajñānasya sāmānyāt ekavidhatvokteḥ na kāsucicchākhāsu anyathocyata iti sūtrārthaḥ । atra bhinnaviṣayaprakārakeṣvapi jñāneṣu jñānatvena sāmyasattvātsāmyādityuktau viṣayaprakāraikyaṃ na siddhyatīti sāmānyāt samānatvāt ekavidhatvāt ityuktaṃ sūtre । bhāṣyapadasyāpyayamevārtha eti dhyeyam ।।

śrutatvāc ca ।
"eko devassarvabhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarvavyāpī sarvabhūtāntarātmā ।
karmādhyakṣassarvabhūtādhivāsaḥ sākṣī cetā kevalo nirguṇaśca"।
iti na śabdaḥ śrūyate । na cāprasiddhaṃ kalpyam ।
sarvaśabdāvācyasya lakṣaṇāyukteḥ ।
itaśca nirguṇaṃ brahma vācyamityāha sūtrakṛt śrutatvācceti। tadaśabdaṃ neti vartate। tathā ca tadviṣṇvākhyaṃ nirguṇaṃ na kevalamīkṣatyādibhiḥ nāśabdaṃ śabdavācyam । kintu "ekaḥ"iti śvetāśvataraśrutau aśrutatvācca'; svavācakanāmnā sākṣāduktatvāccetyartha ityāśayena sūtropāttaśrutiṃ paṭhati eka iti । aekaḥ'; pradhānaḥ svasmin bhedaśūnya iti vā adevo'; dyotanādeḥ asarvabhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ'; sarvaprāṇiṣu guptatayāvasthitaḥ । na kevalaṃ bhūteṣu sthitaḥ kintu asarvavyāpī'; ca deśataḥ kālato guṇataśca sarvaṃ vyāpnotītyarthaḥ । na kevalaṃ sarvabhūteṣu sthitimātraṃ, kintu asarvabhūtāntarātmā'; sarvaprāṇināṃ antaḥsthitvā ā samyak tanniyantā ca mātā ceti vā । ādānādikartṛtvādvā tathoktaḥ । akarmādhyakṣaḥ'; karmādhipatiḥ, "karmopari asyākṣāṇīndriyāṇi vartanta ityadhyakṣaḥ"iti tattvapradīpokteḥ । asarvabhūtādhivāsaḥ'; sarvaprāṇināmāśrayaḥ । sarvaṃ sākṣādīkṣate paśyatīti asākṣī'; । īkṣaṇaṃ ca na prākṛtaṃ kintu caitanyasvarūpamityāha acetā'; jñānarūpa iti । akevalo'; jaḍāmiśraḥ samābhyadhikaśūnya iti vā "kevalaṃ tādṛśābhāvāt"iti dvitīyatātparyokteḥ । kevalaṃ caitanyenekṣaṇamasaṃprajñātasamādhisthasya yogino api bhavatīti tadvyāvartanāyāha anirguṇa'; iti sattvādiguṇabandhahīna ityarthaḥ, prākṛtaguṇahīna iti vā । itiśabdasya aśrutau nirguṇasya'; iti padadvayādhyāhāreṇa śrutatvāditi sūtreṇānvayaḥ । "atra vācyatvaṃ pratipādayatsūtraṃ tadupāttaśrutyudāharaṇapūrvakaṃ paṭhati eka iti"iti kvacitkaṭīkāpāṭhānusāreṇa bhāṣye kvacit śrutipāṭhānantaraṃ sūtrapāṭho dṛśyate । tatpakṣe tvanvayassulabha eveti dhyeyam । śrutatve apyaśabdaḥ kiṃ na syādityaprayojakatvaśaṅkāyāmāha na hīti । ahi'; yataḥ aaśabdaḥ'; avācyaḥ padārtho ana śrūyate'; na śrutipadenocyata ityarthaḥ । ato nāprayojakatvaṃ hetoriti vākyaśeṣaḥ । virodhādityapi hiśabdārthaḥ । nanu aśabdasyāpi brahmaṇo lakṣaṇayā śrutatvaṃ kiṃ na syādityata āha na ceti । aaprasiddham'; avācyasya brahmaṇo lakṣyatvaṃ na kalpyamityarthaḥ । kutaḥ? yato avācyasya vastuno lakṣyatvamaprasiddham ata iti vyāptiparatvenāpīdaṃ yojanīyam । nanu kathametat? gaṅgāpadāvācyasyāpi tīrasya tatpadalakṣyatvaprasiddherityata uktaṃ sarveti । asarvaśabdāvācyasya'; brahmaṇo lakṣaṇāyāḥ vedapadalakṣyatvasyāyukteḥ vipratipannaṃ na lakṣyaṃ, kenāpi padenāvācyatvāt vyatirekeṇa tīravaditi yuktiviruddhatvādityarthaḥ । tathā ca nāsmābhiḥ kevalāvācyatvena lakṣyatvābhāvaḥ sādhyate yena tīrādau vyabhicāraḥ śaṅkayeta, kintu sarvaśabdāvācyatvena । tacca na tīrādigataṃ, tasya tīrādipadavācyatvāt । brahma tu na tathā, tasya sarvaśabdāvācyatayaiva pareṇāṅgīkṛtatvāt । ato na vyabhicāra iti yuktivirodho duṣparihara iti bhāvaḥ । nanu lakṣyatvābhāvavati pravāhādau hetvabhāvādasādhāraṇamiti cet na, lakṣaṇāyogyasyaiva lakṣyapadārthatve
sarvapadārthānāmapi kiñcitpadalakṣaṇāyogyatvena tadabhāvarūpasādhyasya kutrāpyabhāvena sapakṣasyaivābhāvāt ।
। iti īkṣatyadhikaraṇam ।

। ānandamayādhikaraṇam ।
tameva samasvayaṃ prakaṭayati aānandamayo abhyāsāt'; ityādinā samastenādhyāyena prāyeṇa ।
athādhyāyapādayorupodghātatvena pīṭharūpāyāmasyāṃ pañcādhikaraṇyaṃ brahmasvarūpanarūpaṇe anavaśeṣātkimadhyāyātmakaśeṣagranthenetyata āha tameveti । tathāpītyādau yojyam । samanvayaśabdaśca vipariṇāmenāvartanīyaḥ । tathā ca tathāpi prakaṭanaṃ vinādhyāyākhyaśeṣagranthasya kṛtyāntarābhāve api atameva'; "tattu samanvayāt"ityanena hetutayā sāmānyataḥ siddhavadupanyastameva samanvayāt asamanvayam'; upakramādiliṅgajñāpyaṃ samyagvacanavṛttyā sarvaśāstrīyavacanānāṃ harau nirūpaṇaṃ tatparatvaṃ aprakaṭayati'; prativākyagrahaṇena taddhetūpanyāsādinā prapañcayati "ānandamayo abhyāsāt"ityādinā anena prathamenādhyāyena sūtrakāra ityarthaḥ । anyathā pratijñāmātrasya "tadeva śāstrayoni, samanvayāt"iti siddhavadupanyāsamātrasya sādhakatve "viṣṇoranyadeva śāstrayoni, kutaḥ? samanvayāt samyaktātparyaviṣayatvāt, tathā anyadeva tātparyaviṣayaḥ, kutaḥ? upakramādiliṅgāt"ityapi prativādī brūyāditi bhāvaḥ । yathopakramādikaṃ tajjñāpyaṃ tātparyaṃ ca samanvayaśabdārthaḥ tathā bhāṣyaṃ yojitam adhastāt । yadyapyatra sūtrasya pratīkatvena uttaratra udāhariṣyamāṇatvānnātrāpyudāhartavyatā । tathāpi sūtrānudāharaṇe ānandamayākhyaviṣayāparijñānāttasya viṣṇutvasamarthane kā pūrvasaṅgatirityevaṃ śaṅkānudayāt tanmūlapraśnānudayāt ānandamayāparijñāne brahmaṇastadavayavatvapratītimukhenākṣeparūpaśaṅkānudayācca etadākṣeparūpasaṅgatipradarśanāya
ca adhikaraṇasaṅgativiṣayakaśaṅkotthāpanāya atrāpi sūtrodāharaṇaṃ, uttaratra tu pratīkatveneti draṣṭavyam । adhyāyāntaravyāvṛttyarthamānandamayetyādi । prathamenetyanukttvā evaṃvacanena etadadhikaraṇamārabhyādhyāyārambhaḥ, pañcādhikaraṇyāstu nādhyāyāntarbhāva ityapi sūcitam । samanvayādhikaraṇamārabhyaivādhyāyārambhaḥ tasyaitatprapañcatvāditi pakṣe adhyāyena adhyāyaśeṣeṇetyartha ityavirodhaḥ । caturthapāde na samanvayaḥ kriyata iti paramatanirāsāya asamastena'; samagreṇetyuktam । devatāpaśūdrādhikaraṇayoḥ samanvayākaraṇāt samastenetyanupapannamityāśaṅkānirākaraṇāya aprāyeṇa'; prācuryeṇeti । prāya iti sakārāntāvyayaparyāyo ayamakārāntaḥ prāyaśabdaḥ । tasmātprakṛtyāditvāttṛtīyāyāṃ prāyeṇeti bhavati । ata eva viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāyāṃ bhūmārthe aprāyaḥ'; ityavyayamapyasti ityapiśabdaḥ prāyoji । prameyadīpe api sāntasyaivāvyayatvamuktam ।

prāyeṇānyatraprasiddhānāṃ śabdānāṃ paramātmani samanvayaḥ pradarśyate asmin pāde । nānyathā tadadṛṣṭe ।
tarhi adhyāyasyaikārthatvāt pādabhedaḥ kiṃ nibandhana ityataḥ samanvetavyabhedāt samanvaye apyavāntarabheda iti bhāvena prathamādhyāprathamapādapratipādyaṃ darśayati prāyeṇeti । aasmin'; prathame pāde aprāyeṇa'; bāhulyena aanyatra'; viṣṇoranyatra aprasiddhānāṃ'; śrutyādito lokato vādmapātato rūḍhatvena pratīyamānānāṃ nāmātmakānāṃ aśabdānāṃ'; aparamātmani'; viṣṇau niruktaḥ asamanvayaḥ'; apradarśyate'; prapañcyata ityarthaḥ । atrāpi antaradhikaraṇe antaḥsthatvaliṅgasamanvayapratipādanāt avyāptinirāsāya prāyeṇeti । tattvapradīpe tu eka eva bhāṣye prāyeṇeti śabdaḥ । tasyaivottaratrāpi sambandha ityāśayena "prāyeṇānyatra prasiddhānāṃ śabdānāmiti ca sambandhaḥ"ityuktam । tathā ānandamayādhikaraṇe liṅgavicārattadapi prāyeṇeti vyāvartyamiti coktam । yadvā ṭīkāyāmapyāvṛttyabhiprāyeṇaikasyaiva punaruttaratrāpi anvayapradarśanāya pratīkagrahaṇaṃ kṛtamiti na granthavairūpyaṃ kalpyam । ata eva tattvapradīpānusāreṇa "ānandamayanāmnaḥ iti ṭīkāyāmānandamayanāmaśbadaḥ ānandādināmaparo vā yojyaḥ"ityuktaṃ candrikāyām । atha paroktaṃ pādārthaṃ dūṣayati neti । aanyathā'; prathame spaṣṭabrahmaliṅgānāṃ śabdānāṃ dvitīyatṛtīyayoraspaṣṭabrahmaliṅgānāṃ samanvayaḥ pratipādyate । tayostu saviśeṣanirviśeṣaviṣayatayā bhedaḥ । caturthapāde tu pradhānasyāśābdatvoktirityevaṃ rūpo asmaduktādanyaprakāreṇa pādārtho na vācyaḥ ityarthaḥ । kuto netyata āha taditi । atasya'; paroktapādārthaniyamasya aadṛṣṭeḥ'; etadadhyāyagatapādeṣvadarśanādityarthaḥ । sarvasāṅkaryāditi bhāvaḥ । tacca ṭīkādāvuktam ।

brahmajijñāsā kartavyetyuktam ।
tacca abrahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā'
nanvānandamayādhikaraṇamārabhya sarveṣāmadhikaraṇānāmavaśyavaktavye saṅgatipañcake asminnadhikaraṇe lokato anyatraprasiddhānandamayaśabdopalakṣitaguṇivāciśabdānāmānandādiguṇavāciśabdānāṃ ca brahmaṇi samanvayakaraṇāt
asyāstu śāstre adhyāye pāde cāntarbhāvarūpā saṅgatiḥ । tathāpi ānandamayasya viṣṇutvasamarthane kā pūrvasaṅgatirityato avyavahitapūrvādhikaraṇenaiva saṅgatirvaktavyeti niyamābhāvāt
vyavahitapūrveṇa jijñāsādhikaraṇena tadviṣayeṇa ca asyānantaryalakṣaṇalakṣitāmākṣepikīṃ saṅgatiṃ tāvaddarśayati brahmeti । uktaṃ jijñāsādhikaraṇe iti śeṣaḥ । yajjijñāsyatayā pratijñātaṃ brahma tadevetyarthaḥ । yadvā prakṛtānusandhānārthaścaśabdaḥ । itītyanantaraṃ aśrutau'; iti śeṣaḥ । aānandamayāvayavarūpamiti'; ānandamayākhyasya kasyacitpucchākhyāvayavabhūtaṃ pratīyata ityarthaḥ। nanu brahmaṇo avayavatvoktāvapi kimarthamānandamayasya viṣṇutvasamarthanamityata āha na hīti। aata'; ityāvartate । atacca'; ityādi aityata āha'; ityantaṃ saṅgatiprayojanobhayaparatayā vyākhyeyam । na hītyetattadupapādakam । yojanā tu yato abrahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā'; iti śrutau jijñāsyatayoktaṃ brahma ānandamayākhyasya kasyacidavayavarūpaṃ apratīyate'; ucyate yataśca anyāṅgatayā jijñāsyatve api aavayavinam'; ānandamayaṃ vinā aavayavamātrasya'; avayavasyaiva kevalasya brahmaṇo na pṛthak ajñeyatā'; jijñāsyatā sambhavati । amukhyatvāt । nāpi jijñāsāyā eva tyāgo yujyate । "tadvijijñāsasva" iti śrutivihitatvādityevaṃ śaṅkā prāptā । ataḥ śaṅkārūpasaṅgatisadbhāvāt atrānandamayasya viṣṇvanyatvapakṣe brahmajijñāsākṣepāt viṣṇutvapakṣe ca tatsamādhānāt evaṃ ca pūrvapakṣasiddhāntayoḥ phalasadbhāvācca aato'; brahmajijñāsāsiddhyartham aānandamayo abhyāsāt'; ityānandamayasya viṣṇutvam aāha'; samarthayati sūtrakāra iti ।
"tasmādvā etasmādvijñānamayāt । anyo antara ātmānandamayaḥ । tenaiṣa pūrṇaḥ । sa vā eṣa puruṣavidha eva । tasya puruṣavidhatām । anvayaṃ puruṣavidhaḥ । tasya priyameva śiraḥ । modo dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ । pramoda uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ । brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā" iti taittirīyavākyasyāyamarthaḥ । atasmāt'; ātmapadoditāt aetasmāt'; jīvaśarīragatāt vijñānapūrṇatvāt vijñānamayaśabdavācyāt viṣṇoḥ ananyo apyanyaśabdoktaḥ aānandamayaḥ'; ānandapūrṇatvādānandamayaśabdavācyaḥ aātmā'; nārāyaṇaḥ aantaro'; vijñānamayasyāntaḥsthitaḥ atena'; ānandamayena aeṣaḥ'; vijñānamayaśabdavācyo vāsudevaḥ apūrṇaḥ'; niśchidratvena pūritaḥ । vaiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । asa eṣa'; ānandamayaḥ apuruṣavidha eva'; puruṣākāra eva । atasya'; ānandamayasya śarīrasthānīyasya puruṣākāratām aanu'; anusṛtya aayaṃ'; vijñānamayaḥ śarīrasthānīyaḥ apuruṣavidhaḥ'; tasmātprādurbhūtaḥ,
uttaraiḥ pūritāḥ pūrve niśchidratvena sarvaśaḥ ।
sarve api puruṣākārā uttarātpūrvasambhavaḥ ।
iti taittirīyabhāṣyokteḥ । atasya'; ānandamayasya viṣṇoḥ avayavabhūtaṃ apareyaṃ priyanāmakam'; iti bhāṣyokteḥ । parairuttamaiḥ devaiḥ prāpyatvātpriyaśabdavācyaṃ yatsukhaṃ tattasya aśiraḥ'; tadevānandamayākhyasya jīvaśarīrasya parairanyairupakartṛbhiḥ prāpyatvāt priyanāmakamupakārajanyavaiṣayikasukhākhyaṃ yacchiraḥ tatsthaṃ ca । evamānandamayākhyasya viṣṇoḥ ye dakṣiṇottarabāhumadhyadehāḥ modapramodakāritvānandatvanimittairmoda
pramodānandanāmānaḥ te ānandamayākhyajīvaśarīrasya dakṣiṇottarapakṣātmanāmāno dakṣiṇasavyabāhumadhyadehāḥ। amodo'; bhoganimittakaḥ apramodaḥ'; "tadviśeṣotthaḥ"ityaitareyabhāṣyokteḥ ।
munnāma viṣayotthaṃ yatprakṛṣṭaviṣayātpramut ।
sukhaṃ svarūpabhūtaṃ yadānanda iti kathyate ।
iti bṛhadbhāṣyokteśca । apakṛṣṭaviṣayodbhūtatvaprakṛṣṭaviṣayotthatvajīvasvarūpānandatvanimittairmodapramodānandanāmānasteṣu sthitāśca । evamānandamayākhyasya viṣṇoḥ apucchaṃ'; pratiṣṭhati gacchati loka ābhyāmiti vyutpattyā pratiṣṭhāpadokto yaḥ pādākhyo avayavaḥ tadbrahma abrahmasṛṣṭyā tu bṛṃhayet'; iti taittirīyabhāṣyoktarītyā sṛṣṭyādikriyayā viśvaguṇavṛddhikaratvādbrahmaśabdavācyaḥ sa evānandamayākhyajīvaśarīrasya yat pucchaṃ yaḥ pādākhyo avayavaḥ tatsthite brahmākhye pradhānavāyau sthitaḥ । anena kośāvayavasya brahmaśabdavācyatvaṃ brahmaśabdavācyapradhānavāyvadhiṣṭhānatvanimittaṃ, pradhānavāyorbrahmaśabdavācyatvaṃ tu parabrahmādhiṣṭhānatvādityuktaṃ bhavati । anenānandamayādiśabdavācyasya viṣṇoravayava
