siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati ata iti । yataḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ prāpto ataḥ uttaraṃ sūtramāha bhagavānbādarāyaṇa ityarthaḥ । tadeva sūtraṃ paṭhati jyotiriti । sūtre tattvityasya anuvṛttiṃ vipariṇāmaṃ cābhipretya pratijñāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe viṣṇureveti । ajyotiḥ'; tacchabdavācyo viṣṇureva bhavediti yojanā । kuta ityataḥ prāptaṃ acaraṇābhidhānāt'; iti hetvaṃśaṃ caraṇaśabdasya vicaraṇārthatvaṃ karṇādīnāmityasya adhyāhāraṃ cābhipretya vyācaṣṭe karṇādīnāmiti । atra vākye karṇādīnāmetajjyotiḥprati viruddhacaraṇokteḥ karṇādividūratvaliṅgaśravaṇādityarthaḥ । atra karṇādividūratvaṃ nāma tairiyaditi paricchedāyogyavaibhavatvaṃ, na tu karṇādividūratvamātram । tadviṣaye tasyāsambhavāt । abhidhānaparyantadhāvanaṃ hetvasiddhiparihārāyeti draṣṭavyam ।

sa hi aparo mātrayā tanvā vṛdhāna'; 
ityādinā karṇādividūraḥ ।
nanvastu jyotiṣaḥ karṇādividūratvoktiḥ, tāvatā tasya viṣṇutvaṃ kuta ityataḥ karṇādividūratvasya viṣṇvekaliṅgatve śrutimudāharan tatpratijānīte sa hīti । ādiśabdena ana te viṣṇo'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇureva aparo mātrayā'; ityādivākyena karṇādividūra iti pramitaḥ tasmānnāprayojakatā, na vā hetuviśeṣaṇāsiddhirityadhyāhāreṇa yojanā । anena ajyotiḥ'; tacchabdavācyaṃ brahmaiva । kutaḥ? atra karṇādīnāmetajjyotiḥ prati sākalyena tadaviṣayīkaraṇarūpaviruddha acaraṇābhidhānāt'; karṇādividūratvaliṅgaśravaṇāt ittyāvṛttyadhyāhārābhyāṃ sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । māpayati jñāpayati viṣayāniti vā mīyante viṣayā aneneti vā mātrā indriyagaṇaḥ tayā tatastvaṃ aparo'; dūro asīti he viṣṇo anyamahimnaḥ paramantaṃ sīmānaṃ te mahimānaṃ ko api śrotrādinā nāpeti ca prakṛtānuguṇyena śrutirvyākhyeyā । atra tattvapradīpasannyāyaratnāvalīkārayoḥ jyotirityādicatussūcī ekamevāntarbhedādhikaraṇamityabhipretam । agnisūktacchāndogyagataviṣayavākyabhedādanayorbhedaḥ । ṭīkākṛtastujyotissūtramekamadhikaraṇaṃ achandaḥ'; ityāditrisūtrī adhikaraṇāntaramiti jñātavyam । ।
। iti jyotiradhikaraṇam । ।

। chando abhidhānādhikaraṇam ।
chando abhidhānān neti cen na tathā ceto'rpaṇanigadāt tathā hi darśanam ।
atrādhikaraṇe adhivedagatagāyatryādyaśeṣaśabdasamanvayaḥ kriyate । saṅgatyādijijñāsājananāya sūtramevādau paṭhati chanda iti ।। atra chanda ityāvartate । tacca vyastaṃ samastaṃ ca । tathā ca achando abhidhānāt'; agāyatrī vā idam'; iti vākyasthagāyatrīśabdena caturviṃśatyakṣaramantraviśeṣātmakachandasaḥ pratipādanāt, tacchabdasya tatra rūḍhatvāt, gāyatrīśabdavācyo na viṣṇuḥ, kintu chanda eva । yato gāyatrī na viṣṇuḥ, api tu chandaḥ, ato jyotirapi na viṣṇuḥ kintu chandaḥ । kutaḥ? achando abhidhānāt'; chandasā gāyatryā tadaikyābhiprāyeṇa jyotiṣo abhidhānāt upakramāditi cet na, viṣṇureva jyotiḥ । kutaḥ? anigadāt'; gāyatrīpadena viṣṇorevābhidhānāt । gāyatryādipadairviṣṇorevābhidhānaṃ ca tadabhedavidhānārthaṃ kintu tathopāsanārthamevetyāha tatheti । atathā'; gāyatryādiśabdārthaguṇasvarūpatvena acetaso'; manasaḥ aarpaṇāya'; brahmaṇyādhānāyopāsanārthameva viṣṇornigadādityarthaḥ । upāsanetyanuktvā
cetorpaṇetyuktirupāsanāsvarūpakathanārthā । anena prasiddhagāyatryādipadena viṣṇorabhidhānaṃ vyarthamiti śaṅkā parihṛtā। nanu bhavedgāyatrīśabdavācyatvena viṣṇorjyotiśśabdavācyatvasādhanam, yadi gāyatrīśabdavācyatvaṃ viṣṇoḥ pramitaṃ syāt । tadeva kuta ityata āha tathā hīti । ahi'; yasmāt atathā'; gānatrāṇakartṛtvanimittena viṣṇorgāyatrīśabdavācyatvasādhakaṃ adarśanaṃ'; dṛśyate jñāyate artho yayeti vyupattyā agāyati ca trāyati ca'; ityādirūpā śrutirasti tasmāditi sūtrārthaḥ ।

aatha yadataḥ paro divo jyotirdīpyate'; 
ityuktasya jyotiṣo agāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvam'; 
iti gāyatryā samārambhaḥ kṛtaḥ ।
tasmānna viṣṇuriti cet na, tathā cetor'paṇārthaṃ hi nigadyate ।
agnigāyatryādiśabdārtharūpo asāviti cetor'paṇārthaṃ hi nigadyate ।
śrutyādisaṅgativiṣayavākyaviṣayasaṃśayapūrvapakṣatatphalāni sūcayan sūtre pūrvapakṣāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe atheti । uktasyetyāvartyate । tathā ca ahṛdaya āhitaṃ yat'; iti guhānihitatvena yaduktaṃ tasyaiva ajyotiṣaḥ'; punaḥ aatha yadataḥ paro divo jyotirdīpyate viśvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu sarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu anuttameṣūttameṣu lokeṣu । idaṃ vāva tadyadidamasminnantaḥpuruṣe jyotiḥ'; iti chāndogye apyuktasya agāyatryā'; itthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇe tṛtīyā । gāyatrītvena tadrūpatayā asamārambhaḥ'; pāṭhaḥ kṛtaḥ । kuto ayaṃ vijñāyate? yato agāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvaṃ vāgvai gāyatrī vāgvā idaṃ sarvam'; iti vākye agāyatryā'; gāyatrīśabdena tadaikyatātparyeṇa asamārambhaḥ'; upakramaḥ kṛtaḥ ata iti yojanā । tataḥ kimityata āha tasmāditi। jyotirgāyatrīti ca śeṣaḥ । chanda iti cānuṣajyate । tathā ca yasmādgāyatryā samārambhaḥ kṛtaḥ, sa ca yasmādanupasañjātavirodhitvena balavān, tasmādidaṃ jyotirgāyatryeva bhavet । sā ca gāyatrī virṇasamāveśalakṣaṇamantrātmakachanda eva bhavet, na viṣṇuḥ । kutaḥ? tasmāt gāyatrīśabdasya chandasyeva rūḍhatvādvāktvābhidhānācceti yojanā । anena agāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvam'; iti pūrvavākyasthagāyatrīśabdasya viṣṇvanyaparatve tata evottaravākyasthajyotiṣo viṣṇvanyatvāpattyā tata eva agnisūktagatajyotiṣo api tadanyatvameva bhavet । ata evānandamayatvamapi anyasyaiva bhavenna viṣṇoriti pūrvoktākṣepeṇa etadadhikaraṇotthānātpūrveṇāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ । evaṃ gāyatrī viṣayaḥ । kiṃ chandoviśeṣaḥ uta viṣṇuriti sandehaḥ । tathā gāyatrī chandoviśeṣa eva bhavet; tacchabdasya tatra rūḍhatvāditi sayuktikaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ । tathā tasmāt jyotirapi chanda eveti tasyaiva guhānihitatvamāndamayatvaṃ ceti pūrvapakṣaphalaṃ ca sūcitaṃ bhavati । atra pūrvapakṣe gāyatryādiśabdāḥ mantraparāḥ, sarvamapi vākyaṃ tanmāhātmyaparatayā yojanīyam। siddhānte tu aatha'; ityāderayamarthaḥ bhagavanmāhātmyāntarārambhe athaśabdaḥ ayat'; śvetadvīpānantāsanavaikuṇṭhagataṃ nārāyaṇavāsudevavaikuṇṭhākhyaṃ rūpatrayaṃ tat aataḥ'; etasmādvivakṣitādbuddhisthāt adivaḥ paraḥ'; paraṃ tadapekṣayoccasthānasthitamityarthaḥ । ajyotiḥ'; tejomayaṃ evaṃbhūtaṃ tat aviśvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu'
pṛthivyāṃ brahmaṇo merau vaijayante antarikṣagam ।
tṛtīyaṃ satyaloke ca sadanaṃ trividhaṃ matam ।
iti vacanādantarikṣagavaijayantamerusatyalokagatebhyo brahmasadanebhyaḥ krameṇocceṣu asarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu'; antarikṣapṛthivīsvarātmakalokebhyaḥ krameṇocceṣu aanuttameṣu'; na vidyate uttamo loko yebhyasteṣu pratyavareṣviti vā । auttameṣu'; svayamevottameṣu alokeṣu'; śvetadvīpānantāsanavaikuṇṭheṣu adīpyate'; prakāśate
atat'; dīpyamānaṃ tejaḥ aidaṃ vāva'; idaṃ khalu। idaṃ ca kim? ayadidamasmin puruṣe'; hṛdaye aantarjyotiḥ'; tacchabditaṃ brahmāsti tattenaikībhūtamityarthaḥ । yo gāyatrīnāmā gāyatrīsaṃsthaḥ strīrūpo hayaśīrṣākhyo bhagavān tadidaṃ prathamaṃ rūpamityāśayena tasya dvitīyaṃ rūpaṃ vaktuṃ gāyatrītyādivākyaṃ pravṛttam । ayadidaṃ kiñca bhūtaṃ'; pūrṇaṃ matsyādyavatārarūpaṃ yacca asarvaṃ'; sarvāntaḥsthitaṃ rūpaṃ tatsarvaṃ agāyatrī'; gāyatrīnāmā bhagavāneva । vai prasiddham । tasyaiva tṛtīyaṃ rūpamāha vāgiti । gāyatrīnāmā bhagavān avāgvai'; vāṅnāmako viṣṇureva । kuto asya viṣṇutvamityatastallakṣaṇayogādityāha vāgvā iti । aidaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ'; prāṇijātaṃ avāgvai'; vāṅnāmakabhagavadadhīnameva । ataḥ sarvasvāmitvādvāco viṣṇutvamiti । siddhāntasūtrāṃśamanukaroti neti । nigadyata ityatrāpi sambadhyate । tathā ca jyotiḥśabdena viṣṇureva nigadyata ityarthaḥ । kuta ityato nigadāditi hetuṃ yojayati hi nigadyata iti । gāyatrīśabdeneti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yasmādgāyatrīśabdenāpi viṣṇureva anigadyate'; abhīdhīyate tasmādityarthaḥ । viṣṇorgāyatryādiśabdairabhidhānaṃ ca na tadabhedavidhānārthaṃ, kintu tathopāsanārthamevetyāha tatheti । ceto arpaṇetyuktiprayojanaṃ pūrvavat । bhāṣyatvajñāpanāya tathetyādisvapadāni tathāśabdārthakathanena vivṛṇoti agnīti । atra jyotiśśabdopalakṣakāgnipadaṃ jyotissūtrasya bhinnādhikaraṇatvapakṣe anyatra prasiddhasya gāyatrīpadasya viṣṇau prayoge prayojanamatra vadatā sūtrakṛtā pūrvatrottaratra cāgnyādipadasya viṣṇau prayoge prayojanaṃ sūcitamiti darśayitum । na ca gāyatryādipadābhyāmeva gāyatrīpadasamanvayaphalasya pūrvatrottaratra coktasamanvayaphalasya ca sūcanasambhavādagnipadaṃ vyarthamiti vācyam । phalībhūtasamanvayaviṣayatvenāsyāpi avaśyopādeyatvāt । samānaprakaraṇasthavāgādigrāhakatvena ādiśabdasyāpyāvaśyakatvāt । avaśyāpekṣitābhyāmubhābhyāmapyānandamayādyadhikaraṇeṣu uttaratra coktaprayojanasyāpi sūcanasambhavādubhayamapyāvaśyakam । jyotirityādicatuḥsūtryā ekādhikaraṇatvapakṣe tu sākṣātsamanvetavyapaśabdatvenaiva śabdadvayopādānaṃ, na tu phalatvenāgniśabdasyādhikaraṇāntare apyetannyāyasūcanaṃ tu ādiśabdenaiva, na tūbhābhyām । bhinnajātīyānekaśabdagrahaṇārthaṃ śabdadvayottarādipadam । ata eva tattvapradīpe ādiśabdasyobhayatrānvayaṃ prathamādiśabdena tejaḥśabdānāṃ dvitīyena chandaśśabdānāṃ ca grahaṇamabhipretya aagnyāditejaḥśabdānāṃ gāyatryādichandaśśabdānāṃ ca'; ityuktam। kecittu bhāṣyagatahiśabdo jñānārthamatha dhyānārthamiti pramāṇaprasiddhidyotakaḥ, adhikaraṇāntare apyasya nyāyasyānusandheyatvajñāpakaścetyāhuḥ । ceto arpaṇārthamiti sāvadhāraṇam । tathā ca aasau'; bhagavānagnigāyatryādiśabdairagnigāyatryādiśabdārthaguṇasvarūpa iti । tatra aceto arpaṇārthaṃ'; budhyavatāraṇārtham upāsanārthameva nigadyate, na tadabhedavidhānārthamityarthaḥ । itītyantena tathāśabdārtha uktaḥ। anenāprasiddhagāyatryādipadena viṣṇorabhidhānasya vaiyarthyaśaṅkā parihṛtā ।

tathā hi darśanaṃ agāyati trāyati ca'; ityādi ।
nanu bhavedgāyatryādiśabdavācyatvena viṣṇorjyotiśśabdavācyatāsādhanaṃ yadīyaṃ gāyatrī viṣṇuḥ syāttadeva kuta ityato gānatrāṇakartṛtvaliṅgādityāśayena tasyāsiddhiparihārāya pravṛttaṃ tathāhīti sūtraśeṣam
anukṛtya darśanapadoktāṃ śrutiṃ darśayati tatheti । ahi'; yasmāt aityādi darśanaṃ'; śrutirastītyanvayaḥ । yadyapi agāyati trāyate ca'; iti pāṭhaḥ chandogānam, tathāpi śākhāntaramevedamityadoṣaḥ । ādipadena ayā vai sā gāyatrī iyaṃ vāva sā yeyaṃ pṛthivyasyāṃ hīdaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ pratiṣṭhitametāmeva nātiśīyate'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । śrutyarthastu yato gāyatrīvācyo bhagavān vedān agāyati'; mukhānnissārayati prathamo vakteti yāvat । yasmācca atrāyate'; akhilamiti śeṣaḥ। ato gāyatrīśabdenocyate । ayā'; prasiddhā gāyatrī tannāmā viṣṇuḥ asā iyaṃ vai'; iyaṃ khalu । kimiyam? ayeyaṃ pṛthivī'; tannāmā bhagavān । kathaṃ pṛthivī viṣṇurityataḥ tallakṣaṇayogādityāha asyāṃ hīdamiti । aasyāṃ'; pṛthivyāṃ abhūtaṃ'; prāṇijātamāśritamiti । sudhāyāṃ tu pūrvapakṣānuguṇatayā gāyatrī agāyati'; arthaṃ pratipādayati, adhyetṛn atrāyate'; pālayati pāpāt rakṣatītyartha uktaḥ ।

sarvachando abhidho hyeṣaḥ sarvadevābhidho hyasau ।
sarvalokābhidho hyeṣasteṣāṃ tadupacārataḥ ।
iti vāmane ।
nanu gāyatryādiśabdasya anyatra rūḍhatvātkathaṃ liṅgamātreṇa viṣṇutvaniścaya ityato gāyatryādiśruteḥ sāvakāśatvāditi bhāvena gāyatryagnipṛthivyādiśabdāḥ na kevalaṃ śrutyuktayogena viṣṇau sāvakāśāḥ, api tu paurāṇikarūḍhyā gāyatryāḥ bhagavadadhīnatvādapītyāśayena tatra smṛtimāha sarveti । aeṣaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ asarvachando abhidhaḥ'; sarvachandasām abhidhevābhidhā yasyeti bahuvrīhiḥ । chandovācakagāyatryādisarvaśabdavācyaḥ ।
aevamasau'; viṣṇuḥ sarvadevatāvācakāgnyādiśabdavācyaḥ । tathā aeṣaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ sarvalokavācakapṛthivyādiśabdavācya ityarthaḥ । kuta ityataḥ chanda ādīnāṃ bhagavadadhīnatvāditi pratyekaṃ hetutrayasūcanāya hiśabdatrayaṃ, vedaprasiddhijñāpānāya vā । chandasāṃ lokānāṃ ca pratyakṣatvāt devānāṃ ca parokṣatvādeṣo asāviti vicitroktiḥ । kathaṃ tarhyanyatra vyavahāra ityata āha teṣāmiti । chandodevalokānāmityarthaḥ । atat'; tacchabdabodhyatvam aupacārato'; viṣṇusamīpe caraṇāttadadhīnatvādamukhyata evetyarthaḥ। vāmana ityasya ahi'; yato vāmane iti adarśanaṃ'; pratipādanamastyataḥ śrutermukhyavṛtyā viṣṇāveva sāvakāśatvāt liṅgasyāmukhyato apyanyatrānavakāśatvāttena tadbādhopapatterbhavatyeva gānatrāṇakartṛtvaliṅgamātreṇāyaṃ nirṇaya ityupaskareṇānvayaḥ ।

bhūtādipādavyapadeśopapatteś caivam ।
hetvantareṇāpi gāyatryāḥ viṣṇutvaṃ sādhayatsūtramupanyasya tadgṛhītāṃ śrutimudāharati bhūtādīti। itiśabdasya bhūtādītyanenānvayaḥ । sūtre bhūtaṃ viśvamādiḥ prathamoddiṣṭaṃ yeṣu te bhūtādayaḥ, te pādāḥ yasya gāyatrīpadārthasya sa bhūtādipādaḥ, tasya vyapadeśaḥ tatpratipādakaṃ vākyaṃ tasyopapatteḥ yuktatvāditi vigrahaḥ । pādaśabdo bhāvapradhānaḥ । ata eva bhūtādipādatvasyetyuktaṃ ṭīkāyām । evamityasya cobhayatrānvayaḥ । tathā ca apādo asya sarvā bhūtāni । tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi'; ityevaṃ gāyatryāḥ
bhūtādiśabdagṛhītāmṛtākhyāṃśacatuṣṭavattvopadeśāt tasya ca viṣṇāvevopapatteranyatrānupapattereva gāyatrīśabdavācyo viṣṇureva bhavedityarthaḥ । caśabdasya vyapadeśapadenānvaye gāyatryā viṣṇutve sādhye pūrvasūtre darśanapadoktahetoḥ etatsūtroktahetudvayasya ca samuccaye saḥ । yathāśrutānvaye tu bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatvaṃ na kevalaṃ viṣṇorevopapatteḥ siddham, kintu puruṣasūktoktatvācceti hetusamuccaye sa iti jñeyam । chāndogye hi asaiṣā catuṣpadā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī'; iti vākyena yaiṣā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī sā catuṣpadetyevaṃ gāyatrīnāmakasya bhagavataḥ prāguktagāyatrībhūtavākpṛthivīśarīrahṛdayalakṣaṇaṣaḍvidhatvamanūdya aṃśacatuṣṭayavattvarūpaṃ catuṣpādatvaṃ vidhāya svoktārtha eva puruṣasūktamantraḥ samākhyārūpatvenodāhṛto brāhmaṇena atadetadṛcābhyanūktam'; iti atadetat'; bhagavataścatuṣpādatvaṃ aṛcā'; ṛṅmantreṇa aabhi'; niśśaṅkaṃ spaṣṭam aanu'; ānukūlyenoktamityarthaḥ ।

atāvānasya mahimā tato jyāyāṃśca puruṣaḥ ।
pādo asya sarvā bhūtāni tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi'; iti ।
kimuktamityatastanmantraṃ paṭhati tāvāniti । yadyapi ṛci aetāvān'; iti aviśvā'; iti ca pāṭhaḥ । tathāpi śākhāntarapāṭho ayamityadoṣaḥ । aasya'; puruṣasya apuruṣa evedaṃ sarvam'; ityṛcā yassarveśānatvādirūpaḥ tāvānmahimoktaḥ, na kevalametāvān, kintu, puruṣaḥ atataḥ'; pūrvoktadapi mahimno ajyāyān'; adhikamāhātmyopeta ityarthaḥ । jyāyastvameva darśayati pādo asyetyādinā । asarvā bhūtāni'; sarvaṃ viśvam aasya'; viṣṇorekaḥ apādaḥ'; pādavatpādo bhinnāṃśaḥ । yadyapi tattvapradīpe viśvabhūvidhirbhāti । tathāpi ṭīkāyāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtānyasyaikaḥ pāda iti pādavidhānadarśanāt; candrikāyāṃ apaśvekatvavat vidheyagatatvātpādaikatvaṃ vivakṣitam'; ityuktatvācca, tattvapradīpo apyevameva vyākhyeyaḥ । asya aamṛtaṃ'; nāśarahitam ata eva svarūpabhūtaṃ atripāt'; trayāṇāṃ pādānām aṃśānāṃ samudāyo nārāyaṇavāsudevavaikuṇṭhasaṃjñaṃ triṣu rūḍhyā dyotamānatvācca dyuśabdavācyeṣu śvetadvīpānantāsanavaikuṇṭheṣu tiṣṭhatīti ṛcoktamityarthaḥ । yadyapi bhūtaśabdo abhinnapādassarvajīvāḥ'; iti chāndogyabhāṣye jīvaparatayā vyākhyātaḥ । tathāpi asuvarṇam'; iti śrutyanusāreṇa atra viśvārthatayā vyākhyātavyaḥ ।

suvarṇaṃ kośaṃ rajasā parīvṛtam ।
devānāṃ vasudhānīṃ virājam ।
amṛtasya pūrṇāṃ tāmu kalāṃ vicakṣate ।
pādaṃ ṣaḍḍhoturna kilā vivitse iti śruteḥ ।
pāda iti ekadeśaparimitaṃ caturbhāgabala itivadbhinnaṃ ca ।
nanu gāyatryāmiva viṣṇāvapi bhūtādipādatvoktiranupapannā । tasya bhūtabhinnatvādityata āha suvarṇamityādi ।। asuvarṇam'; ityārabhya abhinnaṃ ca'; ityantamekavākyatayārthakrameṇa vyākhyeyam । yajñadattasya, devadattaḥ, ityucyate, viśvamiti ca śeṣaḥ । pāda iti cāvartate । caśabdaevārthe hetau ca । ekadeśaparimitamiti hetugarbhamāvartanīyam । tathā ca aco'; yataḥ śrutisthena pāda iti śabdena na bhūtānāmityamṛtapādatrayavatsvarūpāṃśatvamucyate। yenānupapattiḥ syāt । kintu, yajñadattasya caturbhāgabalo devadatta iti vadbhinnameva viśvam । yataḥ aparimitam'; viṣṇupādaparimitasāmarthyam ataḥ pāda iti viṣṇupādatvenocyate ityarthaḥ । asyāto viṣṇau bhūtādipādavyapadeśopapatteścaivamiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । tarhi viśvacatuṣṭayasamo harirityāgatamityato apyāha pāda itīti। tathā ca yataḥ śrautapāda iti padena caturbhāgabala itivat na viśvaṃ viṣṇusāmarthyasya caturthāṃśaparimitamityucyate । kintu, aekadeśaparimitaṃ'; viṣṇusāmarthyaikadeśaparimitamiti ato noktadoṣa ityarthaḥ । kuta etat jñāyata ityata āha suvarṇaṃ kośamiti । aśruteḥ'; taittirīyaśruteḥ । śrutau tṛtīyārthe ṣaṣṭhī, samudāyaikavacanaṃ caitat । ata eva amuktaiḥ pūrṇām'; ityuktaṃ ṭīkāyām । evaṃ ca tattpradīpaṭīkayorekavākyatayā । tatraikaṃ bhāvasādhanam । na kileti dīrghaḥ sāṃhitikaḥ । tathā ca ekasmin kapāle asuvarṇaṃ'; tanmayaṃ arajasā parīvṛtaṃ'; rajoguṇopalakṣitabagnīranabho ahaṃkṛnmahattattvaguṇatrayaiḥ parivṛtaṃ avirājaṃ'; brahmaṇaḥ śarīraṃ, tattvapradīparītyā viśeṣeṇa rājantamiva akośaṃ'; liṅgavyatyayaḥ, brahmāṇḍākhyaṃ yadasti । devānāṃ avasudhānīṃ'; dravyanidhānamañjūṣām aamṛtaiḥ'; muktaiḥ pūrṇāṃ tāṃ aṣaḍḍhotuḥ'; ṣaḍindriyeṣu viṣayān juhvataḥ, ṣaḍindriyāṇi viṣayeṣu jīvena juhvato vā, ṣaḍindriyaiḥ sārādanakarturvā, viṣṇoḥ akalāmu'; ekadeśaparimitāmeva apādaṃ vicakṣate'; pādaśabdenācakṣate vadanti puruṣasūktādyāgamā iti śeṣaḥ । na kila atra pādaśabdenāṅghri vadanti, nāpi caturthāṃśamityevārthaḥ । kutaḥ? yataḥ sā mañjūṣā apādaṃ'; pādatvaṃ caturthabhāgasāmyaṃ ana vivitse'; na lebhe kileti śrutyarthaḥ । sattarkadīpāvalyām pādaṃ na vivitse iti । pādasāmyaṃ na lebhe ityuktam । atra pakṣadvaye api puruṣavyatyayastulyaḥ । ṭīkākṛtpakṣe lakāravyatyayaśca । yadvā liṅgavyatyayasya chāndasatvaṃ kośamityasya dvitīyāntatvaṃ copetya strīliṅgapadānāmapi kośaviśeṣaṇatvenaika evānvayaḥ।

sa hi puruṣasūktābhidheyaḥ ।
ayajñena yajñamayajanta'; iti yajñaśabdāt ।
ayajño viṣṇurdevatā'; iti hi śrutiḥ ।
syādetadevaṃ yadi atāvān'; ityasyāmṛci viṣṇurabhidhīyate ityatra pramāṇaṃ syāt, tadeva nāsti, ato liṅgamanyaniṣṭhaṃ bhaviṣyatītyataḥ sautracaśabdena bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatve sādhye puruṣasūktoktatvāditi yadanumānaṃ sūcitaṃ tasyāprayojakatvamāśaṅkya pariharati sa hīti । ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇureva apuruṣasūktābhidheyaḥ'; tatpratipādyaḥ tasmātsa eva puruṣasūktoktabhūtādipādo apīti yojanā । anyathā bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇudharmatvābhāve puruṣasūktapratipādyatvaṃ na syāditi bhāvaḥ । yadvā gāyatryā viṣṇutve sādhye sūtre bhinnakrameṇānvitacaśabdasūcitayuktyantaramāha sa hīti । asya tasmādgāyātrī viṣṇureveti pradhānapratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । catuṣpadetyuktagāyatrīcatuṣpādatvasya puruṣasūktamantreṇopapādanāt tatpratipādyatve tadupapādyagāyatrīśabdārthatāpi tasyaiva prāpnotīti bhāvaḥ । puruṣasūktoktasya viṣṇutvaṃ kuta ityata āha yajñeneti । devāḥ ayajñena'; jñānakarmātmakena rudrākhyapaśunā vā ayajñaṃ'; viṣṇum aayajanta'; apūjayanniti śrutyarthaḥ । iti yajñaśabdāditi । iti vākye yajñaśabdaśravaṇādityarthaḥ । yajñaśabdaḥ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścāyaka ityato vidvadrūḍhyetyāha yajña iti । ahi'; yataḥ yajña iti padena viṣṇvākhyā devatācyata ityarthaḥ । yadyapi ayajño vai viṣṇuḥ'; ityadhvaryūṇāṃ śrutiḥ । tathāpi śrutyantaramidamityadoṣaḥ ।

tasmin kāle mahārāja rāma evābhidhīyate ।
yathā hi pauruṣe sūkte viṣṇurevābhidhīyate ।
iti ca skānde ।
nanu puruṣasūktaṃ na viṣṇuprakaraṇaṃ, kintvanyaprakaraṇameva । na ca yajñaśrutivirodhaḥ । paśurūpānyaprakaraṇe tadanyaviṣṇuśruteḥ ayogāditivācyam । tasyāḥ prāsaṅgikatvasambhavāt । na ca tata eva bhūtādipādatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatvaniścayaḥ । apādo asya viśvā bhūtāni'; iti śruterbhūtādipāde yajñaśruterabhāvādtyataḥ puruṣasūktoktasya viṣṇutve smṛtiñcāha tasminniti । mahārājeti kasyacitsambodhanaṃ rāmaviśeṣaṇaṃ vā । tathātve dīrghassyāt । tathā ca he mahārāja atasmin'; tretāyuge sarvaiḥ puruṣanāmabhī rāma evābhidhīyate ityarthaḥ । ata evāṃśādhikaraṇe 
nakṣatramānagaṇitaṃ trayodaśasahasrakam ।
brahmalokasamaṃ cakre samastaṃ sarveṣāmabhavattadā ।
rāmorāma iti hyākhyā sarveṣāmabhavattadā ।
sarvo rāmamayo loko yadā rāmastvapālayat ।
iti skānde ityuktaṃ tattvapradīpe । atra dṛṣṭāntamāha yatheti । yathā kṛtsne pauruṣe sūkte viṣṇureva na tvanyaḥ । paśuḥ naraḥ prāsaṅgikatayābhidhīyate ityarthaḥ । anena siddhasyaiva dṛṣṭāntatvātpuruṣasūktasya viṣṇuparatvaṃ siddhamiti bhāvaḥ । skānda ityantaraṃ etaduktamiti śeṣaḥ । asya sa hīti purvavākyenānvayaḥ।

upadeśabhedān neti cen nobhayasminn apy avirodhāt ।
atripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi'; iti pūrvopadeśaḥ ।
aparo divaḥ'; iti pañcamyantaḥ paścimaḥ ।
tasmānnekaṃ vastvatrocyate iti cet na, trisaptalokāpekṣayā ubhayasminnapyavirodhāt ।
uktamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasyati upadeśeti । aupadeśayoḥ'; saptamīpañcamīyutavākyayoḥ aupadeśena'; gāyatrījyotiṣoḥ dyusthatvadivaḥparatvarūpaviruddhadharmoktyā abhedāt'; virodhāt na dvayorviṣṇvākhyam ekaṃ vastu pratipādyaṃ, kintu bhinnameveti cet na, kintu aubhayasmin'; ubhayatrāpyupadeśe ekameva pratipādyaṃ, katham? avirodhāt । trisaptalokāpekṣayā saptamīpañcamyoḥ ekārthatvena virodhābhāvāditi sūtrayojanāmabhiprayannākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe tripāditi । apūrvopadeśaḥ'; pūrvoktiḥ । apaścimaḥ'; paścāttanaḥ uttara upadeśastadbhinno astīti śeṣaḥ। virodhasphoraṇāya pañcamyanta ityādyuktiḥ । upakramagatasya prābalyopapādanāya pūrva ityuktiḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha tasmāditi । yasmādevaṃ bhinnopadeśadvayamasti tasmādatropadeśadvaye gāyatrījyotiśśabdābhyāṃ naikaṃ vastu viṣṇvākhyamucyate । kutaḥ? yato atra anaikam'; anekaṃ vastu dyusthatvadivaḥparatvarūpaṃ dharmadvayamucyate । kintvatra anaikam'; anekaṃ vastudvayamucyate iti yojanā । siddhāntayatsūtrāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe neti । nātra vastudvayamucyate ityarthaḥ । kiṃ tvitiśeṣaḥ, ekaṃ vastūcyate iti anuṣajyate । ubhayasminniti sādhyāntargatam । apiśabdo na kevalamekatra, kintūbhayatrāpīti samuccaye । tathā ca kintūbhayasmin apyupadeśe ekameva viṣṇvākhyaṃ vastūcyate iti yojanā । virodhātkathametadyujyate ityata āha trisaptalokāpekṣayeti । trilokavivakṣayā saptalokavivakṣayā ca aavirodhāt'; ubhayatrāpyekavastvabhidhāne virodhābhāvādityarthaḥ । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ yadā bhūrbhuvassvariti lokatrayavivakṣā, tadā lakṣayojanocchritāntarikṣākhyabhuva uparitanasya sarvasyāpi dyutvāt śvetadvīpānantasanavaikuṇṭhānāṃ cāntarikṣāduparitanatvāttatratyaṃ nārāyaṇavāsudevavaikuṇṭhākhyaṃ tripācchabdoktaṃ rūpatrayaṃ divitiṣṭhatītyucyate iti na saptamyantopadeśavirodhaḥ । na ca
pṛthivīstheṣu sarvocco loko anantāsanātmakaḥ ।
antarikṣātmakebhyaśca śvetadvīpasthito hariḥ ।
ityukteranantāsanasya nāntarikṣāduparitanateti śaṅkyam । tasya pṛthivīsthatve api bahulakṣayojanocchritatvenaikalakṣayojanocchritāntarikṣāduparitanatvopapatteḥ । sarvapṛthivīsthoccatvoktyā tu na pṛthivīsthānyoccatvayogovyāvartyate । kintu pṛthivīsthoccatvāyogaḥ । yadā tu bhūrbhuvassvarmaharjanaspassatyamiti saptalokavivakṣā । tadendrasadanasya dyutvāt taduccasyāpyuparisthitatvena tatsajātīyasyavaikuṇṭhasya divaḥ paratvam ।
pṛthivyāṃ dyaurmahāmerurākāśe sūryamaṇḍalam ।
divīndrasadanaṃ caiva tatpare tu divaḥ pare ।
iti smṛtermerorapi dyutvāttaduccasya bhūspṛṣṭatvena tatsajātīyasyānantāsanasyāpi divaḥ paratā । evaṃ sūryamaṇḍalasyāpi dyutvāttaduccasyoparisthatvena tatsajātīyasya bhūmeḥ kiñcidantaritasya sarvargasamonnatasya śvetadvīpasyāpi divaḥ paratvamastīti na pañcamyantopadeśavirodho apīti । dyuparatvaṃ ca sambhāvitasajātīyadyuparatvamiti na yāvattvayatkiñcittvamukhena dūṣaṇāvakāśaḥ । vaikuṇṭhasya svargalokātparatvenaiva divaḥ paratvasiddhāvapi tasya asarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu'; ityanenaiva uktatvāt svargatyāgenendrasadanasya dyutvoktiḥ । na ca lokatrayavivakṣayaivānantāsanādīnāmapi mervādiparatvena divaḥ paratvasyāpi siddheḥ saptalokavivakṣā vyartheti vācyam । tathā sati vaikuṇṭhasyāpi dyuśabdārthaniviṣṭatvena tasya sarvadyuparatvāsiddhyāpatyā advyātmakebhyaśca sarvebhyo vaikuṇṭhaścocca ucyate'; iti pramāṇavirodhāpātāt । chāndogyabhāṣye tu 
anantaśayanaṃ caiva tathānantāsanaṃ hareḥ ।
bahulakṣocchrite nitye vimāne saṃsthitaṃ yataḥ ।
citprakṛtyātmani yato divīti kathitaṃ śrutau ।
iti pramāṇabalena citprakṛtyātmakānantāsanaśvetadvīpavaikuṇṭhākhyasthānatraye saptamyanto dyuśabdo dyotamānatvanimittena yaugikaḥ, svargādau tu rūḍha iti upadeśayoravirodha iti prakārāntareṇa virodhaparihāraḥ kṛtaḥ ।
। iti chando abhidhānādhikaraṇam । ।

। pādāntyaprāṇādhikaraṇam ।
prāṇo viṣṇurityuktam ।
tatra atā vā etāḥ śīrṣan chriyaḥ śritāścakṣuḥ śrotraṃ mano vākprāṇaḥ'; ityatra prāṇasya viṣṇutvaṃ na vidyate ।
indriyaissahābhidhānāditi । ata āha 
atrādhikaraṇe lokato anyatra prasiddhaprāṇanāmno viṣṇau samanvayaḥ pratipādyate । śrutyādisaṅgativiṣayavākyaviṣayasaṃśayasayuktikapūrvapakṣān darśayati prāṇa iti ।। ādyaprāṇādhikaraṇe atadvai tvam'; iti vākyoktaprāṇo viṣṇurityuktamityarthaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha tatreti । uktamityanuṣajyate । tasyāvṛttivipariṇāmau । evaṃ tatretyapyāvartanīyam । tathā ca atatra'; tadvai tvamiti vākye uktasya prāṇasya viṣṇutvaṃ na vidyate na yujyate । kutaḥ? yatastatra atadvai tvam'; iti vākyoktaprāṇaviṣaye aukte'; śrute atā vā etāḥ'; ityaitareyavākye uktasya śrutasya prāṇasya viṣṇutvaṃ na vidyata iti yojanā । kuto na vidyate ityata āha indriyaissahābhidhānāditi । indriyaissaha paṭhitatvāt indriyagaṇe gaṇitatvāt ityarthaḥ । anenaitareyaprāṇasya viṣṇvanyatvākṣepamukhena prācīnataittirīyoktaprāṇasyāpyanyatvākṣepāttenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । aitareyaprāṇākhyo viṣayaḥ । prāṇo anya uta viṣṇuriti saṃśayaśca sūcitaḥ । tathā vāyvādiranya eveti pūrvapakṣaḥ । indriyagaṇe gaṇitatvākhyatatsādhakaliṅgaṃ ca sūcitam । atā vā etāḥ'; ityetacca caturmukhaśirasi śiraśśabdapravṛttinimittakathanāya pravṛttam । vaiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । tathā ca yataḥ atā etāḥ'; cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ manovākprāṇa ityetacchabdavācyāstadabhimāninyo devatāḥ । aśīrṣan'; śīrṣṇi śiraḥsaṃjñikamūrdhni śritāḥ । ata eva śrayaṇācchriya iti siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ । anena cakṣurādibhiḥ śritatvaṃ śiraḥpadapravṛttinimittamityuktaṃ bhavati । pūrvapakṣī tu prāṇaśabdamanyamātraparaṃ manyate । siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati ata iti । yataḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ prāptaḥ ata uttaraṃ sūtramāha bhagavān bādarāyaṇa ityarthaḥ ।

prāṇas tathānugamāt ।
ataṃ devāḥ prāṇayanta'; asa eṣo asuḥ sa eṣa prāṇaḥ'; aprāṇa ṛca ityeva vidyāt'; 
atadayaṃ prāṇo adhitiṣṭhati'; ityādyānugamāt ।
sūtraṃ paṭhitvā tatrānugamāditi hetvaṃśaṃ śrutyudāharaṇena vyācaṣṭe prāṇa iti । evamādivākyoktānāṃ devatopadeśyatvādiliṅgānāmatrāsmin prakaraṇe bahuṣu sthaleṣu aanugamāt'; anuvṛtterabhyāsādityarthaḥ । ādipadena aprāṇo hyevaiṣa ya eṣa tapati'; iti sūryamaṇḍalasthatvapratipādakavākyaṃ gṛhyate । tathā asarvāṇi bhūtānyāpipīlikābhyaḥ prāṇena bṛhatyā viṣṭabdhāni'; ityādi vākyaṃ ca gṛhyate ।

atrāpi prāṇo viṣṇureva ।
sautraṃ tathāśabdaṃ vyācaṣṭe atrāpīti । na kevalaṃ atadvai tvam'; ityatra, kintvaitareye apīti samuccaye apiśabdaḥ । sūtre anuvṛttasya tattvityasyārthamāha viṣṇureveti । anena yathā
atadvaitvam'; iti śrutyuktaprāṇo viṣṇuḥ tathaitareyokto api viṣṇureva, na tvanyaḥ । kutaḥ? viṣṇuliṅgānāṃ devatopadeśyatvādīnāmasmin prakaraṇe aanugamāt'; anuvṛtterabhyāsāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।
aitareye ataṃ devāḥ prāṇayanta'; iti ekakhaṇḍasthavākyam । ataṃ'; nārāyaṇaṃ vāyuṃ ca devāḥ aprāṇayanta'; prakarṣeṇa śiṣyapraśiṣyadiṣu nītavantaḥ upadidiśurityarthaḥ । anena viṣṇoḥ sarvadevopāsyatvamuktaṃ bhavati ।
asa eṣo asuḥ sa eṣa prāṇaḥ sa eṣa bhūtiḥ'; ityādyanyakhaṇḍagataṃ vākyam । anena bhūtitvādinā devādyupāsyatvamucyate । asa eṣaḥ'; bhagavān duṣṭanirasanādasuḥ prakṛṣṭānandarūpatvātprāṇaḥ devānāṃ bhūtiśabditajñānādyaiśvaryapradatvādasurāṇām ajñānādyanaiśvaryahetutvācca bhūtyabhūtiśabdavācya ityarthaḥ ।
tatraiva atā vā etāḥ sarvā ṛcaḥ sarve vedāḥ sarve ghoṣā ekaiva vyāhṛtiḥ । prāṇa eva prāṇa ṛca ityeva vidyāt'; iti anyadvākyam । atra prāṇasyasarvavedoktatvamucyate । yāstāḥ etāḥ sarvā ṛcastāsāṃ aekaiva vyāhṛtiḥ'; ekameva vyāhartavyaṃ pratipādyam । tacca kim? prāṇo viṣṇureva । kiñca ye sarve vedāḥ teṣāmapi prāṇa eva pratipādyaḥ। api ca ye samudrādighoṣāḥ teṣāmapi, kimu vedānām । tatra ṛcastu viśeṣata indrādināmavato viṣṇorguṇān alpajñānāmapi prakāśayantīti, prāṇe nārāyaṇe tadviṣayā eva avidyāt'; tatpratipādikā eveti jānīyādityarthaḥ । aitareyabhāṣye tu prathamaprāṇapadamapi viṣayasaptamyantatayā vyāhṛtiśabdaṃ ca vyāharaṇaparatayā vyākhyāya ekameva vyāharaṇaṃ nirdeṣaguṇapūrtivācakatvādekaprakārameva nāmetyarthaḥ uktaḥ । tattvapradīpe apyayamevoktaḥ ।
atha devarathaḥ atasya vāguddhiḥ śrotre pakṣasī cakṣuṣī yukte manaḥ saṅgṛhītā tadayaṃ prāṇo adhitiṣṭhati'; iti vākyāntaraṃ atra prāṇasya deharathatvamucyate । prameyāntarakathanārambhārtho athaśabdaḥ । ucyata iti śeṣaḥ। tathā ca devasya viṣṇoḥ vāyoḥ adhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca ratha ucyate ityarthaḥ । tasyādhyātmaṃ dehākhyarathasya avāk'; vāgākhyā umā uddhiḥ dhāraṇarajjurūpā adhidaivaṃ viṣṇurathasya prasiddhasyandanasya ca nāgākāromā uddhiḥ aśrotre'; dakṣavāmapārśvagatacandratadbhārye apakṣasī'; pārśvayuktāśvau anyatrāśvarūpau pārśvayoryuktau acakṣuṣī'; ubhayapārśvagatasūryatadbhārye ca ayukte'; agrato niyuktāśvau amano'; mano abhimānī rudraḥ asaṅgṛhītā'; sārathiḥ evam adhidaivaṃ prasiddhasyandanasyāpi rudraḥ sārathiḥ । sa cāsāvayaṃ ca tadayamityekaṃ padam । tattvapradīparītyā
bhinnapadatve api taditi rathatayoktaṃ śarīraṃ parāmṛśyate । liṅgavyatyayena taṃ rathamiti vā । ayaṃ prāṇo viṣṇuḥ vāyuścādhitiṣṭhatītyarthaḥ । liṅgena pūrvapakṣite kathaṃ tenaiva siddhānta ityāśaṅkānudayāya liṅgabāhulyoktiḥ ।

viṣṇumevānayan devā viṣṇuṃ bhūtimupāsate ।
sa eva sarvavedoktastadratho deha ucyate ।
iti skānde ।
nanu bāhulyena balavataḥ saiddhāntikaliṅgādapi pūrvavādyuktaliṅgameva balavat । niravakāśatvena svabhāvato balavattvāt । na cāviśeṣeṇanirṇayaḥ, bāhulyena balavato api svābāvabalinaḥ prābalyāt । yadāhuḥ 
dvividhaṃ balavattvaṃ ca bahutvācca svabhāvataḥ ।
tayossvabhāvo balavān upajīvyadikaśca saḥ ।
iti । ataḥ kathaṃ tairviṣṇutvaniścaya ityato devatopadeśyatvādiliṅgānāṃ niravakāśatvamapi smṛtyā sādhayati
viṣṇumiti । devāḥ viṣṇumeva prādhānyena śiṣyādiṣu jñānasampradāyapravartanena aānayan'; upādiśan । bhūtimuddiśya viṣṇumevopāsate । bhūtimiti vidheyaviśeṣaṇaṃ vā । tathā ca viṣṇuṃ bhūtiṃ bhūtirjñānādyaiśvaryarūpa ityupāsate ityarthaḥ । asaḥ'; viṣṇurmukhyavācyatayeti śeṣaḥ, tenaivakāropapattiḥ । atadratho'; viṣṇoreva rathaḥ । atraivakārasya dvirgrahaṇātsarvatrānuṣaṅgaḥ sūcitaḥ । tena sarvaliṅgānāmapi niravagakāśatvamuktaṃ bhavati । skānde ityanantaraṃ liṅgānāmananyathāsiddhatvamuktamiti vākyaśeṣaḥ । tathā caikaprakāreṇa prabalātpūrvapakṣiliṅgātprakāradvayenāpi prabalasya saiddhāntikaliṅgasyādhikyena nirṇayopapattiriti bhāvaḥ । abhyupetya cedamuditam । vastustu pūrvapakṣiliṅgasya na niravakāśatvenāpi prābalyamasti, prāṇaiḥ sahagaṇitatvasyāntaryāminiṣṭhatāsambhavāt ।

brahmaśabdānugamācca ।
yadā bahutvaniravakāśatvākhyaprakāradvayenāpi durbalaliṅgasyobhayathāprabalaliṅgato bādhasambhavena tainaiva prāṇasya viṣṇutvasiddhiḥ, tadā kimu vācyaṃ niravakāśabrahmaśabdābhyāsāditi bhāvenānugamapadaṃ prakārāntareṇa vyācaṣṭe brahmeti । asmin prakaraṇe aetadbrahma'; abrahmaṇo lokaḥ'; abrahmemaṃ puruṣam'; audaraṃ brahmetyācakṣate'; aa iti brahma'; ityādi niravakāśabrahmaśabdābhyāsāccetyarthaḥ । etadviṣṇusvarūpaṃ brahma guṇapūrṇam । ayaṃ jīvo brahmaṇaḥ parasyāśrayaḥ । imaṃ puruṣaṃ caturmukhaṃ parabrahma prāpadyata । vāyuryatra sthita urveva garaṇaṃ stavanaṃ cakre tatsthānamudaraṃ tadgatamityarthaḥ ।

na vaktur ātmopadeśād iti ced adhyātmasaṃbandhabhūmā hy asmin ।
aprāṇo vā ahamasmyṛṣe'; iti vakturātmo
padeśādindra eveti cet na, aprāṇastvaṃ prāṇaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni'
iti bahvadhyātmasambandho hyatra vidyate ।
uktamākṣipya samādadhatsūtraṃ paṭhitvākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe neti । prāṇa ityanuvartate । tathā ca prāṇo viṣṇuriti na yuktam । kutaḥ? aprāṇo vā ahamasmyṛṣe'; iti vākyena bṛhatīsahasravakturviśvāmitrasyendreṇa prāṇatayā ātmanaḥ svasyaivopadeśādityarthaḥ । prāṇa indra eveti phaloktiḥ । na tūktahetoḥ sādhyoktiḥ । aprāṇo vāhamasmyṛṣe'; iti vākyaṃ tu atamindra uvāca ṛṣe priyaṃ vai me dhāmopāgāḥ varaṃ te dadāmīti । sa hovāca tvāmeva jānīyāmiti । tamindra uvāca'; iti pūrvavākyena saha vyākhyeyam। tatprakārastu ataṃ'; viśvāmitraṃ aindraḥ'; tadantaḥstho bhagavānuvāca । kimiti? he ṛṣe me priyaṃ dhāmopāgāḥ prāpnuhi । vaiśabdo avadhāraṇe prasiddhau vā। evaṃ trivāraṃ śaṃsanena dhāmaśabditasālokyaprāptibhagavatpuraprāptisādhanabhagavatprasādaṃ prāptaḥ asaḥ'; viśvāmitraḥ indrāviṣṭena hariṇā varaṃ te dadānīti punaruktassan uvāca । kimiti? tvāṃ sāmānyataḥ pūrvam ahaṃ jāne । adhunā kīdṛśastvamiti viśeṣato jānīyāmiti । evamuktaḥ aindraḥ'; tadantargato hariḥ ṛṣiṃ pratyuvāca । kimiti? he ṛṣe ahaṃ prakṛṣṭānandarūpatvātprāṇaśabdavācyo asmīti । atra vākyasamanvayapakṣe asmadādiṣūpapadeṣu vihitānāmasmītyāditiṅantapadānāṃ tadvṛtteḥ sulabhatvāditi tattvanirṇayaṭīkārītyā ahamitīndrāntaḥsthena hariṇā svātmano nirdeśādasmīti uttamapuruṣopapattiḥ । pūrvapakṣirītyā śrutyarthastu spaṣṭaḥ । ahaṃ prāṇo asmīti padānāṃ aheyatvaprakṛṣṭānandatvasaṃhartṛtvajñātṛtvanimittaiḥ bhagavati samanvayapakṣe tu na tadanupapattiriti dhyeyam । nañadhyāhāreṇa siddāntāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe neti । anugamādityanuvartate । hiśabdo yata ityarthe । tathā cetthaṃ tattvapradīpaṭīkoktā yojanā nāyaṃ prāṇa indraḥ, kintu viṣṇureva । kutaḥ? aanugamāt'; prāguktaprabalatamaliṅgādeḥ । tathā satyupadeśavirodha iti
cet na, kutaḥ? yato atra prakaraṇe svasthitasyaiva prathamaṃ aprāṇo vā ahamasmyṛṣe'; iti vākyena paramātmatvamuktamindreṇa । tarhyaikyoktivirodha ityapi na । yato atra tasyaiva prāṇākhyaparamātmanaḥ aprāṇastvaṃ prāṇaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni'; ityevamādivākyena abahvadhyātmasambandhaḥ'; indrādijīvarūpabahudehasambandhaḥ sarvagatatvameva ṛṣiṃ prati indreṇoktaṃ avidyate'; asti natvaikyamata iti । sūtroktasambandhabāhulyaṃ sambandhini paryavasyatītyāśayena
bahvityuktam । bhūmaśabdasya bhāvavācitve api bhāvabhavitrorabhedāt bhavitari prayogaḥ । sūtre tu paranipāta ārṣaḥ । athavā adhikaścāsāvātmā cādhyātmā tasya sambandhaḥ bahuścāsāvadhyātmasambandhaśceti vigrahaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yataḥ aatra'; indre abahuḥ'; bahulaḥ paramātmasambandhaḥ sannidhiviśeṣo vidyata ityarthaḥ । vidyata ityanantaraṃ tadapekṣayāyam upadeśo na svāpekṣayeti śeṣaḥ । tathācendre tātkālikeśvarasannidhānaviśeṣābhiprāyā aprāṇo vā aham'; ityuktiḥ, na svāpekṣayeti nopadeśavirodha iti bhāvaḥ । kuto na svāpekṣayetyataḥ prāṇastavamityādyāha । yojanā tu hi yasmāt aprāṇastvam'; ityādi vākyenāsya prāṇasya abahvadhyātmasambandhaḥ'; adhyātmatvenāntaryāmitvena indrādirūpabahudehasambandhaḥ sarvagatatvamuktaṃ vidyate na caitadatra jīvaviśeṣendre vidyate yujyate tasmāditi । prathamapakṣe ayasyātmā śarīram'; iti śruterindrādīnāṃ viṣṇudehatvādaikyavyapadeśaḥ śarīraśarīribhāvanibandhana iti jñāpanāyādhyātmetyuktiḥ । anena bṛhatīsahasravakturviśvāmitrasya taṃ pratīndreṇa prāṇatayātmopadeśādayaṃ prāṇo na viṣṇuḥ, kintu indra eveti cet nendro ayaṃ prāṇaḥ, kintu viṣṇureva । kutaḥ? anugamāt prāguktabalatamaliṅgādeḥ । na copadeśavirodhaḥ । yato ayamindragatādhyātmaviṣaya eva । kutaḥ? hi yasmādasmin prakaraṇe adhyātmasambandhabhūmā । atrādhyātmasambandhaśabdenātmādhikāre vartamānamiti । adhiścāsau ātmā ceti dehaḥ paramātmā cocyate । tathā ca yasmādadhyātmano viṣṇorindraviśvāmitrādidehasambandha ukto asti tasmāt । athavā hi yasmāt asminnindre adhyātmasambandhabhūmā adhirīśvare adhikasyātmanaḥ paramātmanaḥ sambandhasyāveśasya bhūmā bāhulyaṃ vidyate tasmādupadeśasya sannihitaparamātmaviṣayatvopapteriti bhāvaḥ । tadapi kutaḥ? hi yasmāt asmin prakaraṇe adhyātmasambandhabhūmoktaḥ tasmāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

śāstradṛṣṭyā tūpadeśo vāmadevavat ।
śāstramantaryāmī ।
nanu yadi prāṇaśabdenendreṇāpi viṣṇureva svātmādisarvagatatayocyate tarhi mayi prāṇa iti nirdeśaḥ syāt । viṣṇāvahamityādirūpopadeśāyogādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhati śāstreti । turevārtho apyarthaḥ, yatha ityarthe smṛtisūcakaśca । yujyata iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca yato api prāṇasya viṣṇutve apyupadeśaḥ prāṇo vāham ityevaṃrūpo yujyate, ato na tadanupapattiḥ । kathamayaṃ yujyate? yato ayamupadeśaḥ aśāstradṛṣṭyā'; śāsti sarvamiti śāstraṃ antaryāmī bhagavān, taddṛṣṭyā tadapekṣayaiva pravṛtto na tvaikyena । na cāntaryāmiṇi ahamādiprayogādarśanāt tadayogaḥ । yato avāmadevavat'; tatkartṛkaprayogavat । yathā vāmadevo nāma ṛṣiḥ antaryāmivivakṣayā aahaṃ manurabhavam'; iti svasmin ahaṃmanvādiśabdān prayuyuje । tathā ayamapyupadeśo yujyate ata iti sūtrayojanāmabhiprayan sautraśāstrapadaṃ vyācaṣṭe śāstramiti । tathācāntaryāmī viṣṇariha śāstrapadenokta ityarthaḥ । antaryāmīti prakṛtābhiprāyeṇa । yadvā śāsti prerayati sarvāniti vyutapattyā antaryāmītyetadeva śāstramityasya vyākhyānaṃ bhavatīti
nāpadārthatvaśaṅkāvakāśaḥ । ata eva bhāgavate dhyeye antaryāmiṇyeva śāstraśabdaprayogaḥ। aitareyabhāṣye aśāsturantaryāmiṇaḥ'; iti śāstṛśabdaṃ mūlīkṛtya vyākhyāne api, tadanusāreṇa ca tattvapradīpe śāsturantaryāmiṇo viṣṇoriti vyākhyānepi nāsya tadvirodhaḥ śaṅkyaḥ, yatastatparyāyaśabdavyākhyānenaiva śāstraśabdo vyākhyāto bhavatītyāśayena śāstraśabdaparyāyaśāstṛśabdo vyākhyāyate । yadvā śāstraśabde śāstṛ a ityavayavavibhāgamabhipretya śāstrityaṃśasyāntaryāmiṇa ityanena aśabdasya viṣṇorityanena ca vyākhyātattvāt, atra tu avayavavibhāgamavivakṣitvā śāstramityakhaṇḍapadasyāntaryāmiti vyākhyānāt tadanukūlatayā asaṃvicchāstram'; iti vacanopanyāsācca na virodhaḥ ।

asaṃvicchāstraṃ paraṃ padam'; iti hi bhāgavate ।
antaryāmiṇo viṣṇoḥ śāstrapadavācyatve pramāṇamāha saṃviditi । prathamaskandhe vyāsaṃ prati nāradavākyamidam ।
svapno māyāgrahaḥ śayyā jāgradābhāsa ātmanaḥ ।
nāmarūpakriyāvṛttiḥ saṃvicchāstraṃ paraṃ padam ।
asyārthaḥ ātmano jīvasya māyāvāsanākhyasaṃskāropādānakavastujñānarūpaḥ
svapnaḥ । agrahaḥ jāgratsvapnaviṣayajñānarahitā śayyā suṣuptiḥ nāmarūpakriyāsu śabdārthakarmasu vṛttirvyāvṛttiryanyāḥ sā । ābhāsaḥ pratyayaḥ saṃjñādiviṣayajñānarūpo jāgracca । āhatyaitadavasthātrayaṃ yasmādātmanaḥ parabrahmaṇo bhavati, tatsaṃvit sarvaviṣayaka
yathārthajñānarūpaṃ sarvajñaṃ vā । śāstraṃ sarvaniyantṛ, paraṃ uttamaṃ padaṃ sadbhiḥ prāpyaṃ brahma aham acintayamiti । bhāgavata ityanantaraṃ aprayogāt'; iti śeṣaḥ । asyāntaryāmītyanenānvayaḥ ।

tattannāmnocyate viṣṇuḥ sarvaśāstṛtvahetutaḥ ।
na kvāpi kiñcinnāmāsti tamṛte puruṣottamam ।
iti pādme ।
nanvantaryāmiṇi ahamādiprayogaḥ kathaṃ sambhavatītyāśaṅkyāṃ tatra tuśabdasūcitāṃ smṛtimevāha tattaditi। viṣṇuḥ atattannātmā'; anyaparatvena prasiddhāhamādināmnocyate iti । anena tasyāntaryāmiṇi viṣṇau vidvadrūḍhirdarśitā । asarvaśāstṛtvahetutaḥ'; sarvaniyantṛtvanimitteneti । anena mahāyogo darśitaḥ । tatra tasya svātantryanimittokteḥ । anena paramata ivāsmanmate api lākṣaṇikatvaṃ parihṛtam apuruṣottamam'; antaryāmiṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ aṛte'; vinā, anyatra akvāpi'; jīvādau akiṃ cit'; ahamādirūpaṃ anāma'; vācakatayā nāstīti । anena harau paramamukhyatā anyatra kevalamukhyatā coktā । anyathā na kvāpīti sāmānyaniṣedhāyogāt । atrāhamādiśabdāḥ pratyagādivācitvena prasiddhāḥ, pratyagādayaśca sarvadā piṇḍībhūtāḥ, tānavivekenājñāḥ kevalajīvādau prayuñjate dahati śabdamiva kāṣṭhe । prājñāstu mukhyāmukhyavivekavanto hyamukhmarthamanādṛtya mukhyārthe harau prayuñjataiti tattvanirṇaṭīkoktamanusandheyam । apādme'; ityanantaram aantaryāmiṇyahamādipadānāṃ mukhyatvokteḥ śāstradṛṣṭyā ahamādyupadeśo yukta eva'; iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

aahaṃ manurabhavaṃ sūryaśca'; ityādivat ।
nanvantaryāmiṇi ahamādiprayogādarśanāt tadayoga ityāśaṅkāṃ sūtroktadṛṣṭāntavivaraṇena pariharati ahamiti । aahaṃ'; vāmadevasaṃjñakaṛṣyantaryāmī tattadantaryāmitayā manuḥ sūryaścābhavamiti ṛṅmantrārthaḥ । ādipadena aahaṃ kakṣīvānṛṣirasmi vipro ahaṃ kutsam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । aityādivat'; evamādiprayogavadityasya aśāstradṛṣṭyopadeśaḥ'; ityanenānvayaḥ ।

jīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgān neti cen nopāsātraividhyādāśritatvād iha tadyogāt ।
atāvanti śatasaṃvatsarasyāhnāṃ sahasrāṇi bhavanti'; 
iti jīvaliṅgaṃ prāṇasaṃvādādimukhyaprāṇaliṅgaṃ tasmāt neti cet 
punaruktamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasya ākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe jīveti । anusandhīyate
uktamiti ca śeṣaḥ । saṃvādo vivādaḥ kalahaḥ prāṇasya prāṇaissaha saṃvāda iti vigrahaḥ । tathā ca yasmādatra prakaraṇe ataṃ śataṃ varṣāṇyabhyārcat tasmācchataṃ varṣāṇi puruṣāyuṣo bhavanti'; ityanena yacchatasaṃvatsaraparyantaṃ prāṇasya jīvadehe avastānahetukaṃ śatāyuṣṭvarūpaṃ jīvaliṅgamuktaṃ tat atāvanti śatasaṃvatsarasyāhnāṃ sahasrāṇi bhavanti'; ityādinā bahuṣu sthaleṣu anusandhīyate । yasmācca atā ahiṃsantāhamukthamahamukthamasmi'; iti vākyena prāṇasya prāṇairindriyaiḥ saha saṃvādarūpamukhyaprāṇaliṅgamuktam । yasmāccādipadagṛhītaṃ aprāṇo vaṃśa iti sthaviraḥ śākalyastadyathā śālāvaṃśe sarve anye vaṃśāḥ samāhitāssyuḥ evamasmin prāṇe cakṣuśśrotraṃ mano vāgindriyāṇi śarīraṃ sarva ātmā samāhitaḥ'; iti vākyena sarvajīvendriyadehadhārakatvarūpaliṅgaṃ coktamasti tasmādayaṃ prāṇo na viṣṇuḥ, kintu jīvamukhyaprāṇāveveti yojanā । yadyapi atasmācchataṃ varṣāṇi puruṣāyuṣo bhavanti'; iti śatāyuṣṭvaliṅgapratipādakavākyamevodāharaṇīyaṃ, na tu atāvanti'; iti vākyam । tathāpi liṅgasya bahuṣu sthaleṣu anugamo astīti jñāpanāyopaniṣado jīvaliṅge tātparyamastīti jñāpayitum anusandhivākyamevodāhṛtam । siddhānte śrutyarthastu puruṣāyuṣaḥ śatasaṃvatsarasyāhnāṃ sahasrāṇi śatasaṃvatsarāntaḥpraviṣṭāharniyāmakasūryagatabhagavatpuruṣarūpāṇi tāvanti sahasrāṇi । kiyanti? bṛhatīsahasragatākṣarāṇāṃ vācyāni puṃrūpāṇi yāvanti sahasrāṇi tāvanti । tathā ca tāni ṣaṭtriṃśatsahasrāṇi sampannāni bhavanti । atāḥ'; cakṣurādidevatāḥ aahiṃsanta'; vivādamakurvan । kinviti? ahamasya caturmukhadehasyoktho asmi utthāpako asmīti ।

na, antarbahissarvagatatvenetyupāsātraividhyādihāśritatvācca ।
parihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe neti । prāṇo viṣṇurneti na, kintu viṣṇurevāyaṃ, na jīvādirityarthaḥ । kuto netyatastatra prāguktānugamahetvanuṣaṅgaṃ, na coktajīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgavirodha ityatastatrahetutvena yataḥ śāstradṛṣṭyā tvayamupadeśaḥ ityasyānuṣaṅgaṃ, kimarthamantaryāmīti praśnasyāntarupāstyarthamiti parihāraṃ cābhipretya na copāsane avāntarabhedābhāva iti codyottaratvena pravṛttam aupāsā'; iti sūtrāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe antariti । gatatvenetyasyāntarbahissarvaśabdaiḥ pratyekaṃ sambandhaḥ । itiśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ । tathā ca dehāntargatatvena tadbahirgatatvena sarvagatatveneti prakāreṇa aupāsātraividhyāt'; bhagavadupāsanasya trividhatvādityarthaḥ। nanu tathāpi kathanaṃ vyarthaṃ vastuta upāsanātraividhyasyehānuktasyāntaryāmikathanāprayojakatvādityataḥ pravṛttam aāśritatvāt'; ityaṃśaṃ caśabdādhyāhāreṇa vyācaṣṭe iheti । etatprakaraṇe uktatvādityarthaḥ । upāsātraividhyasyeti vipariṇāmenātrānvīyate । co
hetūpapādakahetusamuccaye । tathā ca atroktatraividhyāntargatāntaropāsanārthamantaryāmikathanaṃ yuktamiti bhāvaḥ ।

asa etameva sīmānaṃ vidāryaitayā dvārā prāpadyata'; 
asa etameva puruṣaṃ brahma tatamamapaśyat'; 
aetaddha sma vai tadvidvānāha mahidāsa aitareyaḥ'; 
ityādinā ।
atropāsanātraividhyamucyata ityatrāpi kiṃ liṅgamityata āha sa iti । asaḥ'; vāsudevo bhagavān aetameva sīmānaṃ'; śiromadhyaṃ vidāryaiva aetayā dvārā'; suṣumnānāḍyā aprāpadyata'; prāptaḥ । caturmukhahṛdayamiti śeṣaḥ । anena bhagavato dehāntaḥpraveśokteḥ ukteścopāsanārthatvāt antarupāstiruktā bhavati । asaḥ'; caturmukhadehe prākprapadābhyāmantaḥ praviṣṭo nārāyaṇaḥ aetameva puruṣaṃ'; vyāsakṛṣṇakapilādirūpamātmānam ātataguṇaṃ svasvarūpabhūtamādānādikartāraṃ vā । tatamaṃ alopaḥ samāne'; iti sūtrāttalopaḥ । tamabarthe mapratyayo vā । tathā ca tatamaṃ atiśayena vyāptaṃ niravadhikavyāptimantaṃ abrahma'
guṇapūrṇam aapaśyat'; tadguṇakatayā tadrūpaṃ dadarśetyarthaḥ । kecittu takāra eva vyāptyabhidhāyaka ityāhuḥ । anena sarvagatatvaṃ tathopāsanārthamuktam । atadetat'; prakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ avidvān'; jānannaitareyaḥ itarāyā apatyaṃ pumān viśālasaṃjñāt ṛṣeḥ utpannaḥ aitareyaḥ । amahidāso'; mahino mahātmāno devāḥ dāsabhūtāḥ yasyāsau bhagavānāhetyarthaḥ । hasmavaiśabdāḥ prasiddhidyotakāḥ । atra bahirupāstyarthaṃ mahidāsa āheti bahirupāstiruktā bhavati । na ca vācyamatra svarūpamātramucyate, nopāsanārthamiti । upāsanāṃ vinoktiprayojanābhāvāt । ityādinetyasyetyādināvākyenopāsanātraividhyasyāśritatvādarthāduktatvādityanvayaḥ । ādiśabdena ataṃ prapadābhyāṃ prāpadyata brahmemaṃ puruṣametasyāmetam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । nanu aetaddhasmavai tadvidvānāha hiraṇyadanvaidaḥ'; itivanmahidāso api ṛṣitvenocyatāmiti cenna । asyāḥ upaniṣadaḥ aitareyasaṃjñayaivetarāputrasya mahidāsasya ṛṣitvasiddhyā taduktervyarthatvāt ।

mahidāsābhidho jajñe itarāyāstapobalāt ।
sākṣātsa bhagavānviṣṇuryastantraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ vyadhāt ।
iti brahmāṇḍe ।
tathāpi mahidāsasya viṣṇutvaṃ kuto jñāyata ityata āha mahidāseti । ajajñe'; vyakto babhūva । asa ca'; mahidāsaḥ 
mahidāsastvaitareyo bahvṛcopaniṣadgataḥ ।
sākṣātsa bhagavānviṣṇustannāmaiko munirhyabhūt ।
iti chāndogyabhāṣye anantaroktabhagavadanyaḥ tatsaṃjñaketarāputraḥ ṛṣiratra na vivakṣitaḥ, kintu । yo avaiṣṇavaṃ'; viṣṇuviṣayaṃ atantraṃ'; granthaṃ avyadhāt'; nirmame । yadvā atantraṃ'; pañcarātraṃ vyadhāt nāradādibhyo vyācakhyau । yaśca asākṣāt'; svayaṃ abhagavān'; pūrṇajñānādimān aviṣṇuḥ'; tadavatārabhūtaḥ pūrvoktaḥ sa evātra vivakṣita ityāha sākṣāditi। brahmāṇḍe purāṇa ityasyāśritatvādityanenānvayaḥ । mahidāsasya viṣṇutvoktiriti tadarthaḥ । tena caśabdānvayaḥ ।

tattadupāsanāyogyatayā ca puruṣāṇām ।
nanvekavidhopāsanayā sarveṣāṃ brahmāparokṣasambhavātkimupāsātraividhyena ityataḥ pravṛttaṃ atadyogāt'; iti sūtraśeṣaṃ vyācaṣṭe tattaditi । upāsanetyanena puruṣāṇāmityanena ca tadityasyāvṛttiḥ sūcitā । caḥ samuccaye । tathā ca teṣāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ manuṣyarṣigandharvadevākhyādhikāriṇāṃ teṣu trividhopāsaneṣu madhye tattadupāsane yathākramaṃ bahirantarvyāptirūpaikaikopāsana eva yogyatayā yogyatvena hetunetyarthaḥ । asyopāsātraividhyādityanenānvayaḥ । tathā cānekavidhopāstiyogyatāvatāmadhikāriṇāṃ naikavidhopāsanayā brahmajñānamiti tattraividhyamāvaśyakamiti bhāvaḥ ।

keṣāṃcitsarvagatvena keṣāṃciddhṛdaye hariḥ ।
keṣāñcidbahirevāsau upāsyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।
iti brāhme ।
puruṣāṇāmuktānekavidhopāsanayogyatā kuto jñāyata ityataḥ kartṛviśeṣānanupādāya sāmānyataḥ upāsakatraividhyapratipādikāṃ smṛtiṃ paṭhati keṣāñciditi । apuruṣottamo'; hariḥ akeṣāñcit'; devānāṃ devaiḥ sarvagatatvena prakāreṇopāsyaḥ । akeṣāñcit'; ṛṣigandharvādīnāṃ ahṛdaye'; svasvahṛdayākāśe upāsyaḥ । akeṣāñcit'; manuṣyottamānāṃ tu bahirevopāsya ityarthaḥ । prācuryādevamuktiḥ । iti brāhma ityasya tattadupāsanayogyatayā tadviśiṣṭatvena puruṣāṇāmāśritatvāduktatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ ।

agnau kriyāvatāṃ viṣṇuryogināṃ hṛdaye hariḥ ।
pratimāsvaprabuddhānāṃ sarvatra viditātmanām ।
iti ca ।
। iti pādāntyaprāṇādhikaraṇam ।
iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite brahmasūtrabhāṣye prathamādhyāyasya prathama pādaḥ
atraivādhikaraṇe kartṛviśeṣapratipādakaṃ viśeṣapramāṇamāha agnāviti । viṣṇuḥ akriyāvatāṃ'
yajñādikriyānuṣṭhātṛṇām aagnau'; gārhapatyādau upāsyaḥ hariḥ । ayoginām'; ṛṣīṇāṃ hṛdaye upāsyaḥ । aaprabuddhānāṃ'; mandamatīnāṃ atyalpapratibhānāṃ manuṣyottamānāṃ apratimāsu'; kṛṣṇarāmādivigraheṣu upāsyaḥ । aviditātmanāṃ'; viśeṣato jñātabhagavadrūpāṇām aśrutapratibhānāṃ devānāṃ tu asarvatra'; sarvasthāneṣūpāsya ityarthaḥ । atrāgnau pratimāsviti vākyadvayena bahirmātropāsanopalakṣyate । ata eva sthānadvayoktiḥ । yathāśruteḥ sūryādau
viṣṇūpāsterbahirupāstitvaṃ na syāt । yogināmityanenāntarupāstiruktā । aṛṣayo antaḥprakāśāḥ'; iti śruteḥ । sarvatreti sarvagatopāstiriti jñātavyam । na cātra "yeṣāṃ bahirupāsanena mokṣasteṣāmapi hṛdyupāsanaṃ kiñcitkāryameva"iti bṛhadbhāṣyeṇa "bhagavān bimbadarśanenainaṃ mocayati"iti nyāyavivaraṇena ca virodhaśśaṅkyaḥ । agnāviti vākye anyaniṣedhābhāvena bimbaśabditasvasvayogyātmāparokṣārthaṃ hṛdyupāsanasyāpi sarvaiḥ kāryatvābhyupagamāt । mocakayogyāparokṣadvārābhūtāvatārādyaparokṣasādhanopāsanāya eva taistaiḥ prācuryeṇa prakaraṇasyāgnāviti vākyena vyavasthayā pratipādanācca । vacanadvayasyāpyekārthasādhakatvādasyāpi brāhme āśritatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ । tattadupāsanayogyatāvattvena puruṣaviśeṣāṇāmuktatvāditi tadarthaḥ । ato na tadyogāditi hetvasiddhiḥ śaṅkyeti bhāva ।
anena nātroktaprāṇo viṣṇuḥ, kintu jīvamukhyaprāṇāveva । kutaḥ? ajīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgāt'; śatāyuṣṭvarūpajīvaliṅgasyaprāṇasaṃvādādirūpamukhyaprāṇaliṅgasya ceha śravaṇāditi cet na, viṣṇurevāyaṃ prāṇaḥ, na jīvādiḥ । kutaḥ? aanugamāt'; hetoreva, na cānyaśrutiliṅgavirodhaḥ । uktarītyā atadyogāt'; teṣāmantaryāmiviṣayatvopapatteḥ । yataśśāstradṛṣṭyāyam upadeśa iti vā । kimarthamatrāntaryāmikathanamiti cet, antarupāstyarthamiti brūmaḥ । na copāsane avāntarabhedābhāvaḥ । aupāsātraividhyāt'; antarādibhedena bhagavadupāsanasya trividhatvāt । na ca tathāpi kathanamayuktam । vāstavatraividhyasyehānuktasya kathanāprayojakatvāditi vācyam । aiha'; prakaraṇe tatraividhyasyāśritatvāduktatvāt । na caikavidhopāsanayā sarveṣāṃ brahmāparokṣasambhavāt kimupāsātraividhyeneti vācyam । atadyogāt'; teṣāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ tasmin tadupāsana eva yogyatvāt । anekavidhopāstiyogyatāvatāṃ ca puruṣāṇāṃ ekavidhapāsanayāparokṣāsambhavena yogyatābhedādupāsātraividhyasyāvaśyakatvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । na ca vivādakartṛtvaliṅgasyāntaryāmiviṣayatve audāsīnau ca tāvāstāṃ keśavaścābjasambhavaḥ'; iti vacanavirodhaḥ śaṅkyaḥ । tasyāntaryāmiviṣayabhinnabāhyarūpaviṣayatvāt । ato anyaliṅgānāṃ tattadantaryāmiviṣayatvopapatteḥ tadvirodhābhāvāt । viṣṇurevāyaṃ prāṇaḥ ānandamayaśceti yuktā tajjijñāseti siddham ।
। iti pādāntyaprāṇādhikaraṇam ।
iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryāṇāṃ sarvatantrasvatantrāṇāṃ
śrīmadraghunāthatīrthapūjyapādānāṃ śiṣyeṇa
śrīmajjagannāthayatinā kṛtāyāṃ
śrīmadbrahmasūtrabhāṣyadīpikāyāṃ
prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ
।
tataḥ saptadaśe jātaḥ satyavatyāṃ parāśarāt ।
cakre vedataroḥ śākhā dṛṣṭvā puṃso alpamedhasaḥ । śrīmadbhāgavatam, 
taduktam īśāvāsyabhāṣyaṭīkāyāṃ abrahmādīnām aprāptajñānamutpadyate śriyastu sarvadā vidyata iti vivekaḥ'; iti।
